[I,001,i_I,001,iii]	namaḥ mañjughoṣāya sa śrīmān akalaṅka dhīḥ svayam upetya āryaḥ anujagrāha yam vyaktam tasya na vetti ayam jaḍa matiḥ lokaḥ garīyaḥ padam tatra upāsita loka bhartari kṛtā su alpā api anartha udayā sammohāt avadhīraṇa iti kṛpayā tad nītiḥ uddyotyate hita ahita prāpti parihārayoḥ niyamena samyak jñāna pūrvaka tvāt aviduṣām tad vyutpādana artham idam ārabhyate 
[I,001,iv]	tat dvividham samyak jñānam pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti na hi ābhyām artham paricchidya pravartamānaḥ artha kriyāyām visaṃvādyate nanu anyat api śābda upamāna ādikam pramāṇam asti pramāṇasya sataḥ atra eva antar bhāvāt pramāṇe eva sadṛśa ātmanā apratyakṣasya sambandhāt anyatas pratipattitaḥ dvividhaḥ eva hi arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ parokṣaḥ ca tatra yaḥ jñāna pratibhāsam anvaya vyatirekau ātmanaḥ anukārayati sa pratyakṣaḥ tat asādhāraṇam vastu rūpam sva lakṣaṇam anyaḥ tu buddhau sākṣāt svabhāva upādhāna sāmarthya rahitaḥ ayukta pratipattiḥ eva na ca anya darśane anya kalpanā yuktā atiprasaṅgāt tasya na antarīyaka tāyām tu syāt sa hi pratibaddha svabhāvaḥ yathāvidhaḥ siddhaḥ tathāvidha sannidhānam sūcayati sāmānyena ca sambandhinaḥ arthasya pratipattiḥ anumānam iti dve eva pramāṇe anyathā pratipatti ayogāt 
[I,003,i]	na vai pratibandhaḥ eva liṅga lakṣaṇam kim tarhi grāhya dharmaṇi dharmiṇi ca darśanam na ca etat śabdānām asti iti katham na pramāṇa antaram te tarhi tatra adṛṣṭāḥ kam artham upanayanti apanayanti vā yat prāk dṛṣṭam tatra smṛtim ādadhāti sā kim aśabda liṅgā svayam kathañcid anusmarate na bhavati asti vā anayoḥ avasthayoḥ viśeṣaḥ tat ime kvacid kiñcid asiddham anupanayantaḥ anapanayantaḥ vā katham kasyacid sādhanam na ca tebhyaḥ artha siddhiḥ teṣām tatra pratibandha asiddheḥ vaktuḥ abhipretam tu artham sūcayeyuḥ iti saḥ eva ca tathā apratipādyamānaḥ āśrayaḥ astu 
[I,003,ii]	tad bhāva bhāva anupalabdhī tarhi prabhava abhāva sādhane na anumānam ananvayāt na hi atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti sādhana antara abhāvāt tat sādhana tve ca nidarśana anavasthā prasaṅgāt na tatra viṣaya darśanena viṣayiṇaḥ vṛtta sambandhasya smaraṇāt na hi anvaya vyatirekābhyām anyaḥ hetu phalayoḥ tad bhāvaḥ tathā yukta upalambham anupalabhamānā na asti iti āhuḥ tad nimitta upadarśanena anupalabdhena asti iti vyavahāraḥ sādhyate mūḍham prati jana na khyātyā pitṛ tva vat adṛśya anupalambhe api nimitta abhāvāt sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhaḥ ajana nakhyātyā apitṛtva vat tasmāt sarvam svatas asiddham anyat sādhanam avyabhicārya ātma sambandham apekṣate iti na apratyakṣam pramāṇam anumānāt vyatiriktam asti 
[I,004,i_I,004,ii]	na apratyakṣam pramāṇam asti iti aparaḥ tat ayuktam yasmāt pramāṇa itara sāmānya sthiteḥ anyadhiyaḥ gateḥ pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣedhāt ca kasyacid sa khalu pratyakṣam pramāṇam na anumānam iti bruvāṇaḥ kāsāñcid jñāna vyaktīnām pravṛttau saṃvādam visaṃvādam ca upalabhya tad lakṣaṇam vyāptyā kathayet yathopad deśam pravartamānasya avipralambha artham tat yathā dṛṣṭa sādharmyāt tathā prasādhitam na anumeya tām atipatati tat ca asiddham iti na kiñcid pramāṇam apramāṇam vā anyatra anubhūta viṣayābhyaḥ anirdeśya lakṣaṇābhyaḥ jñāna vyaktibhyaḥ na ca tābhiḥ sva santāna bhāvinībhiḥ alakṣitābhiḥ ayam param vyavahārayitum īśaḥ iti apraṇayanam eva śāstrasya praṇayan vā svām eva vṛttim sva vācā viḍambayati para avabodha artham ca śāstram praṇayan anumānam pratikṣipati iti ayuktam tasya aprāmāṇye vṛtti vaiphalyāt 
[I,005,i_I,005,ii]	na ca śarīram eva buddhiḥ tad siddhau api buddhi vikalpe saṃśayāt na enam anya sambandhinam puruṣa mātra pratyakṣam anveti pratiṣedham ca ayam kvacid kurvāṇaḥ na pratyakṣeṇa kartum arhati iti tasya abhāva viṣaya tva virodhāt artha sāmarthya apekṣaṇāt anapekṣāyām vyavadhāna ādi bhāve api bhāva prasaṅgāt pratyakṣasya eva nivṛtteḥ abhāva niścayaḥ iti ced byāhatam etat tat ca na asti tena ca pratipattiḥ iti nivṛtteḥ vā asya asat iti kutas niyama abhāvāt bhāve vā saḥ eva avyabhicāraḥ anupalabdheḥ iti sā tena abhāvam pratipādayantī liṅgam eva 
[I,005,iii]	kasyacid saṃvāde api tad jātīyasya vyabhicāra darśanāt anāśvāsaḥ iti ced na tad rūpa anupalakṣaṇāt svabhāva pratibandhaḥ hi liṅga lakṣaṇam na ca tasya vyabhicāraḥ tad abhāve svabhāva abhāvāt tathā hi arthasya asambhave abhāvāt pratyakṣe api pramāṇa tā pratibaddha svabhāvasya tad hetu tve samam dvayam 
[I,006,i]	pratyakṣam api artha avisaṃvādāt eva pramāṇam sa ca avisaṃvādaḥ tasmāt ātma lābhāt anyatas bhavataḥ abhavataḥ vā bhāve niyamena tad samvāda ayogāt na artha vyabhicārāt artha saṃvādanam pratyakṣasya kim tarhi artha darśanāt iti ced tat punar artha darśanam artha bhāvaḥ vā syāt artha bhāvaḥ ced sarve arthāḥ pratyakṣāḥ iti sarvaḥ sarva darśī syāt jñāna bhāvaḥ ced katham anyasya bhāve asambaddhasya bhāva niyamaḥ darśanāt bhāva siddhiḥ iti ced nanu tat eva idam paryanuyuktam kim idam darśanam nāma iti tasmāt jñāna bhāvāt artha bhāvam icchatā jñānasya tad pratibandhaḥ vācyaḥ sa ca kārya svabhāvayoḥ liṅgayoḥ anumāne api tulyaḥ iti na pramāṇa lakṣaṇam anumānam na anveti 
[I,007,i_I,007,iii]	tatra pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham abhra antam timira āśu bhra maṇa nauyāna saṃkṣobha ādi anāhita vibhramam avikalpakam jñānam pratyakṣam kā punar iyam kalpanā abhilāpinī pratītiḥ kalpanā abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsā pratītiḥ kalpanā tayā rahitam na hi sa indriya jñāne sambhavati arthasya sāmarthyena samudbhāvāt 
[I,007,iv]	tat dhi artha sāmarthyena utpadyamānam tad rūpam eva anukuryāt na hi arthe śabdāḥ santi tadātmanaḥ vā yena tasmin pratibhāsamāne te api pratibhāseran na ca ayam artha asaṃsparśī saṃvedana dharmaḥ artheṣu tad niyojanāt tatas arthānām apratīti prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam upanipatya vijñānam janayat nānā ātmanā antarīyakam pratibhāsam punar kartum yuktaḥ rasa ādayaḥ iva parasparam na api tat balena udīyamānam vijñānam artha antaram anusartum yuktam rasa ādi jñāna vat sataḥ api vā tad ātmanaḥ indriya antara jñāna utpattau asāmarthyāt atiprasaṅgāt ca vikalpakam tu manaḥ vijñānam artha śakti sannidhāna anapekṣam vikalpa vāsanā utthāpitam aniyata indriya artha grāhi kutaścid anubhava sambandhāt saha pṛthak vā gṛhṇīyāt 
[I,008,i]	api ca artha upayoge api punar smārtam śabda anuyojanam akṣadhīḥ yadi apekṣeta saḥ arthaḥ vyavahitaḥ bhavet na hi saṅketa kāla bhāvitam abhilāpa sāmānyam asmarataḥ tad yojanā sambhavati śabda antaraḥ iva na ca artha abhipāta kṛte asatya antare vikāre śabda viśeṣe smṛtiḥ yuktā tasyāḥ atad kṛta tve tad nāma agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt tatas smṛtyā vyavadhānāt na artha upayogaḥ anantara vyāpāra phalaḥ syāt 
[I,009,i_I,009,iii]	atas ca yaḥ prāk ajanakaḥ buddheḥ upayoga aviśeṣataḥ sa paścāt api syāt ātma abhedena sāmarthya aviśeṣāt na ekasya ekatra kriyā kriye syātām tena syāt artha apāye api netra dhīḥ arthasya sākṣāt buddhau anupayogāt smṛti prabodhe ca upayukta tvāt na asya anupakāriṇaḥ buddhiḥ bhāvam apekṣeta artha abhipāta kṛte ca buddhi janmani abhilāpa smṛti antara abhāvāt siddham avikalpakam pratyakṣam 
[I,009,iv_I,009,v]	kim ca viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca sambandham laukikīm sthitim gṛhītvā saṅkalayya etat tathā pratyeti na anyathā kiñcid kenacid viśiṣṭam gṛhyamānam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tad sambandha loka vyavasthā pratītau tad saṅkalanena gṛhyate daṇḍya ādi vat na anyathā artha sambandha adhidhāna vyavasthā parijñāne abhāvāt jāti guṇa kriyāvatām etat na sambhavati eva rūpa viveka sambandhayoḥ apratibhāsanena ghaṭanā yogāt kṣīra udaka vat detat vedini yatra api viveka pratipattiḥ asti tasya api grahaṇam 
[I,010,i]	saṅketa smaraṇa upāyam dṛṣṭa saṅkalana ātmakam pūrva apara parāmarśa śūnye tat cākṣuṣe katham na hi idam iyataḥ vyāpārān kartum samartham sannihita viṣaya balena utpatteḥ avicāraka tvāt vicāraka tve ca indriya manaḥ vijñānayoḥ abheda prasaṅgāt abhede ca atīta anāgata vastu prabheda grahaṇa agrahaṇa ūhānūha artha bhāva apekṣā anapekṣā ādi prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,010,ii_I,011,i]	manaḥ vijñāna abhisaṃskṛtam indriya jñānam pratyeti iti ced na yathā uktā grāhiṇaḥ tathā pratipatti ayogāt aviṣaye apravṛtteḥ jāti ādi sambandha atīta śabda vyavahāra ādīnām indriya jñāna aviṣaya tvāt tasmāt na indriya jñānam artha saṃyojanām kalpanām āviśati vikalpa utthāpitā sā ca nivartyeta icchayā matiḥ na artha sannidhim īkṣeta 
[I,011,ii]	api ca iyam viśeṣaṇa ādi vikalpa utthāpitā satī pravṛttā api samagrasāmagrīkā punar icchayā nivartyeta tad anya vikalpavat śakyante hi kalpanāḥ pratisaṅkhyānena nivartayitum na indriya buddhiḥ sāmagrī sākalye api vinivartya go buddhim aśvam api kalpayataḥ goḥ darśanāt na api iyam artha sannidhim apekṣeta na hi gavā ādi vikalpaḥ artha sannidhau eva bhavati 
[I,011,iii]	 na anyathā idantayā iti ced na hi ayam gauḥ iti asannihite arthe bhavati idam ca naḥ pratyakṣam sannihita artha niścaya lakṣaṇa tvāt na etat asti yasmāt avidyamāna abhede api tad akṣā gocara tvataḥ spṛśataḥ api asti sā buddhiḥ kaḥ hi indriyā viṣayasya arthasya tad indriya jñāna utpattau avidyamānāt bhedaḥ tad sāmarthyasya tatas sarvathā sākṣāt vinivṛtteḥ parampara upayogasya atītāt api darśanāt tat ayam aviṣaya tvāt abhūta aviśiṣṭam api spṛṣṭvā ayam ghaṭaḥ iti pratipanna pratyakṣī bhavitum arhati 
[I,012,i_I,012,iii]	 dravyam tat spārśanam yadi tat na spārśanam api dravyam spṛṣṭvā gṛhṇāti iti ced na ayam ghaṭaḥ iti jñāne varṇa pratyavabhāsanāt na hi ayam ghaṭaḥ iti jñānam sparśana indriya jam yuktam tathā asamanvāhāre varṇasya api pratyavabhāsanāt tena rūpa sparśa vijñāna anvayaḥ mānasam eṣa smārtaḥ vikalpaḥ api ca yat sannidhāne yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tad dṛṣṭeḥ tad dhanau smṛtiḥ yuktā tad gati abhāve tu śabda bhede smṛtiḥ katham tat asmṛtau ca tena artham saṃsṛṣṭam vetti asau katham 
[I,013,i]	yadi eṣa niyamaḥ sva abhidhāna viśeṣaṇa apekṣāḥ eva arthāḥ vijñānaiḥ vyavasīyante iti nivṛtta idānīm indriya vijñāna vārttā abhidhāna viśeṣe amṛteḥ ayogāt sati hi artha darśane artha sannidhau dṛṣṭe śabde tatas smṛtiḥ syāt agni dhūma vat na ca ayam aśabdakam artham paśyati apaśyan ca na śabda viśeṣam anusmarati ananusmaran na yojayati ayojayan na pratyeti iti āyātam āndhyam aśeṣasya jagataḥ 
[I,013,ii]	abhipatan eva arthaḥ prabodhayati ā antaram saṃskāram tena smṛtiḥ na artha darśanāt iti ced na tad sambandhasya asvabhāvika tvāt samaya adarśane abhāvāt puruṣa icchātaḥ arthānām svabhāva aparāvṛtteḥ na samaya kāla utpattiḥ svabhāvasya parāvṛttau ca tasya tādātmyāt anyasya asamaya darśinaḥ api syāt na hi prati puruṣam arthānām ātma bhedaḥ nairātmya prasaṅgāt ātma sthiteḥ abhāvāt tasmāt ayam aśabda saṃyojanam eva artham paśyati darśanāt 
[I,013,iii]	atha vā pratyakṣa sādhanaḥ eva indriya dhiyaḥ kalpanā virahaḥ yatas saṃhṛtya sarvatas cintām stimitena antarātmanā sthitaḥ api cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate sākṣa jā matiḥ apratibhā samāna abhijalpa apratibhāsamānā pratyakṣā eva sarva prāṇinām indriya buddhiḥ iti kim atra anyena sādhanena na ca imāḥ kalpanāḥ apratisaṃviditāḥ eva udayante vyayante vā yena satyaḥ api alakṣitāḥ syuḥ tathā hi punar vikalpayan kiñcid āsīt me kalpanā īdṛśī iti vetti na pūrva ukta avasthāyām indriyāt gatau 
[I,014,i]	sa punar pratisaṃhārāt vyutthita cittaḥ kiñcid vikalpayan sva citta dhārāḥ saṅkalayati evam ca evam ca kalpanā mama āsīt iti tat imāḥ kalpanāḥ pratyakṣa bhāvinyaḥ katham saṃhṛta vikalpe darśane avibhāvitā nāma tat ayam asaṃsṛṣṭa vikalpaḥ vā pratyakṣaḥ darśana ātmā dṛśya ātmanaḥ vā vikalpasya darśane adṛṣṭiḥ vikalpa kalpanām indriya jñāne pratihanti 
[I,014,ii_I,015,i]	na vai buddhiḥ pratyakṣā yena indriya jñānasya vikalpa upagame bādhā syāt saḥ eva tāvat ayam vikalpaḥ saṃviditaḥ upayan āpayan ca kva antar bhāvyatām arthe buddhau vā na arthe adhyātmam parisyanda ādīha avaśena udaya astamayā yogāt ca buddhiḥ atra vivarteta sā ca apratyakṣatā vivṛttā api na prakāśeta na ca prakāśaḥ arthaḥ tathā āvṛttiḥ na api anyaḥ kaścid iha anuṣaṅgī iti abhāvaḥ eva artha abhilāpa anukāriṇaḥ anubhava ātmanaḥ vikalpasya sukha ādi saṃvedanam ca buddhiḥ sā ca parokṣa iti na anugraha upaghātau tatas syātām puruṣa antara saṃvedana vat ananuyan ca eṣām pratyakṣeṇa katham ātmani anviyāt ajñāte arthe buddheḥ asiddheḥ tad jñāne anumānāt anveti iti ced jitam jaḍa ejaya ghoṣaṇām avaghuṣya yena evaṃvadinaḥ api avadheya vacasaḥ loke artha jñānam ca nāma buddhi sādhanam pratyeti na buddhim iti ślāghanīya prajñaḥ devānām priyaḥ iti 
[I,015,ii]	na artha jñānam buddheḥ liṅgam kim tarhi indriya arthau iti ced avyabhicārī hetuḥ manaḥ iti ced tat api pūrvakam eva anantara vijñāna hetuḥ vijñānam vidmaḥ tasya viṣaya antara avadhāna vaiguṇye anyatra vijñāna nud patteḥ tat ca asiddham vyaktaḥ viṣayaḥ iti ced nanu sā vyaktiḥ buddhiḥ eva tad upādhiḥ saḥ api asiddhaḥ eva na vyaktiḥ buddhiḥ artha ātmā iti ced sa kim abuddhi janmā buddhim gamayet pratibandha abhāvat arthāt manaḥ ca sādhāraṇa tvāt anya buddheḥ api anumana prasaṅgaḥ siddhe api hi liṅge asiddhayā buddhyā sambandha abhāvāt ananumānam tasmāt pratyakṣā iyam anabhilāpā ca pratibhāti iti 
[I,016,i_I,016,ii]	śabdena avyāpṛta akṣasya buddhau apratibhāsanāt arthasya dṛṣṭau iva tat anirdeśyasya vedakam tat ca idam pratyakṣam anabhilāpya viṣayam avyāpṛta indriyasya darśana vat buddhau śabdena apratibhāsanāt na hi sa śabda arthaḥ yaḥ śābde na pratibhāsate na ca śabda viṣayaḥ eva vastu ākāra antareṇa darśane pratibhāsanāt etāvat mātra nibandhana tvāt ca atattvasya vastu abhāve api śābda pratibhāsā pracyuteḥ asat artha pratibhāsā viśeṣāt sati api pratītiḥ atadātma grāhiṇī tad bhāva abhāvayoḥ ananukārāt rasa buddhi vat gandhasya cakṣuḥ buddhi vat ca rūpasya ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam hi kāraṇam vijñānasya viṣayaḥ na ananukṛta anvaya vyatirekam kāraṇam na akāraṇam viṣayaḥ tasmāt na vastu viṣayāḥ śābda vikalpāḥ 
[I,017,i_I,017,ii]	artha pratipattaye ca śabdāḥ prayujyante na ca indriya arthaḥ anvayī yatas sabdena dṛṣṭa sambandhaḥ vyavahāre pratīyeta tathā hi ekatra dṛṣṭaḥ bhedaḥ hi kvacid na anyatra dṛśyate na hi vyakti ātmānaḥ parasparam anuyanti śakti pratibhāsa ādi bhedāt na tasmāt bhinnam asti anyat sāmānyam buddhi abhedataḥ 
[I,017,iii_I,017,v]	na hi vyakti ātmanaḥ vyatiriktam anvayinam ertham paśyāmaḥ yam śabdaḥ anudhāvet artha nānātve hi buddhi nānātvam dṛṣṭam bhūta guṇavat tad abhede api artha bheda kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ sarva ātmasu eka tva aniścayāt anānātu a pratipatteḥ anāna ekam jagat syāt atha api syāt pratibhāsamānam api sāmānyam anupalakṣaṇāt na vivekena niścīyate iti tat ayuktam yasmāt dhī śabda vṛtteḥ anyatra tatas na anupalakṣaṇam abuddhi śabda anvata bhājaḥ hi bhedān ayam sāmānya darśana balena anvayan katham anupalakṣakaḥ nāma na hi yatas yatra jñāna abhidhāna vṛttiḥ tad anupalakṣaṇe tasya tathā pratītiḥ daṇḍi vat 
[I,018,i]	tasmāt viśeṣa viṣayā sarvā eva indriya jā matiḥ tatra sāmānya apratibhāsanāt pratibhāsinām ca ananvayāt viśiṣṭam eva anabhilāpyam vastu rūpam indriyatayaḥ pratyāviśanti katham tarhi idānīm aniścaya ātmanaḥ pratyakṣāt vyavahāraḥ niścinvanhīdantayā sukha duḥkha sādhanayoḥ prāpti parihārāya pravartate na ayam doṣaḥ yasmāt tad dṛṣṭau eva dṛṣṭeṣu saṃvid sāmarthya bhāvinaḥ smaraṇāt abhilāṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ pravartate 
[I,018,ii_I,019,i]	artha ālocana mātre api pratyakṣe anubhava sāmarthya bhāvinaḥ anubhūta pratisandhāyinaḥ smaraṇāt tad dṛṣṭau eva dṛṣṭeṣu abhilāṣa itarābhyām vyavahāraḥ bhavati vastu dharmaḥ hi eṣa yat anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smṛti bījam ādhatte tādṛśa darśanāt asya prabodhaḥ abhilāṣa vāsanā vivṛttiḥ atas vṛttiḥ ca mānasam ca akṣa vijñāna anantara pratyaya udbhavam tad artha anantara grāhi 
[I,019,ii_I,019,iv]	pratyakṣam iti vartate mānasam api indriya jñānena samanantara pratyayena sva viṣaya ananta rakṣaṇa sahakāriṇā janitam pratyakṣam atas eva ca na anindriya dṛṣṭiḥ na api viṣaya antarasya sva jñāna kāla bhāvī tad atulya kriyā kālaḥ narthaḥ sahakārī iti ced na ubhayoḥ tulya kāla tvāt asataḥ prāc asāmarthyāt sāmarthya kāle ca kārya niṣpatteḥ anupayogāt jñāna hetoḥ viṣayasya sahabhāvaḥ viruddhaḥ bhinna kālam katham grāhyam iti ced grāhyatām viduḥ hetu tvam eva yukti jñāḥ jñāna ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam iti antaraślokaḥ 
[I,020,i]	na ca idam pūrva pramāṇa viṣaya grāhi anadhigata viṣaya tvāt pramāṇasya anyathā ca atiprasaṅgāt abhraṣṭa darśana saṃskārasya gṛhīta grahaṇasya smārtāt aviśeṣāt niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi aviśeṣa ādhāyi sādhanam iti api sādhana nyāyam atipatati krama bhāva virodhaḥ ca sarvāsām tad artha hetūnām buddhīnām anyaiḥ akārya bhedasya apekṣā yogāt anapekṣāt ca kramotapatti ayogāt ādheya bheda tve ca anya tvam kṣaṇika tvāt arthānām atipātāt ca na asatām grahaṇam tasmāt artha antaram eva pratyaya viśeṣa utpatteḥ manaḥ pratyeti 
[I,020,ii_I,020,iii]	 sukha ādīnām sva vedanam sukha ādīnām sva saṃvedanam api pratyakṣam sukha ādi grahaṇam spaṣṭa saṃvedana pradarśana artham sarva jñānānām ātma saṃvedanasya pratyakṣa tvāt na hi sukha ādīnām ātma saṃvedane vikalpāḥ saṃbhavati yasmat aśakya samayaḥ hi ātmā sukha ādīnām ananya bhāj na anuditaḥ pratiniyataḥ sukha ādi ātmā viṣayīkriyate saṃvittyā tasyāḥ tad ātma rūpa tvāt na enam iyam abhilāpena saṃsṛjati tathā vṛtteḥ ātmani virodhāt tad rūpasya prāc adarśanāt abhilāpa ābhoge ca viṣaya pratyastamayāt tad vivekena saṃvidaḥ api agrāhya hrāhakasya ca samayasya abhāvāt anyena api atīta rūpasya asaṃvedanāt apunarbhāvini samayasya vaiyarthyāt ca 
[I,021,i_I,021,iv]	teṣām atas sva saṃvittiḥ nābhi jalpa anuṣaṅgiṇī aśakya samaya tvāt na sukha ādīnām ātma saṃvittiḥ āviṣṭa abhilāpā sā pratyakṣam pramāṇam na evam sukha ādayaḥ saṃvedana rūpāḥ eka artha samavāyinā tu jñānena saṃvedyante iti eke teṣām api tat atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvaḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad sukha ādi kim ajñānam vijñāna abhinna hetu jam tad atad svabhāvānām bhāvānām tādrūpyam atādrūpyam ca paryanuyuktāḥ hetu prakṛtim eva te api ālamberan tad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad rūpāḥ atad rūpa hetu jāḥ atad rūpāḥ yathā śāli bīja ādibhyaḥ tad prasavāḥ tad anyebhyaḥ anyaḥ iti ākasmika tve deśa kāla prakṛti niyama ayogāt 
[I,022,i]	tatra sukha ādi utpattiḥ na āviṣayā yathāsvam viṣaya upanibandhanānām sukha ādīnām tad sannidhāna abhāve abhāvāt na api anindriyāḥ rūpa ādi anuṣaṅgiṇām tat viṣaya indriya virahe adarśanāt anupahata indriya upanidhau ca punar sambhavāt na api amanaskārāḥ ubhaya sannidhau api middha ādi viplutadhiyaḥ abhāvāt etāvān eva vijñāna utpatteḥ api kāraṇa kalāpaḥ tad prakṛteḥ tad kārya svabhāva niyame na anupalambha ātmanaḥ sukha ādayaḥ saṃskārāt niyamaḥ iti cer na tasya sāmarthya adarśanāt tanmātra bhāvinaḥ anya hetu tva kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti āpi pūrvakam eva yogyam vijñānam utpaśyāmaḥ antaḥkaraṇa abhipātinām sukha ādīnām vijñāna bhāvanā paṭu manda tā ādi bheda anuvidhānāt hetu sāmyāt sukha ādi bheda abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tasyāḥ sāmagryāḥ eva antara viśeṣa kṛta tvāt saṃśaya nirṇaya ādi bheda vat 
[I,022,ii]	na antarāḥ sukha ādayaḥ na api cetanāḥ tad ātmanām śabda ādīnām anubhavāt tad anubhava khyātiḥ iti aparaḥ tasya api aviśeṣe api bāhyasya viśeṣāt prīti tāpayoḥ bhāvanāyāḥ viśeṣeṇa na artha rūpāḥ sukha ādayaḥ yadi hi śabda ādi ātmānaḥ sukha ādayaḥ syuḥ śabda ādi aviśeṣe bhāvanā viśeṣāt prīti paritāpa viśeṣaḥ na syāt nīla ādi ābhāsa viśeṣa vat te anapekṣita tad atiśayāḥ bhāvanā anurodhinaḥ bauddhāḥ eva prajñā ādivat 
[I,023,i]	cetanāḥ ca api vedya tvāt atad rūpa apravedanāt cetanāḥ ca ete sukha ādayaḥ saṃvedya tvāt na hi yat yat viṣaya ākāram saṃvedanam na bhavati tat tasya vedakam aparaspara rūpam iva sukha ādi saṃvedanam idam asya saṃvedanam iti sambandhasya abhivyakti nimitta tvāt indriya ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt sārūpyam eva tad vedana lakṣaṇam 
[I,023,ii]	sārūpyam api atada ātmanaḥ prāk paścāt api ātma apracyuteḥ caitanyasya katham iti ced ayam aparaḥ asya doṣaḥ astu na tu asarūpam vedakam nāma na hi vitti sattā eva tad vedanā yuktā tasyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt sarva vedanā prasaṅgāt tām tu sārūpyam āviśat sarūpa yatnam ghaṭayet idam eva ca naḥ sukham yat sātam saṃvedanam iti siddhāḥ sukha ādayaḥ cetanāḥ 
[I,024,i]	viṣaya sārūpyāt saṃvedanasya tādātmye asaṃvedanāḥ sukha ādayaḥ iti ced na tvad pakṣe api asti sukha ādi saṃvedanam iti darśana artha tvāt apakṣepasya tatra api saṃvedanam eva ekam āntaram prīti paritāpa rūpam paśyāmaḥ na ca asya ayam ātma apara upadhānaḥ yuktaḥ tad aviśeṣe api svabhāva abhyāsa viśeṣāt tad ātma atiśaya siddheḥ buddhiḥ atiśayavatī na saṃvedanam iti ced kā iyam buddhiḥ adhyavasāyaḥ kim idam saṃvedanam anubhavaḥ kaḥ anayoḥ bhedaḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ padārthaḥ asaṃvedanaḥ anyā saṃvid asaṃvedanam sārūpyam buddhi lakṣaṇam iti anyasya api tad sarūpasya tad prāptiḥ viśeṣaḥ vā vācyaḥ antaḥkaraṇa tva ādayaḥ api tad nibandhanāḥ na vā apratipatti aṅgam iti anughoṣyāḥ tathāvidhasya anyatra api svaccha tva ādeḥ viśeṣasya bhāvāt saṃvid niṣṭāḥ ca viṣaya vyavasthitayaḥ tāḥ katham avetanaḥ arthaḥ vyavasthāpayet atiprasaṅgat atiśaya vat ca bauddham sukham anariśaye api śabādi sukhāḥ iti api vārttā mātram ekatra yugapad anayoḥ virodhāt tasmāt na caitanyāt anya atiśayavatī buddhiḥ 
[I,025,i_I,025,iii]	tad rūpa vyatirekeṇa buddheḥ anupalakṣaṇāt ekam eva idam saṃvid rūpam harṣa viṣāda ādi aneka ākāra vivartam paśyāmaḥ tatra yatheṣṭam sañjñāḥ kriyantām apratyakṣā saṃvid pratyakṣaḥ buddhi vivarte iti ced pratyakṣaḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ tad apratyakṣa tve anya pratyakṣa vat sarva apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt viṣayaḥ asti iti ca viṣaya upabhogaḥ prāptaḥ tad bhogasya apratyakṣa tvāt asiddheḥ sataḥ api asat aviśeṣāt laiṅgika upabhogasya ca ābhoga tvāt anya bhoga vat liṅga ayogāt atas api asiddhiḥ eva yathā uktam prāk tatra ca pratyakṣe viṣaya upalambhe samāptaḥ vyavahāraḥ iti apārthakam aparam caitanyam tam ca eka rūpam eva paśyāmaḥ iti na anyā buddhiḥ anyaḥ anubhavaḥ 
[I,026,i_I,026,iv]	saṃsargāt avibhāgaḥ ced ayaḥ golaka vahni vat vibhaktau api cetanā adhyavasāyau saṃsarga vipralabdhaḥ ayam na vivecayati ayaḥ golakam iva vahneḥ tad rūpa sparśa adhyavasāsāt bheda abheda vyavasthā evam utsannā sarva vastuṣu sarva artha upalambheṣu saṃsarga śaṅkayā ekatvān adhyavasāyāt bhinna upalambhayoḥ api sukha ādi nīlā ādi a ākārayoḥ anānātvāt kam bata ayam āśritya hetum bhada abhedau vyavasthāpayet 
[I,026,v_I,027,i]	abhinna vedanasya aikye yat na evam tad vibheda vat sidhyet asādhana tve asya na siddham bheda sādhanam bhinna ābhaḥ sita duḥkha ādiḥ abhinnaḥ buddhi vedane abhinna ābhe vibhinne ced bheda abhedau kim āśrayau iti saṅgraha ślokau ayaḥ golake api vahni sambandhāt artha antaram eva tat tathā utpannam ekam dṛśyate na nānā rūpayoḥ dravyayoḥ saṃsargāt avibhāgaḥ punar tad dravya santāna sthiti kāraṇa vicchedāt tad nivṛttiḥ tad upādāna kāraṇa apekṣiṇaḥ ca śīta sparśa ādeḥ apara utpattiḥ 
[I,027,ii_I,027,iv]	tasmāt antarāḥ sukha ādayaḥ saṃvedanāḥ ca bhāvanā balataḥ spaṣṭam bhaya ādau iva bhāsate yat jñānam avisaṃvādi tat pratyakṣam akalpakam yoginām api śruta mayena jñānena arthān gṛhītvā yukti cintā mayena vyavasthāpya bhāvayatām tat niṣpattau yat spaṣṭa avabhāsi bhaya ādau iva tat avikalpakam avitatha viṣayam pramāṇam pratyakṣam ārya satya darśana vat yathā nirṇītam asmābhiḥ pramāṇa vārttike 
[I,027,v]	kāma śoka bhaya unmāda caura svapna ādi upaplutāḥ abhūtān api paśyanti puratas avasthitān iva yathā viplavamā vega pratipatti pradarśanāt parokṣa gati sañjñāyām tathā vṛtteḥ adarśanāt tasmāt bhūtam abhūtam vā yat yat eva abhibhāvyate bhāvanā pariniṣpattau tat sphuṭa akalpa dhī phalam iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,028,i_I,028,iii]	tathā hi aśubha pṛthivīkṛtsnā ādikam abhūta viṣayam api spaṣṭa pratibhāsam nirvikalpakam ca bhāvanā bala niṣpannam iṣyate astu nāma bhāvanā balena spaṣṭa ābham nirvikalpakam tu katham yasmāt na vikalpa anubaddhasya spaṣṭa artha pratibhāsitā pratyasta mita artha vaiśadyaḥ hi sarve eva vipluta dhiyaḥ api saṃsṛṣṭa abhilāpaḥ pratyayaḥ tat na ayam sphuṭa pratibhāsaḥ vikalpakaḥ bhavitum arhati tathā hi svapne api smaryate smārtam na ca tat tādṛś arthavat 
[I,029,i_I,029,ii]	middha upaplutānām api anubhūta smaraṇa ākārāḥ vikalpāḥ bhavanti na ca te tathā avabhāsinaḥ smaryante tat na viplavaḥ anyaḥ vā vikalpam sphuṭayati avikalpakaḥ eva sphuṭa avabhāsaḥ iti svapna jñānam tarhi viśada ābham pratyakṣam bhavatu avikalpanāt na abhrāntam iti nirdeśāt atas eva vikalpaḥ avastu nirbhāsāt visaṃvādāt upaplavaḥ pratyakṣa ābhaḥ dvividhaḥ ucyate vastu pratibhāsam hi pratyakṣam tad abhāve tad ābhāsa pracyuteḥ iti uktam na ca evam vikalpaḥ tad pratibhāsasya vastuni ananurodhāt tasmāt pratyakṣa ābhāsaḥ viplavaḥ ca akṣaja tve api tad anyebhyaḥ aviśeṣatas 
[I,029,iii_I,030,ii]	yaḥ api kaścid viplavaḥ indriya jaḥ tad anyā indriya ja aviśeṣāt asau api vastu ananurodhi pratibhāsaḥ vipralambhāt pratyakṣa ābhāsaḥ etena mānasaḥ api viplavaḥ vyākhyātaḥ na eva dvi candra ādi bhrāntiḥ indriya ja iti eke tat na aindriye bhāva abhāva anurodhasya tattva lakṣaṇa tvāt tasya iha api tulya tvāt indriya vikāre ca vikārāt tad nibandhana tvāt ca āśraya sthiteḥ sarpa ādi bhrānti vat manaḥ bhrānteḥ akṣa vikṛtau api nivṛtti prasaṅgāt tathā akṣa vikāra nivṛttau api anivṛtti prasaṅgāt tasmāt indriya jam api etat bhrānteḥ apratyakṣam atas eva iti karaṇa vyavacchinnāt vikalpa vargāt pṛthak taimira upalakṣitam viplavam pratyakṣa ābhāsam āha sa apavāda tva sūcana artham anyatra cakṣuḥ ādi paramāṇūnām dvi candranīla ādi ābhāsa vijñāna hetu tva vacanāt kim punar asya pramāṇasya phalam prameya adhigatiḥ sā hi jñānam tat ca phalam iti kim idānīm pramāṇam yatas iyam prameya adhigatiḥ avyavadhānā tattvam pratilabhate tatra arthena ghaṭayati enām na hi muktvā artha rūpa tām tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ pramāṇam meya rūpa tā 
[I,031,i]	na hi kriyā sādhanam iti eva sarvam sarvasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam kim tu yā yatas tatra anubhava mātreṇa sadṛśa ātmanaḥ jñānasya sarvatra karmaṇi tena ātmanā bhavitavyam yena asya idam iti pratikarma vibhajyate anātma bhūtaḥ ca asya indriya artha sannikarṣa ādiṣu hetuṣu vidyamānaḥ api bhedaḥ bhinne karmaṇi abhinna ātmanaḥ jñānasya na bhedena niyāmakaḥ kriyā nibandhana tvāt karaṇa tattvasya tad aviśeṣe tasyāḥ api viśeṣa asiddheḥ sataḥ api vā viśeṣasya tad anaṅga tayā akaraṇa tvāt tasmāt yatas asya ātma bhedāt asya iyam adhigatiḥ iti ayam asyāḥ karmaṇi niyamaḥ tat sādhanam na ca iyam artha ghaṭanā artha sārūpyāt anyatas jñānasya sambhavati na hi paṭu manda tā ādibhiḥ sva bhedaiḥ bhedakam api indriya ādi arthena etat ghaṭayati tatra pratyāsatti nibandhana abhāvāt asti anubhava viśeṣaḥ artha kṛtaḥ yatas iyam pratītiḥ na sārūpyāt iti ced atha katham idānīm sataḥ rūpam na nirdiśyate na idam idantayā śakyam nirdeṣṭum anirūpitena nāma ayam ātmanā bhāvān vyavasthāpayati idam asya idam na iti su vyavasthitāḥ bhāvāḥ 
[I,032,i]	tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ sādhanam meya rūpa tā sādhane anyatra tad karma sambandhaḥ na prasidhyati sā ca tasya ātma bhūtā eva tena na artha antaram phalam dadhānam tat ca tām ātmani artha adhigamana ātmanā savya apāram iva ābhāti vyāpāreṇa sva karmaṇi tad vaśāt tad vyavasthānāt akārakam api svayam iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,032,ii^1]	etena indriya sannikarṣa artha ālocana viśeṣaṇa jñānāni pratyuktāni tatas karma sambandha asiddheḥ avyavadhāna abhāvāt kāraka atiśaya asiddheḥ sarva kārakopa yoge api kriyāyām antyasya tasya eva bhedakasya sādhakatama tvāt satsu api indriya ādiṣu abhinnasya prativiṣayam bhedakam asya karaṇam iti na hi indriyāṇi bhedakāni sarva jñāna hetu tvāt na artha ālocanam atādrūpye tasya eva tad artha ālocana tva asiddheḥ tathā viśeṣaṇa jñānam 
[I,032,ii^2]	aviṣaya kṛta viśeṣasya viśeṣaṇa jñāna viśeṣya jñāna aviśeṣāt vyavasthā siddheḥ kriyā sādhanayoḥ viṣaya nānātva virodhāt ca abhinna viṣaya tvedvayam vyartham krama bhāvaḥ ca abhinna nimittayoḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ sakṛt bhāve sādhya sādhana tā abhāvaḥ jñāna aṃśayoḥ tu sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ vyavasthā āśraya tvāt vastu abhedāt kriyā karaṇayoḥ aikya virodhaḥ iti ced na dharma bheda abhyupagamāt abhinne api vastuni śakti bhedena vyavasthā bheda darśanāt ca na ayam vastu sanniveśī vyavahāraḥ na api sannikarṣaḥ pramāṇam sarva ātmanā sannikṛṣṭasya api kaiścid eva dharmaiḥ pratipatteḥ tad aviśeṣe api eṣa viśeṣaḥ buddhi pratibhāsa kṛtaḥ iti tasya eva prāmāṇyam yuktam 
[I,033,i]	atha kā iyam artha saṃvid yā pramāṇa phalam yat eva idam pratyakṣam prativedanam asti idam vedanam tad artha vedanam kena utpatti sārūpyābhyām anantaram tarhi vijñānam tulya viṣayam viṣayaḥ prāpnoti kva tarhi idānīm ayam anubhavaḥ nanu asya eva rūpam vayam api anububhutsavaḥ idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vā iti darśana śravaṇābhyām yatra avasāya pratyayaḥ te tasya anubhavaḥ iti ced nanu sā eva tayoḥ pratyāsattiḥ atra vicāryate katham tat tasya darśanam iti tayoḥ hi sambandham āśritya draṣṭuḥ eṣa viniścayaḥ sa tad abhāve na syāt na ca viṣaya sārūpyam vijñānasya tad pratibhāsinaḥ sthūla ākārasya pratyekam paramāṇuṣu abhāvāt ekaḥ ca ayam jñāna sanniveśī iti na ca bahūni rūpāṇi sañcitāni tathā pratibhānti iti yuktam eka rūpasya bāhulya virodhāt bahuṣu ca tathāvidhaḥ na asti iti na tayoḥ sārūpyam 
[I,034,i]	na api sthūlaḥ ekaḥ viṣayaḥ tathā avabhāsī pāṇi ādi kampe sarvasya kampa prāpteḥ akampane vā cala acalayoḥ pṛthak siddhi prasaṅgāt vastra udaka vat ekasya ca āvaraṇe sarvasya āvaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ abhedāt na vā kasyacid āvaraṇam iti avikalam dṛśyeta avayavasya āvaraṇam na avayavinaḥ iti ced ardha āvaraṇe api anāvṛta tvāt prāgvat asya darśana prasaṅgaḥ avayava dvāreṇa tad darśanāt adṛṣṭa avayavasya asya apratipattiḥ iti ced na bheda abhāvena sarvathā apratipatti prasaṅgāt sarva avayavānām ca yugapad draṣṭum aśakya tvāt sarvadā ca asya adarśana prasaṅgaḥ katipaya avayava pratipattau darśane alpa avayava darśane api tathā sthūlasya darśanam syāt rakte ca ekasmin rāgaḥ araktasya vā gatiḥ avayava rāge vā avaya vi rūpam araktam iti rakta āraktam dṛśyeta tasmāt na ekaḥ kaścid arthaḥ yaḥ vijñānam sarūpayati 
[I,035,i_I,036,ii]	atas eva na anyaḥ anubhāvyaḥ buddhyā asti tasyāḥ na anubhavaḥ aparaḥ grāhya grāhaka vaidhuryāt svayam sā eva prakāśate vyastam hi viṣaya lakṣaṇam iti na kvacid anubhavaḥ na api asya kaścid tatra api grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇa vaidhuryāt tasmāt ātmā eva buddheḥ anubhavaḥ sa ca na anyasya kasyacid pratyakṣa prativedya tvam api asyām tad ātmatā eva sā ca tādātmyāt svayam prakāśate tena ātmanaḥ prakāśikā iti api ucyate prakāśa vat nīla ādi anubhavaḥ iti api tad svabhāvaḥ anubhavaḥ eva avedya vedaka ākārāḥ yathā bhrāntaiḥ nirīkṣyate vibhakta lakṣaṇa grāhya grāhaka ākāra viplavā tathā akṛta vyavastheyam keśa ādi jñāna bheda vat yadā tadā na sañcodya grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇā iti antaraślokau tadā anya saṃvidaḥ abhāvāt sva saṃvid phalam iśyate 
[I,036,iii]	yeṣām bhuddhiḥ eva upadarśita grāhya grāhaka ākāra utpadyate teṣām anyasya saṃvedyasya abhāvāt sva saṃvedanam phalam tad svabhāva tvāt artha pratipatteḥ yadi hi iṣṭa ākāraḥ saḥ anubhavaḥ aniṣṭa ākāraḥ vā tadā iṣṭaḥ aniṣṭaḥ vā viṣayaḥ pratividitaḥ bhavati vidyamāne api hi bāhye arthe yathāsva saṃvedanam eva artha niṣpatteḥ tat eva phalam yuktam na hi arthasya yathā svabhāvam vyavasthitiḥ sarva jñānānām eka ākāra tva prasaṅgāt aneka ākārāḥ tu vijñaptayaḥ yena ekam rūpam ekasya manaā apamanyasyām anaāpam dṛṣṭam 
[I,037,i]	iṣṭa aniṣṭa avabhāsinyaḥ kalpanā na indriya buddhayaḥ iti ced na tatra api ariṣṭa ādau apratisandhāna darśanāt anyatra api śabda gandha rasa viśeṣaiḥ abhinnaiḥ prāṇi viśeṣāṇām aindriyakasya eva sukha asukhasya utpatteḥ tasmāt sva saṃvedana rūpā eva artha pratītiḥ tasyāḥ ca viṣaya ākāra tā eva sādhanam yathā ākāram asyāḥ prathanāt artha sthiteḥ sva saṃvedana rūpa tvāt sva vid api iyam artha vid eva kāryataḥ draṣṭavyā atas eva na pramāṇa phalayoḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ svabhāva cintāyām tādātmyāt artha saṃvidaḥ sva saṃvid phalam ucyate 
[I,037,ii_I,038,i]	tathā avabhāsamānasya tādṛśaḥ anyādṛśaḥ api vā jñānasya hetuḥ arthaḥ api iti arthasya iṣṭā prameya tā yathā kathañcid tasya artha rūpam muktvā avabhāsinaḥ artha grahaḥ katham satyam na jāne aham api īdṛśam iti antaraślokau katham punar asati bāhye arthe pramāṇa prameya phala sthitiḥ uktam atra yathādarśanam iyam vyavasthā na tu yathātattvam iti viṣaya ākāraḥ kaścid paricchedaḥ ca antaraḥ sva saṃvidita rūpaḥ jāyamānaḥ lakṣyate tatra yathālakṣaṇam eva iyam meyamāna phala sthitiḥ 
[I,038,ii]	avibhāgaḥ api buddhi ātmā viparyāsita darśanaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvitti bhedavān iva lakṣyate mantra ādi upapluta akṣāṇām yathā mṛd śakala ādayaḥ anyathā eva avabhāsante tad rūpa rahitāḥ api tathā eva adarśanāt teṣām anupapluta cakṣuṣā dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahān alpaḥ api dṛśyate yathā anudarśanam ca iyam meyamāna phala sthitiḥ kriyate avidyamānā api grāhya grāhaka saṃvidām anyathā ekasya bhāvasya nānā rūpa avabhāsinaḥ satyam katham syuḥ ākārāḥ tad eka tvasya hānitaḥ anyasya anyatva hāneḥ ca nābhedaḥ arūpadarśanāt rūpa abhedam hi paśyantī dhīḥ abhedam vyavasyati bhāvāḥ yena nirūpyante tad rūpam na asti tattvataḥ yasmāt ekam anekam ca rūpam teṣām na vidyate sādharmya darśanāt loke bhrāntiḥ nāma upajāyate atadātmani tādātmya vyavasāyena na iha tat adarśanāt jagat yasmin nekasya api tad ātmanaḥ asti iyam api yā tu antarupaplavasam udbhavā doṣa udbhavāt prakṛtyā sā vitatha pratibhāsinī anapekṣita sādharmya dṛś ādiḥ taimira ādi vat iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,039,i_I,039,ii]	bhavatu nāma yathādarśanam pramāṇa ādi vyavasthā vijñaptimātra tāyām sā eva katham sidhyati uktam atra grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇa ayogāt iti api ca saha upalambha niyamāt abhedaḥ nīla tad dhiyoḥ na hi bhinna avabhāsi tve api artha antaram eva rūpam nīlasya anubhavāt tayoḥ saha upalambha niyamāt dvi candra ādi vat na hi anayoḥ eka ākāra anupalambhe anya upalambhaḥ asti na ca etad svabhāva viveke yuktam pratibandha kāraṇa abhāvāt rūpa ālokayoḥ tu tad jñāna utpādana yogya tā pratilambha lakṣaṇaḥ asti pratibandha indriya yogya tā utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ vā iti nānā lokaḥ rūpa upalambhaḥ syāt kāryasya kāraṇa avyabhicārāt na antarīyaka tayā ālokaḥ saha rūpeṇa grāhya lakṣaṇa tvāt gṛhyeta na vā kevalasya api ālokasya darśanāt anālokasya vā rūpasya kaiścid prāṇi viśeṣaiḥ iti na tayoḥ api saha upalambha niyamaḥ nīla ākāra saṃvedanayoḥ tu niyamaḥ eva na sa nānātve yuktaḥ nīla pīta vat 
[I,040,i]	viṣayasya vijñāna hetu tayā upanidheḥ prāk upalambhaḥ paścāt saṃvedanasya iti ced apratyakṣa upalambhasya na artha dṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati na hi viṣaya sattayā viṣaya upalambhaḥ kim tarhi tad upalambha sattayā sā ca aprāmāṇikāḥ na sattā nibandhanān vyavahārān anuruṇaddhi tad aprasiddhau viṣayasya api aprasiddhiḥ iti astaṅgatam viśvam syāt sataḥ api asiddhau sattā vyavahāra ayogya tvāt tasmāt na anupalabhamānaḥ kasyacid saṃvedanam vedayate nāma kiñcid 
[I,041,i]	upalabhyate saṃvedanam anyena iti ced sa tāvat viṣayaḥ sva upalambha kāle na siddhiḥ siddheḥ asiddheḥ anya upalambha kāle tu siddhaḥ iti upalambhe api tadā na siddhaḥ anyadā viparyaye siddhaḥ iti su vyāhṛtam anyena api saṃvedana upalambhe saḥ api asiddhaḥ saṃvedanam na sādhayati iti upalambha antara anugamaḥ tat na tāvat ayam puruṣaḥ kaścid artham pratyeti upalambha niṣṭhām pratīkṣamāṇaḥ ekā siddhau sarva asiddheḥ na ca upalambhānām utpatti niṣṭhā iti andhamūkam jagat syāt kvacid niṣṭhāyām sa svayam ātmānam viṣaya ākāram ca yugapad upalabhate iti tad anye api tathā syuḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt tat siddhaḥ saha upalambha niyamaḥ eka vyāpāre krama ayogāt tasya aviśeṣāt 
[I,042,i_I,042,ii]	saṃvedanam iti api tasya tādātmyāt tathāprathanam na tad anyasya kasyacid ātma saṃvedana vat tatas api na tad artha antare yuktam anartha antara tve tu nīla ādeḥ anubhavāt tad ā ātma bhūtaḥ prakāśate tathā iti nīla ādi anubhavaḥ syāt sa ca tādātmyāt tathā aprakāśamānaḥ api sva para ātmanoḥ prakāśakaḥ syāt prakāśa vat tasmāt grāhaka ākāraḥ sva saṃvidaḥ sādhanam iṣṭam tatas asyāḥ tad bhāva vyavasthāpanāt 
[I,042,iii]	tatra ātma viṣaye māne yathā rāga ādi vedanam iyam sarvatra saṃyojyā māna meya phala sthitiḥ tatra api anubhava ātma tvāt te yogyāḥ sva ātma saṃvidi iti sā yogyatā mānam ātmā meyaḥ phalam sva vid grāhaka ākāra saṅkhyātā pariccheda ātma tā ātmani sā yogyatā iti ca proktam pramāṇam sva ātma vedanam iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,043,i_I,043,v]	bāhye api arthe tatas abhedaḥ bhāsamāna artha tadvidoḥ sati api bāhye arthe saha upalambha vedanābhyām bhāsamānasya nīla ādeḥ tad saṃvidaḥ ca avivekaḥ siddhaḥ dvairūpyam tat dhiyaḥ viṣaya jñāna rūpābhyām atas dvi rūpā buddhiḥ siddhā bhavati yadi bhāsamānaḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ buddheḥ abhinnaḥ tatas bhinnam asti iti kutas bāhya siddhiḥ syāt vyatirekataḥ 
[I,043,vi]	satsu sama artheṣu anyeṣu hetuṣu jñāna kārya aniṣpattiḥ kāraṇa antara vaikalyam sūcayati sa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ syāt yadi atra kaścid upādāna viśeṣa abhāva kṛtam kārya vyatirekam na brūyāt saḥ api katham sarva jñānānām viṣayam vyatirecayan nupaplava itarayoḥ pramāṇa itara tām brūyāt viśeṣa abhāvāt upaplava vāsanā visandhi doṣāt aprabuddhasya api anāśvāsikam vyavahāram utpaśyan nekam apramāṇam ācakṣīta aparam āsaṃsāram aviśliṣṭa anubandham dṛḍha vāsana tvāt iha vyavahāra avisaṃvāda apekṣayā pramāṇam sāṃvyavahārikasya ca etat pramāṇasya rūpam uktam atra api pare mūḍhāḥ visaṃvādayanti lokam iti cintā mayīm eva tu prajñām anuśīlayantaḥ vibhrama viveka nirmalam anapāyi pāramarthika pramāṇam abhimukhīkurvanti tat api leśataḥ sūcitam eva iti 
[I,045,i_I,045,ii]	anumānam dvidhā sva artham para artham ca jñāna abhidhāna rūpa tvāt na prāprapratipatti nibandhane apṛthak vacanam śabdasya viśeṣa abhāvāt iti ced na pravṛtti bhedāt arthaḥ hi liṅginam gamayati tat liṅgam śabdaḥ iti na lakṣaṇa antarasya avācya tvāt yat kvacid adṛṣṭam tasya yatra pratibandhaḥ tad vidaḥ tasya tat gamakam tatra iti vastu gatiḥ tatra gamaka lakṣaṇa vidhānena pratipipādayiṣoḥ vacana anukrama darśanam kṛtam eva anyathā abhidhāne gamaka dharmāt yotanāt na hi ye yathā yam artham vidanti vacana jñāḥ te tad pratipādane punar upadeśa antaram apekṣante satyam etat tathā api bāla vyutpatti nimittaḥ ayam ārambhaḥ yathāvastu pratipadyamānāḥ api tad dharma avyāpti vyatirekābhyām nigadantaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ avinā abhāva avacanāt upamāna sādhya tadā vṛtti vacanānām ca prayogāt 
[I,046,i_I,046,iii]	tatra sva artham tri rūpāt liṅgataḥ artha dṛś tri lakṣaṇāt liṅgāt yat anumeye arthe jñānam tat sva artham anumānam pratyakṣa vat asya phala vikalpaḥ vijñeyaḥ tat etat atasmin tad grahāt bhrāntiḥ api sambandhataḥ pramā sva pratibhāse anarthe artha adhyavasāyena pravartanāt bhrāntiḥ api artha sambandhena tat avyabhicārāt pramāṇam na hi svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā bhāva kāraṇa vyatireke bhavataḥ abhedāt ātma niṣpatteḥ ca tathā tayoḥ abhāve tad jam jñānam tad prabhavā vā bhāva kāraṇa pratipattiḥ tathā sati dṛśye vastuni avikala tad anya kāraṇasya darśanasya vrāvṛttiḥ na ca saḥ eva pratibhāsaḥ arthaḥ yuktaḥ tasya punar pratyakṣena anyathā darśanāt 
[I,047,i]	yaḥ hi bhāvaḥ yathābhūtaḥ sa tādṛś liṅga cetasaḥ hetuḥ tad jā tathābhūte tasmāt vastuni liṅgi dhīḥ liṅga liṅgi dhiyoḥ evam pāramparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhāt tad ābhāsa śūnyayoḥ api avañcanam tasyāḥ tad rūpa śūnyāyāḥ tad rūpa adhyavasāyataḥ tad rūpā vañcaka tve api kṛtā bhrānti vyavasthitiḥ maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ maṇi buddhyā abhidhāvataḥ mithyājñāna aviśeṣe api viśeṣaḥ artha kriyām prati yathā tathā yathārtha tve api anumāna tad ābhayoḥ artha kriyā anurodhena pramāṇa tvam vyavasthitam iti saṅgrahaślokāḥ 
[I,048,i]	atas eva pramāṇyam vastu viṣayam dvayoḥ pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ artha kriyā yogya viṣaya tvāt vicārasya sukha duḥkha sādhane jñātvā yathārham pratipitsavaḥ hi kiñcid parīkṣante prekṣā pūrva kāriṇaḥ na vyasani tayā na ca anumāna pratibhāsaḥ eva artha sādhanam niruddhe api artha sādhane vastuni tasya anirodhāt tatas ca kasyacid arthasya asiddheḥ atas eva sat api sāmānyam na arthaḥ tasmāt vastu rūpā visaṃvādanam eva asya api pramāṇyam tad pratibaddha vaḥ tu liṅga apekṣaṇāt ca 
[I,048,ii]	ācāryaḥ punar artha bhidām jagau pratibhāsasya bhinna tvāt ekasmin tad ayogataḥ na hi ekasya tau anyonya vilakṣaṇau ākārau yujyete tad ālambana viṣaya bhedāt pramāṇayoḥ viṣaya bhedam āha na pramāṇa vyāpāra viṣaya bhedāt bhedaḥ iti api asya abheda pratiṣedhaḥ eva draṣṭavyaḥ na nānā viṣaya tā anumāna vikalpasya nirviṣaya tvāt tad pratibhāsasya sva viṣaya sammata anvaya vyatirekān anuvidhānāt pratyakṣa vat sāmānyasya ca vastunaḥ anya tvena avācya tvāt 
[I,049,i]	katham idānīm dvayoḥ api prāmāṇyasya vastu viṣaya tve sāmānyasya pratipattiḥ liṅgāt anyatas sva lakṣaṇasya iti āha atad rūpa parāvṛtta vastu mātra prasādhanāt sāmānya viṣayam proktam liṅgam bheda apratiṣṭhiteḥ yad prayojanāḥ hi arthāḥ jñātum iṣṭāḥ tad viparyaya vyatirekiṇaḥ artha mātrasya upanidhāyakam liṅgam iti sāmānya viṣayam proktam tatas bheda apratiṣṭhānāt na vastu sattā viprakarṣāt liṅga pratipatteḥ api tathārūpa tvāt anvaya apekṣaṇāt ca itarat punar bheda antara vimarśa vivekena pratiṣṭhitena eva rūpeṇa akriyate iti sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam aparasmāt artha pratipatteḥ na tu evam para aṅgāt pratītiḥ tasya asāmarthyāt artha avisaṃvādaḥ tu dvayoḥ api tulyaḥ iti vastu viṣyam prāmāṇyam 
[I,050,i_I,050,ii]	tat punar trairūpyam anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati niścitā anumeyaḥ atra jijñāsita viśeṣaḥ dharmī tatra darśanam pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā tathā tad tulyaḥ eva ca dharmi viśiṣṭasya anyatra vṛtti virodhaḥ aviśeṣaṇe vā na anumeya dharma tā iti ced na ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt 
[I,050,iii]	ayogam yogam aparaiḥ atyanta ayogam eva ca vyavacchinatti dharmasya nipātaḥ vyatirecakaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyābhyām kriyayā ca saha uditaḥ vivakṣātaḥ aprayoge api tasya arthaḥ ayam pratīyate vyavaccheda phalam vākyam yatas caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ nīlam sarojam iti vā yathā pratiyogi vyavacchedaḥ tatra api artheṣu gamyate tathā prasiddheḥ sāmarthyāt vivakṣā anugamāt dhvaneḥ tad ayoga vyavacchedāt dharmī dharma viśeṣaṇam tad viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ na niranvaya doṣa bhāj iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,051,i_I,051,ii]	anya yoga vyavacchedena ca viśeṣaṇaḥ ekasya tad bhāve anyasya atattvam syāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya yoginaḥ ca nipātasya aviśeṣaḥ etena sādhya dharme api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ unneyaḥ tena sati api viśeṣaṇe na ananvayaḥ tathā sāmānyam ca sādhyam na ca siddha sādhanam tad ayoga vyavacchedasya asiddheḥ tad tulyaḥ eva iti avadhāraṇāt dharmiṇī avṛttiḥ iti ced na anya niṣedha artha tvāt tatra vṛttau labdhāyām samuccīyamāna avadhāraṇam anyat vyavacchinnatti naram ca nārāyaṇam eva ca ādasu svatas sutau dvau janayām babhūva iti yathā 
[I,052,i]	tasya sādhyasa jātīya vṛttinaḥ liṅgasya asati na astitā tṛtīyam rūpam sā ca niścitā ante vacanāt niścita tvam triṣu api rūpeṣu draṣṭavyam artha antara svabhāvayoḥ prabhava tanmātra anubandha siddhau kāraṇa bhāva anupalabdhyā grāhya viṣayayā siddhā na itarayā iti yāvat anupalabdhau api viparyaye pratyakṣa vṛttiḥ vyatireka niścayaḥ 
[I,052,ii]	tad tulyaḥ eva asti iti vyatireke siddhe asati nāstita abhidhānam asati eva na astitāḥ na anyatra na viruddhaḥ iti niyama artham iti āha tatra asambhavāt eva na anya dharma vṛtti niṣedha āśaṅkā viruddha niṣedhe api tatra eva niṣedhe doṣaḥ syāt na ca tad tulyaḥ eva vṛttiḥ iti atad tulyaḥ viruddhaḥ eva yena tatas eva vyatirekāt agniḥ auṣṇyam na gamayet kim tarhi tad tulya vyatirekaḥ api tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti avācyam eva tṛtīyam rūpam syāt prayoga darśana artha tvāt adoṣaḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ niścita vyāptikam ekam api rūpam prayuktam arthāpattyā dvitīyam gamayati iti atas ekasya prayogaḥ syāt iti 
[I,053,i_I,053,ii]	nanu śrāvaṇa tvam vyatireki api agamakam na avyatirekāt na hi śrāvaṇa tvam kutaścid vyaticiyate sandeha sādhanāt vyatirekiṇaḥ ca sandeha ayogāt kṛtaka tvāt iva anitya tve vastu dharmasya sarva vastunaḥ vyāvṛtti virodhāt vṛtti śaṅkayā eva tatas saṃśayaḥ anvayaḥ tu na dṛṣṭaḥ iti vyatirekī kathyate na ca evaṃvidhaḥ vyatirekaḥ gamakaḥ yaḥ tu gamakaḥ sa saṃvarṇitaḥ eva sa ca na asati anvaye śakyaḥ darśayitum tad bhāva hetu bhāvayoḥ darśana sādhana tvāt dvi rūpam tarhi liṅgam na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ pṛthak rūpa tvāt te tu ekena api vākyena śakye darśayitum iti prayoga samāsaḥ ucyate na rūpa samāsaḥ tathā hi āha artha āpattyā vā anyatareṇa ubhaya pradarśanāt iti 
[I,053,iii]	na asati nāstita asiddhiḥ asataḥ hi adhikaraṇa tva ādi ayogāt iti aparaḥ paśavaḥ api hi tāvat yat ayuktam paśyanti na tadā eva tat ācaranti saḥ ayam paśoḥ api paśuḥ mahataḥ api mahīyasaḥ yat avamanyate iti kim anyadana ātma jña tāyāḥ saḥ ayam taiḥ eva artha vyatireka samāveśibhiḥ padaiḥ asatsu vyavahāra ayogam darśayan param pratiruṇaddhi iti vyaktam etat rāja śāsanam na ca svayam abrūvan param bodhayitum īśaḥ brūvan vā doṣam imam parihartum asati hetoḥ apratiṣedhe vidhiḥ prāptaḥ abhāva vyatireka lakṣaṇa tvāt asya sā eva tāvat asataḥ na nivṛttiḥ iti nivṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ katham iṣṭā 
[I,054,i^1]	nivṛtti abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vastu bhāvaḥ asataḥ api san vastu abhāvaḥ tu na asti iti paśya vā andhya vijṛmbhitam nivṛttiḥ yadi tasmin na hetoḥ vṛttiḥ kim iṣyate sā api na pratiṣedhaḥ ayam nivṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate vidhānam pratiṣedham ca muktvā śabdaḥ asti na aparaḥ vyavahāraḥ sa ca asatsu na iti prāptā atra mūka tā satām ca na niṣedhaḥ asti saḥ asatsu ca na vartate jagati anena nyāyena nañarthaḥ pralayam gataḥ deśa kāla niṣedhaḥ ced yathā asti sa niṣidhyate na tathā na yathā saḥ asti tathā api na niṣidhyate tasmāt āśritya śabda atham bhāva abhāva samāśrayam abāhya āśrayam atra iṣṭam sarvam vidhi niṣedhanam tābhyām sa dharmī sambaddhaḥ khyāti abhāve api tādṛśaḥ śabda pravṛtteḥ asti iti saḥ api iṣṭaḥ vyavahāra bhāj 
[I,054,i^2]	 anyathā syāt padārthānām vidhāna pratiṣedhane eka dharmasya sarva ātma vidhāna pratiṣedhanam anānātma tayā bhede nānā vidhi niṣedha vat eka dharmiṇī a saṃhāraḥ vidhāna pratiṣedhayoḥ ekam dharmiṇam uddiśya nānā dharma samāśrayam vidhau ekasya tad bhājam iva anyeṣām upekṣakam niṣedhe tad viviktam ca tad anyeṣām apekṣakam vyavahāram asatya artham prakalpayati dhīḥ yathā tam tathā eva avikalpya artha bheda āśrayam upāgatāḥ anādi vāsanā udbhūtam bādhante artham na laukikam tad phalaḥ atat phalaḥ ca arthaḥ bhinnaḥ ekaḥ tatas tatas taiḥ taiḥ upaplavaiḥ nīta sañcaya apacayaiḥ iva atadvān api sambandhāt kutaścid upanīyate dṛṣṭim bheda āśrayaiḥ te api tasmāt ajñāta viplavāḥ iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,056,i_I,056,ii]	etad lakṣaṇā anupalambha ātma kāri a ākhyāḥ hetavaḥ trayaḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvaḥ kāryam ca iti trīṇi eva liṅgāni yathā pradeśa viśeṣe kvacid na ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ yadi hi syāt upalabhya sattvaḥ eva syāt na anyathā iti vṛkṣaḥ ayam śiṃśapā tvāt agniḥ atra dhūmāt atra dvau vastu sādhanau ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ svabhāva pratibandhe hi sati arthaḥ artham na vyabhicarati sa ca tad ātma tvāt 
[I,056,iii]	tad ātma tve sādhya sādhana bheda abhāvaḥ iti ced na dharma bheda parikalpanāt tathā ca āha sarve eva ayam anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ buddhi ārūḍhena dharma dharmi nyāyena iti dharma dharmi tayā bhedaḥ buddhi parikalpitaḥ na arthaḥ api vikalpa bhedānām sva tantrāṇām anartha āśraya tvāt tad kalpita viṣayāt artha pratītau anartha pratilambhaḥ syāt sarva bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva para bhāvābhyām yasmāt vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ tasmāt yatas yatas arthānām vyāvṛttiḥ tad nibandhanāḥ jāti bhedāḥ prakalpyante tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tasmāt yaḥ yena dharmeṇa viśeṣaḥ sampratīyate na sa śakyaḥ tatas anyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,057,i_I,057,iii]	kāryasya api svabhāva pratibandhaḥ tad svabhāvasya tad utpatteḥ iti etau dvau anumeya pratyayau sākṣāt anutpatteḥ atad pratibhāsi tve api tad utpatteḥ tad avyabhicāriṇau iti pramāṇam pratyakṣa vat asattā niścaya phalaḥ anupalambhaḥ asat vyavahāra pravartana phalaḥ anupalambhaḥ tat avyabhicārī siddhe vyavahāre sataḥ viṣayasya avyabhicārāt 
[I,058,i]	anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt asattāyām sādhyāyām upalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ api anyayā anupalabdhyā sādhyate iti anavasthānāt apratipattiḥ syāt atha upalabdhi abhāvaḥ vinā anupalabdhyā syāt tathā sattā abhāvaḥ api syāt iti apārthika anupalabdhiḥ atha anya upalabdhyā anupalabdhi siddhiḥ iti pratyakṣa siddhāḥ na anupalabdheḥ tathā anya sattayā asattā kim na sidhyati yadā punar evaṃvidha anupalabdhiḥ eva asatām asattā tadā siddhena viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ asan jñāna śabda vyavahārān pratipadyate pratipādayati ca viṣaya pradarśanena samaye pravartanāt yathā gauḥ ayam sāsna ādi samudāya ātmaka tvāt iti tathā ca dṛṣṭānta asiddhi codanā api prativyūḍhā viṣaya pratipattau api apratipanna viṣayiṇām darśanāt 
[I,058,ii]	bhāva vyatirekaḥ hi abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ upalabdheḥ sā katham asattā bhāvasya upalambha nivṛttyā vā katham abhāvaḥ kārya vyatireke api kāraṇa abhāva asiddheḥ upalambha nibandhanā hi tādṛśām sattā prajñaptiḥ upalabdhi yogya svabhāvasya anya hetu sākalye tat avyabhicārāt ca upalambhaḥ sattā ucyate sāmagrī pariṇām āpekṣa tvāt syāt vyabhicāraḥ api iti na kārya kāle abhāva pratipatteḥ anya upalambhe tad anupalambha siddheḥ prabhāvavataḥ adhiṣṭhānāt sataḥ api anupalabdhiḥ iti na viṣaya indriyayoḥ ekasya dvayoḥ vā ananyathā tve ayogāt adhiṣṭhānasya tad saṃskāre tu syāt anupalambhaḥ tadā api tathāvidha indriya grāhya abhāvaḥ asti eva tasmāt jñānam tad yogya tā vā asya sattā tad vyatirekaḥ anupalabdhiḥ asattā tayā viṣayī sādhyate etena iha kāraṇasya kārya vyabhicāraḥ pratyuktaḥ atra api anupalabdhyā tad nimittaḥ siddhaḥ vyavahāraḥ api tad nimitta sattā sādhyate anya naimittika vat 
[I,059,i_I,060,ii]	sā eva tāvat anupalabdhiḥ katham siddhā iti ced etat uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ sa ca ayam anupalmbhaḥ caturvidhaḥ pravṛtti bhedāt yāvān kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvaḥ anupalabdheḥ tathā hi sa dividhā kriyate kasyacid vidhinā pratiṣedhena vā vidhau viruddhaḥ vā vidhīyeta aviruddhaḥ vā aviruddhasya api sahabhāva virodha abhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ viruddhasya api anupalabdhim antareṇa virodha apratipattiḥ tathā hi aparyanta kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt virodha gatiḥ sa ca anupalabdheḥ anyonya vyatireka sthita lakṣaṇa tā vā virodhaḥ nitya aniyatva vat tatra api eka upalabdhyā anya anupalabdhiḥ eva ucyate anyathā hi aniṣiddha upalabdheḥ abhāva asiddeḥ eka niṣedhena anya abhāva sādhane siddhā eva anupalabdhiḥ niṣedhasya anupalabdhi rūpa tvāt tatra api artha antara niṣedhe sādhye kārya kāraṇayoḥ anubhayasi vā niṣedhaḥ hetuḥ tatra api anubhayasya apratibandhāt tad abhāve anya abhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[I,061,i]	kārya anupalabdhau pai na avaśyam kāraṇāni tadvanti bhavanti iti kutas tad abhāvaḥ śaktam kāraṇam na aśaktam na ca śaktiḥ kenacid pratibandhum śakyate antya avasthāyām pariṇāma abhāvāt kṣaṇasya avivekāt kārya utpatti viguṇa utpādana lakṣaṇa tvāt pratibadhasya anyathā akiñcitkarasya apratibandhāt bhavati eva tādṛśasya kāraṇasya kārya vivekāt abhāva gatiḥ yathā na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni dhūma kāraṇāni santi dhūma abhāvāt iti tat kāryam hetu vyāpti avyatirekāt tad svabhāva aviśiṣṭam iti tad anupalambhaḥ svabhāva anupalambhaḥ eva uktaḥ tathā tad viruddha upalambhaḥ yathā na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni śīta kāraṇāni santi agneḥ iti kāraṇa dravya sāmānyam abhipretya kārya anupalmbhaḥ agamakaḥ ucyate yathā na agniḥ atra dhūma abhāvāt iti kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ abhāvam gamayati svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu svayam asattā eva tatra kevalam viṣayī sādhyate abhāvaḥ vā tad bhāva vyāpinaḥ kāryasya abhāvena yadā api vyāpaka dharma anupalabdhyā vyāpya abhāvam āha tadā api abhāvaḥ eva 
[I,062,i_I,062,ii]	tat evam vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām kasyacid niṣedhe sarva gamakānām anupalabdhiḥ rūpam na aparaḥ partiṣedha hetuḥ sā iyam pratiṣedha viṣaya anupalabdhiḥ prayoga bhedena caturdhā bhvati viruddha siddhyā yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra agneḥ iti etena vyāpaka viruddha siddhiḥ uktā veditavyā yathā na tuṣāra sparśaḥ atra agneḥ iti viruddha kārya siddhyā yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra dhūmāt iti hetu asiddhyā yathā na dhūmaḥ atra anagneḥ iti svabhāva asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anupalabdheḥ iti etena vyāpaka svabhāva asiddhiḥ uktā veditavyā yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt iti sarvatra ca asyām abhāva vyavahāra sādhanyām anupalabdhau dṛśya ātmanām eva teṣām tad viruddhānām ca sannihitā anya upalambha kāraṇāt asiddhiḥ siddhiḥ ca veditavyā anyeṣām hetu phala bhāva abhāva virodha asiddheḥ 
[I,063,i_I,063,ii]	dṛśyasya darśana abhāva kāraṇā sambhave sati bhāvasya anupalabdhasya bhāva abhāvaḥ pratīyate iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ yadi viruddha kārya upalabdhyā api abhāva siddhiḥ tad kāraṇa upalabdhyā kim na sidhyati na tat vyabhicārāt yathā na śīta sparśaḥ atra kāṣṭhāt iti kāraṇānām kārya ārambha aniyamāt na avaśyam śīta bādhakaḥ agniḥ yatas tad abhāvaḥ gamyeta antyasya avasthā viśeṣasya avyabhicāraḥ iti ced na tatas kārya utpatteḥ akṣepāt ā antya lakṣaṇa utpatteḥ pratibadhaḥ sambhāvyate antya lakṣaṇe apratibandhaḥ tad liṅga darśanāt sambandha smṛti apekṣiṇaḥ anumeya pratipattau tad uptpatteḥ prāk kāryam eva antyakṣaṇa anantara tvāt utpannam pratyakṣībhavati na ca apratyakṣe kārye kāraṇa bhāva gatiḥ yatas kāranāt tat pratīyeta tasmāt na kāraṇāt kārya siddhiḥ 
[I,063,iii]	nimittayoḥ punar virodhe gamikā eva yathā na asya roma harṣa ādi viśeṣāḥ santi sannihita dahana viśeṣa viruddhasya paritāpasya hetoḥ agneḥ śītena virodhāt śīta vicchede tad kāryasya api abhāvaḥ iti etena tad kāryāt api tad viruddha kārya abhāva gatiḥ uktā veditavyā yathā roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣavān ayam pradeśaḥ dhūmāt iti ittham ca hetu asiddhyā eva tad viruddha siddhiḥ prāk eva nirdiṣṭā iti iyam prayoga bhedāt daśāvidha anupalabdhiḥ 
[I,064,i_I,064,iii]	ittham viruddha kārye api deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt bhasma iva aśīta sādhane iti antaraślokaḥ na asattā niścayaḥ vipra karṣiṇām trividhā hi viprakarṣiṇaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva vipra karṣaiḥ na teṣu anupalambhaḥ abhāvam gamayati sat avaśyam kenacid upalabhyate vyatīta asamprāpta upalambham vā tat katham na anupalambhāt abhāvaḥ na sarva upalambha nivṛtteḥ atra āliṅga tvāt ātma parayoḥ apratipatteḥ tasmāt ayam ātma upalambha nivṛttim eva pramāṇayan pratikṣipati sā vipakṛṣṭeṣu api asti na ca te na santi eva 
[I,065,i]	tatra api sati pratyakṣa anumāna āgamānām ekasya vṛttiḥ iti ced na śāstrasya kvacid anadhikārāt śāstram hi pravartamānam puruṣa artha sādhanam kvacid upāyam āśritya pravartate anyathā sambaddha pralāpasya aprāmāṇyāt tatra ca prakaraṇe bahavaḥ arthāḥ na avaśyam nirdeśyāḥ yathā pratyātma niyatāḥ kāścana puruṣāṇām cetaḥ vṛttayaḥ aniyata nimitta bhāvinyaḥ deśa kāla vyavahitāḥ vā prakaraṇa anupayoginaḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ na tān śāstram viṣayīkaroti na ca teṣām tathā aviprakṛṣṭānām sva sāmarthya upadhānāt jñāna utpādana śaktiḥ na ca avaśyam eṣām kārya upalambhaḥ yena anumīyeran na ca te pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api na santi iti śakyante vyavasātum 
[I,065,ii]	yaḥ api jñāpaka abhāvāt atīndriyaḥ partikṣipyate arthaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ vā yathā na asti virakam cetaḥ devatā viśeṣaḥ vā na asti dāna hiṃsā ādi virati cetanānām abhyupadaya hetuta iti pratyakṣe api arthe phalasya anantarya abhāvāt atad phala sādharmyāt tad viparyāsaḥ eṣaḥ vyavahitānām api hi hetoḥ phalānām utpattiḥ darśanāt mūṣika alarka viṣa vikāra vat tad bhāva virodha abhāvāt atra anupalabdhi mātram apramāṇam bhāve kim pramāṇam iti ced atas eva saṃśayaḥ astu bhavet vā pramāṇam iti apratikṣepaḥ tat atra keṣāñcid svabhāvānām arthānām vā darśana pāṭava abhāvāt kāraṇānām kārya utpādana niyama abhāvāt ca bhavet jñāpakā siddhiḥ neyatā tad abhāvaḥ punar paryāyeṇa keṣāñcid abhivyakteḥ 
[I,066,i_I,066,ii]	na api śabdāḥ yathābhāvam vartante yatas tebhyaḥ artha prakṛtiḥ niścīyeta te hi vaktuḥ vivakṣā vṛttayaḥ iti tat na antarīyakāḥ tām eva gamayeyuḥ na ca puruṣa icchāḥ sarvāḥ yathā artha bhāvinyaḥ na ca tad apratibaddha svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ anyam gamayati yathā artha darśana ādi guṇa yuktaḥ puruṣaḥ āptaḥ tad praṇītaḥ āgamaḥ avisamvādi iti ced iṣṭaḥ ayam arthaḥ śakyeta jñātum saḥ atiśayaḥ yadi 
[I,066,iii]	sarve eva āgamam anāgamam vā pravṛtti kāmaḥ anveṣate prekṣā pūrva kārī na vyasanena tasya puruṣa parīkṣayā pravṛttau apravṛttiḥ eva tathābhūtasya jñātum aśakya tvāt na aniṣṭeḥ tādṛśām avitatha abhidhānāt tathā hi na anya guṇa doṣa niścaye liṅgam asti te hi cetaḥ dharma tvena atīndriya tvāt sva prabhava kāya vāc vyavahāra anumeyāḥ syuḥ vyavahārāḥ ca prāyaśas buddhi pūrvam anyathā api kartum śakyante puruṣa icchā vṛtti tvāt teṣām ca citra abhisandhi tvāt tat ayam liṅga saṅkarāt katham aniścinvan pratipadyeta 
[I,067,i]	mā bhūt puruṣa āśrayam vacanam āgamaḥ praṇetuḥ duranvayatvāt apauruṣeyam avitatham syāt na tasya ayogāt artha abhidhāne puruṣa upadeśa apekṣa tvāt ca upalambha yogya ayogya ātmanoḥ prāpti parityāgayoḥ svabhāva antara utpatti hāninā antarīyaka tvāt nityam tad ātmatāyām kadācid upalambha anupalambha abhāva prasaṅgāt na api para apekṣā tasya tatra akiñcitkara tvāt anya karaṇe tasya iti sambandha ayogāt upakārasya tad sambandhe kaḥ sambandhaḥ anupakārya upakārakayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ ced saḥ api tad ātmānupakāre na sidhyati para ātmani tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ anavasthā ca janya janaka bhāve saḥ anapekṣasya nityam syāt apekṣāyām ca pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt kādācid kaḥ śabdasya upalambha yogyaḥ ātmā sa ca puruṣa vyāpāra anvavyatireka anuvidhāyī pauruṣeyaḥ anyathā api na antarīyaka tā bhavān na para ātmanaḥ pratipattiḥ arthasya 
[I,068,i]	na hi sattā śabdasya artha viśeṣe pratibaddhā tasyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt indriya viṣaya vat paraspara yogya tā niyāmikā iti ced na tatra api eka pratiniyamasya tad janma lakṣaṇa tvāt tad upakṛtam indriyam jñānam janayati iti a anyathā anupakāriṇaḥ anapekṣā syāt viṣaya antara vat tena eva kasmāt upakriyate iti ced atra vastu svabhāvaiḥ uttaram vācyam yaḥ evam bhavanti tathā hi na yava aṅkuraḥ śāli bījāt bhavati api tu yava bījāt evam śabdānām api yadi arthebhyaḥ janma syāt syāt yogyatā niyamaḥ tad abhāve asya idam iti na sidhyati na api arthavat tā arthebhyaḥ jñāpana icchā tayā artha jñāpanāya prayujyante iti tas tadvantaḥ syuḥ kāya vijñapti ādi vat atadāgamebhyaḥ na tatra pratītiḥ ākāśāt iva ghaṭa ādiṣu 
[I,068,ii]	na vai śabda svabhāvaḥ niyataḥ artheṣu yatas tad utpattiḥ kim tarhi jñāpana śaktiḥ ayam asya eva pratipādakaḥ iti sā api tatra pratibaddhāḥ bhāva abhāvābhyām kārya tām na atipatati tanmātra lakṣaṇa tvāt anyeṣu api asyāḥ tat yvatirame ca niyama ayogāt śakteḥ ca anartha antara tvāt saḥ eva svabhāva niyamaḥ artha antara tve tatas artheṣu jñāna utpattiḥ iti śabdaḥ avācakaḥ syāt tasya iti sambandhaḥ ca na sidhyati tasmāt sarvathā sarve eva kvacid niyamaḥ svabhāva bhūtaḥ sva hetu prakṛteḥ niyāmakasya janakatām eva dīpayati 
[I,069,i]	na vai na antarīyaka tayā śabdāt artha pratipattiḥ api tu yogyatayā pradīpāt iva rūpe tad bhāva abhāvayoḥ darśana adarśana smṛti apekṣe hi śabda liṅge sva viṣayam pratipādayataḥ adarśana smṛti vipra moṣayoḥ apratipatteḥ sandehe sandehāt bahuṣu darśane ca ekatra draṣṭuḥ abhāvāt punar darśane ca bhāvāt viśeṣa antara dṛṣṭau anyathā prayoge viparyayāt yathā darśana pratīteḥ darśana parāvṛttau ca artha antara parigrahāt kalimāryādi śabdānām iva matta kāla atiśaya varṣa upasarga ādiṣu dramih ārya deśayoḥ 
[I,070,i]	tasmāt ime darśanam adarśanam ca apekṣamāṇaḥ tad sādhanam avyabhicāram eva pratipādane liṅga vat avalambante anupadeśāt apratipatteḥ upadeśe ca śabdānām artheṣu anāvaraṇāt tat eva puruṣa icchāyāḥ svātantryam vyavasthām vidhurayati vistareṇa ca ayam asmābhiḥ vādaḥ pramāṇa vārttike pratiṣiddhaḥ iti na iha pratanyante 
[I,070,ii^1]	svayam rāga ādimān na artham vetti vedasya na anyatas na vedayati vedaḥ api veda arthasya kutas gatiḥ tena agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti śrutau khādet śva māṃsam iti eṣa na arthaḥ iti atra kā pramā prasiddhaḥ loka vādaḥ ced tatra kaḥ atīndriya artha dṛś aneka artheṣu śabdeṣu yena arthaḥ ayam vivecitaḥ svarga uḥ vaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ arūḍha artha vācakaḥ śabda antareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśyeva astu kalpanā aprasiddha artha yogasya tad prasiddhi prasādhane na asiddhārthaḥ svayam śaktaḥ tulyaḥ paryanuyogataḥ prasiddhiḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ pramāṇam sa ca na iṣyate tatas ca bhūyas artha gatiḥ kim etat dviṣṭa kāmitam atha prasiddhim ullaṅghya kalpane kim nibandhanam prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tad grahe kim nibandhanam utpāditā prasiddhyā eva śaṅkā śabda artha niścaye yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām tatra dṛśyate 
[I,070,ii^2]	na yukti bādhā yatra asti tat grāhyam laukikam yadi gṛhyate vāta putrīyam kim na yuktyā na bādhitam āgama artha āśrayā yuktiḥ atyakṣeṣu na ca itarā tad arthasya apratiṣṭhānāt yukteḥ atra na sambhavaḥ anyathā asambhava abhāvāt nānā śakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām eṣa sthāṇuḥ ayam mārgaḥ iti vakti iti kaścana anyaḥ svayam bravīmi iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ parīkṣyatām sarvatra yogyasya eka artha dyotane niyatiḥ kutas jñātāḥ vā atīndriyāḥ kena vivakṣā vacanāt ṛte vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṅketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ apauruṣeye sā na asti tasya sā ekārtha tā kutas svabhāva niyame anyatra na yojyeta tayā punar saṅketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutas yatra svātantryam icchāyāḥ niyamaḥ nāma tatra kaḥ dyotayet tena saṅketaḥ na iṣṭām eva asya yogyatām iti antaraślokāḥ 
[I,072,i]	eka deśa avisaṃvādanam api āgama lakṣaṇam āhuḥ tad vipakṣe adarśana amātrāt avyabhicāra asidhi āniścita artham nanu prayoga sāmarthyāt eva artha anubandhaḥ siddhaḥ śabdānām asati viṣaye aprayogāt yuktam etat kim tu tathā prasiddhau api icchāyāḥ anivāraṇāt anyathā api loke vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ tasmāt na āgamasya api nivṛttiḥ artha abhāvam gamayati 
[I,073,i_I,073,ii]	pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ abhāva sādhanī sakala kāraṇasya asya artha sattāyām abhāva asambhavāt tatra arvāk darśanasya ātma pratyakṣa nivṛtti pramāṇayataḥ tad grahaṇa yogya pratiṣedhaḥ yuktaḥ na ca sarvam evam iti apratiṣedhaḥ sarvatra pravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrva tvāt saḥ apravṛtti phalaḥ mataḥ saḥ ayam viprakṛṣṭa viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna abhāvaḥ sañjñāna śabda vyavahāra pratiṣedha phalaḥ upalabdhi pūrvaka tvāt teṣām 
[I,073,iii]	anyaḥ pravartana phalaḥ tad nimittasya darśanāt pūrvakaḥ punar anupalambhaḥ asañjñāna śabda vyavahāra pravartana phalaḥ api viṣaya darśanena prasiddhasya vyavahārasya sādhanāt dvayoḥ api anupalabdhyoḥ sva viparyaya hetu abhāva abhāvābhyām sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha phala tvam tulyam ekatra saṃśayāt anyatra viparyayāt tatra dvitīyā sat vyavahāra niṣedha upayogāt pramāṇam uktā na tu vyatireka darśana ādau upayujyate saṃśayāt aniścita jñāpana aṅgāt pratīteḥ prathamā tu atra pramāṇam niścaya phala tvāt 
[I,074,i_I,074,ii]	tad bhāva mātra anvayini svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ātmani tādātmyam hi arthasya tanmātra anurodhini eva na anyāyatte tad bhāve abhūtasya paścāt tādātmya virodhāt kāraṇānām ca kārya vyabhicārāt tasmāt tad bhāva mātra anubandhinam eva ātmanaḥ svabhāvaḥ gamakaḥ sa ca ayam hetu tvena upādīyamānaḥ upādhi apekṣaḥ śuddhaḥ vā nāśe kāryatva sattva vat upādīyate apekṣita para vyāpāraḥ hi svabhāva niṣpattau bhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ tena iyam kṛtaka śrutiḥ svabhāva abhidhāyinī api para upādhim enam ākṣipati etena pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādayaḥ api vyākhyātāḥ evam upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ kvacid svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ucyate kvacid anapekṣaḥ yathā anitya tvaḥ eva sattvam kvacid svabhāva bhūta dharma bheda prigraheṇa yathā tatra eva utpattiḥ anayā diśāḥ anye api svabhāva hetu pravibhāgāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ 
[I,075,i]	tasya ca svabhāvasya svena sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptiḥ yadi pramāṇena niścīyate tadā gamakaḥ aniścitāyām tu vyāptau dharmi samāśraye vā tad svabhāvatayā gamakasya āgamaka tvāt na hi prakāśa tayā prakāśayan pradīpaḥ tad rūpa apratipattau svām artha kriyām karoti tasmāt niścitaḥ vyāpyaḥ gamakaḥ vyāpakaḥ gamyaḥ tasya vyāpyasya ayam nivartakaḥ vyāpaka dharmaḥ svayam nivartamānaḥ evam hi ayam asya vyāpakaḥ siddhaḥ bhavati yadi asya abhāve na bhavet tat anena dvividhasya api hetuḥ gamya gamaka tā lakṣaṇam uktam veditavyam 
[I,075,ii]	dvividhaḥ hi hetuḥ prayogataḥ sādharmyavān vaidharmyavān ca na anayoḥ vastutas kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra prayoga bhedāt tad darśanāt svayam api pratipattau tathā syāt iti sva arthe api anumāne vibhajya ucyate sādharmyeṇa api hi prayoge arthāt vaidharmya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhyena hetoḥ anvaya abhāvāt tathā vaidharmyeṇa api anvaya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvasya sandehāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ tau punar hetū yat kiñcid kṛtakam tat sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti anvayī sāmarthyāt eva atra anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti bhāvaḥ tasmāt na avaśyam pakṣa nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ vyatireki api na anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam bhavati śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti siddha tad svabhāva tayā tad abhāve na bhavataḥ kṛtaka tvasya śabde ca bhāva khyātau tad ātmanaḥ sataḥ bhāvaḥ iti sāmarthyāt tad siddheḥ na anumeya vacanam anvayaḥ tu arthāpattyā siddhaḥ na hi atada ātma niyatasya tad nivṛttyā nivṛttiḥ tasmāt niyamam prasādhya nivṛttiḥ vaktavyā 
[I,076,i]	katham idānīm kṛtakaḥ avaśyam anityaḥ iti pratyetavyaḥ yena evam ucyate yasmāt ahetu tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt anubandhitā na hi bhāvāḥ vinaśyantaḥ tad bhāve hetum apekṣante sva hetoḥ eva naśvarāṇām bhāvāt tasmāt yaḥ kaścid kṛtakaḥ sa prakṛtyā eva naśvaraḥ tathā hi sa apekṣāṇām hi dharmāṇām na avaśyambhāvita īkṣyate nirapekṣaḥ bhāvaḥ vināśe sa apekṣa tve hi ghaṭa ādīnām keṣāñcit nityatā api syāt yadi api bahulam vināśa kāraṇāni santi teṣām api sva pratyaya adhīna sannidhi tvāt na avaśyam sannidhānam iti kaścid na vinaśyet api na hi avaśyam hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ vaikalya pratibandha sambhavāt 
[I,077,i_I,077,ii]	etena vyabhicāri tvam uktam kārya avyavasthiteḥ sarveṣām nāśa hetūnām hetum at nāśa vādinām iti antaraślokaḥ tat ayam bhāvaḥ anapekṣaḥ tad bhāvam prati tad bhāva niyataḥ asambhavat pratibandhā iva kāraṇa sāmagrī sva kārya utpādane nanu anapekṣāṇām api keṣāñcid kvacid na avaśyam tad bhāvaḥ bhūmi bīja udaka sāmagryām api kadācid aṅkurānutpatteḥ na tatra api santāna pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt na evam bhāvasya kadācid apekṣā tatra api antyā sāmagrī yāvi avahitā kārya utpatteḥ sā phalavatī eva sā eva tatra aṅkura hetuḥ pūrvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tad arthaḥ na ca tām kaścid pratibandhum samarthaḥ iti ukta prāyam 
[I,078,i]	nanu yava bīja ādayaḥ api śāli aṅkure janye anapekṣāḥ tad utpatti pratyayānām kadācid tatra api sannidhānāt katham na sa apekṣāḥ yāvatā saḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ tad utpādanaḥ śālibījasya iti tad svabhāva apekṣāḥ evam tarhi kṛtakānām api keṣāñcid satām vā saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ na asti yaḥ vinaśvaraḥ tad svabhāva apekṣa tvāt na naśvarāḥ śāli ādi bījānām api sa svabhāvaḥ sva hetoḥ iti yaḥ na tad hetuḥ saḥ atad svabhāvaḥ syāt niyata śaktiḥ ca sa hetuḥ sva rūpeṇa pratītaḥ eva na ca svabhāva niyamaḥ arthānām ākasmikaḥ yuktaḥ anapekṣasya deśa kāla dravya niyama ayogāt tathā atra api kaścid niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas ime kecid naśvara ātmānaḥ jātāḥ na ca atra kaścid niyāmakaḥ svabhāvasya asti sarva janminām vināśa siddheḥ janmi svabhāvaḥ na aśī iti ced na vai janma nāśi svabhāvasya hetuḥ na ca ahetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ tasmāt na atra kaścid dhetoḥ svabhāva pravibhāgaḥ tad abhāvāt phalasya api na asti iti asamānam 
[I,079,i_I,079,ii]	nanu idam api aniśceyam eva sarva sāmagrī janmānaḥ naśyanti iti tāsām aniḥśeṣa darśanāt vicitra śaktayaḥ hi sāmagryaḥ dṛśyante tatra kācid syāt api yān aśvara ātmānam janayet na artha kriyā śakti lakṣaṇa tvāt vastunaḥ sarva sāmarthya upākhyā viraha lakṣaṇam hi nirupākhyam caramasya tarhi kṣaṇasya anupākhya tā prasaṅgaḥ na sattva saṅkhyā takṣaṇa antara anupāda āna tā lakṣaṇa tvāt caramatvasya bhavati eva hi tasya api jñeya vyāpini jñāne antaśas sāmarthyam virūpe api dhātau dhātu antare tu aneka upakāraḥ eva syāt anābhoge asāmarthyam iti ced na anābhoga asambhavāt eka dharmasya api ajñāne para artha vṛtteḥ kārya akāryānavabodhāt sarvatra śaṅkā utpatteḥ sarvasya kvacid kathañcid upakārāt tad ajñāne tad aṅga vikala tvāt akṣūṇa vidhāna ayogāt na api caramasya asāmarthyam eva kasyacid karaṇāt akāriṇaḥ api pratyaya vaikalye syāt sākalye tu karoti eva 
[I,080,i_I,080,ii]	na evam akṣaṇikasya sarvathā sambhavāt na hi tasya akṣaṇikasya artha kriyā sambhavati krama yaugapadya virodhāt akramaḥ anapekṣasya kartuḥ sva sattā mātreṇa kṣepā yogāt prāk akartuḥ paścāt api svabhāva aparāvṛtteḥ apekṣāyām ca uktam na api yugapad kriyā tad svabhāvasya paścāt api akriyā yogāt tat ayam bhāvaḥ nivṛtta sarva sāmarthyaḥ sattā lakṣaṇam atipatati artha kriyā samartham yat tat atra paramārtha sat asantaḥ akṣaṇikāḥ tasyām krama akrama virodhataḥ iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ 
[I,080,iii]	skandha dhātu āyatana lakṣaṇasya vā kṛtakasya anitya tā sādhanāt adoṣaḥ atad rūpasya apramāṇa tayā siddheḥ anvaya vidhāna ayogāt tat eva ca naḥ kṛtakam yathā uktam abhidharme katame dharmāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ pañca skandhāḥ iti tatra pañca indriyāṇi svabhāva cyutimanti tad kārya vijñāna viccheda vikāra darśanāt tādavasthye ca teṣām tad ayogāt apekṣā virodhāt ca tathā viṣayāḥ sukha duḥkhe nimitta upalakṣaṇam rāga ādayaḥ viṣaya upalambhaḥ ca pratividitā eva upayanti apayanti iti anityāḥ te evamprakṛtayaḥ sva hetu prakṛtim evaṃrūpām sādhayantaḥ tathāvidha janmanām anyeṣām ca svabhāvam enam ālagayanti etena dhātu āyatane vyākhyāte dharmadhātu āyatane api skandha traya svabhāvaḥ eva iti na virodhaḥ etena sattā vyākhyātā 
[I,081,i]	kim tarhi idānīm vināśe anapekṣāyāḥ sāmarthyam yāvatā skandha ādayaḥ anyaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ anityāḥ sādhyante keṣāñcid anitya tva siddhau tathāvidhānām tad vyāptiḥ anapekṣāyāḥ hetu sattve tu vināśasya kasyacid tathā abhāve api anyatra hetoḥ vaikalyāt avināśaḥ api syāt iti avyāptiḥ sā iyam nirapekṣatā vināśasya kvacid kadācid ca bhāva virodhinī tad abhāvam svabhāvena sādhayati yaḥ hi svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ sa yadi kadācid bhavet kvacid vā tad kāla dravya apekṣaḥ iti nirapekṣaḥ eva na syāt 
[I,081,ii]	sa tarhi vinaśvara svabhāvaḥ nirapekṣaḥ iti ahetukaḥ syāt na ahetukaḥ sattā hetoḥ eva bhāvāt tathā utpatteḥ sataḥ hi bhavataḥ tādṛśasya eva bhāvāt na avaśyam sataḥ kutaścid bhāvaḥ iti ced ākasmikī tarhi sattā iti na iyam kasyacid kvacid kadācid viramet tat dhi kiñcid upalīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiñcid pratibaddham apratibaddham vā sā iyam sattā pratibandhinī ced na niyamavatī syāt tasmāt na iyam ākasmikī kvacid katham tarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ jātasya tad bhāve anya anapekṣaṇāt api ca na vināśaḥ nāma anyaḥ eva kaścid bhāvāt kim tu bhāvaḥ eva vināśaḥ saḥ eva kṣaṇa sthāyī jātaḥ iti tam asya mandāḥ svabhāvam ūrdhvam vyavasyanti na prāk darśane api pāṭava abhāvāt iti tad vaśena paścāt vyavasthāpyate vikāra darśanena iva viṣama jñaiḥ tat ayam sattā vyatirekeṇa na anyat kiñcid vināśaḥ apekṣate iti tad vyāpī 
[I,082,i_I,082,ii]	katham punar etat gamyate nirapekṣaḥ vināśaḥ iti asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ abhāva kāriṇaḥ kriyā pratiṣedhāt ca iti caśabdāt katham asāmarthyam siddhe hi bhāve kārakaḥ na tam karoti na api anya kriyāyām tasya kiñcid tādavasthyāt atas tad nāśanaḥ na anya kārī tena ayam tad atad rūpākaraṇāt akiñcitkaraḥ na apekṣyate 
[I,083,i]	katham kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ vināśaḥ iti hi bhāva abhāvam manyante tat ayam vināśa hetuḥ abhāvam karoti iti prāptam tatra yadi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ iti na abhāvaḥ syāt tad abhāvam karoti iti bhāvam na karoti iti kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ asya kṛtaḥ syāt tathā api ayam akiñcitkaraḥ kim iti apekṣate iti siddhā vināśam prati anapekṣatā bhāvasya 
[I,083,ii_I,083,iii]	tasmāt bhavati eṣa svabhāvataḥ yatra nāma bhavati asmāt anyatra api svabhāvataḥ saḥ ayam kvacid bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ anapekṣa tvāt svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati tathā anyatra api svabhāva bhāvī viśeṣa abhāvāt evam anye api svabhāva hetavaḥ yathāsvam pramāṇaiḥ siddha tanmātra anubandhaḥ eva sādhya dharme gamakāḥ veditavyāḥ yaḥ hi bhāva mātra anubandhī svabhāvaḥ tatra eva avinābhāvaḥ bhāvasya bhāva mātra anurodhī svabhāvaḥ iti saḥ eva svayam vastutas bhāvaḥ sa ca ātmānam parityajya katham anyatra bhavet iti 
[I,084,i_I,084,ii]	artha antare tu gamye kāryam hetuḥ avyabhicārāt na hi atadutpatteḥ avyabhicāraḥ anāyatta rūpāṇām sahabhāva niyama abhāvāt yadi artha antaram hetuḥ katham tarhi idānīm sa tasya dharmaḥ tad āśrayāt katham kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ atas eva anyathā āśraya asiddheḥ nanu ca pradeśaḥ āśrayaḥ agniḥ kāraṇam dhūmasya saḥ api hi dhūmasya tad kāraṇānām vā pratiṣṭhānāt dhetuḥ eva 
[I,084,iii]	yadi tad utpatteḥ kāryam gamakam tadā sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt na tad abhāve bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt tasmāt kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinābhāvi kāraṇe teṣām hetuḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt taiḥ eva dharmaiḥ ye taiḥ vinā na bhavanti aṃśena janya janaka tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāt liṅga viśeṣa upādhīnām ca sāmānyānām aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām vyabhicārāt na iṣyate 
[I,085,i_I,085,ii]	katham idam gamyate na dhūmaḥ agnim vyabhicarati iti tad vyabhicāre asya hetumatta avyatikramāt yeṣām upalambhe tad lakṣaṇam anupalabdham yat upalabhyate tatra eka abhāve api na upalabhyate tat tasya kāryam tat ca dhūme api asti sa sakṛt api tathā adarśanāt tad kāryaḥ siddhaḥ akārya tve akāraṇāt sakṛt api abhāvāt 
[I,085,iii]	nanu araṇi nirmathana ādiṣu asati api agnau bhāvāt akāryam na indhana vikāra hetoḥ uṣṇa sparśa viśeṣasya agni tvāt kāryasya ca kāraṇam antareṇa bhāve ahetu tā eva syāt na hi yasya yam antareṇa bhāvaḥ sa tasya hetuḥ bhavati bhavati ca dhūmaḥ agnim antareṇa tat na tad hetuḥ syāt anya hetuka tvāt na ahetukaḥ iti ced na tatra api tulya tvāt tad abhāve api agnau bhavati iti katham ca tatas anyatas vātajjanana svabhāvāt bhavet svayam atad svabhāvasya ajananāt tasya ahetu tā syāt 
[I,086,i]	na vai saḥ eva bhavati tādṛśasya bhāvāt anyādṛśāt bhavan katham tādṛśaḥ tādṛśāt dhi bhavan tādṛśaḥ syāt anyādṛśāt api tādṛśa udbhave tad śakti niyama abhāvāt na hetu bhedaḥ bhedakaḥ iti akāraṇam viśvasya vaiśvarūpyam syāt tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ sarvam ca sarvasmāt jāyet tasmāt kāraṇa bheda abhedābhyām kārya bheda abhedau tat na dhūmaḥ arthāt dṛṣṭa ākāra vijātīyāt bhavati ahetu tva prasaṅgāt 
[I,086,ii^1]	tathā ca nityam sattvam asattvam vāhetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ hi bhāvānām kādācid ka tva sambhavaḥ sa hi dhūmaḥ ahetuḥ bhavat nirapekṣa tvāt na kadācid na bhavet tad bhāve vaikalya abhāvāt iṣṭa kāla vat tadā api vā na bhavet abhāva kāla aviśeṣāt apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācid kāḥ bhavanti bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ tad bhāva yogya tā yogya tā yogāt tulya yogya tā yogyatayoḥ deśa kālayoḥ tadvat tetarayoḥ niyama ayogāt sā ca yogyatā hetu bhāvāt kim anyat tasmāt eka deśa kāla parihāreṇa anya deśa kālayoḥ vartamānaḥ bhāvaḥ tad sāpekṣaḥ nāma bhavati tathā hi tathā vṛttiḥ eva apekṣā 
[I,086,ii^2]	tad kṛta upakāra anapekṣasya tat niyama ayogāt tat niyata deśa kāla tvāt dhūmaḥ yatra dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt vaikalye ca punar na dṛṣṭaḥ tat janyaḥ asya svabhāvaḥ anyathā sakṛt api abhāvāt sa tad pratiniyataḥ anyatra katham bhavet bhavan vā na dhūmaḥ syāt tat janitaḥ hi svabhāva viśeṣaḥ dhūmaḥ iti tathā hetuḥ api tathābhūta kārya janana svabhāvaḥ anyatas api bhāve na sa tasya svabhāvaḥ iti sakṛt api na janayet na vā sa dhūmaḥ adhūma janana svabhāvāt bhāvāt tad svabhāva tve ca saḥ eva agniḥ iti avyabhicāraḥ 
[I,087,i_I,088,i]	agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrdhā yadi agniḥ eva saḥ atha anagni svabhāvaḥ asau dhūmaḥ tatra katham bhavet dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ hi vahniḥ tad śakti bhedavān adhūma hetoḥ dhūmasya bhāve sa syāt ahetukaḥ iti saṅgraha ślokau katham tarhi idānīm bhinnāt sahakāriṇaḥ kārya utpattiḥ yathā cakṣu ūrūpādeḥ vijñānasya na vai kiñcid ekam janakam tad svabhāvam vā kim tu sāmagrī janikā tad svabhāvā sā eva anumīyate sā eva ca sāmagrī svabhāva sthiti āśrayaḥ kāryasya atas eva sahakāriṇām api aparyāyeṇa jananam yat api kiñcid vijātīyāt bhavat dṛṣṭam gomaya ādeḥ śālūka ādiḥ tatra api tathā abhidhāne api asti eva sva bīja prabhavāt svabhāva bhedaḥ hetu svabhāva bhedāt yathā kadalī bījakandodbhavā sphuṭam eva tādṛśam bhedam lokaḥ vivecayati ākāra bhedāt 
[I,088,ii]	anantaram vā kāraṇam kāryam anumāpayati tad tulya rūpāṇām kārya dravyāṇām tulyam yathā pravṛddhayoḥ kadalyoḥ kandodbhavaḥ yatra tu sākṣāt dhetu bhedaḥ tatra rūpa bhedaḥ api yathā tayoḥ eva bīja kanda udbhavayoḥ na api ākāra bhedaḥ eva tad atattve nibandhanam api tu svabhāva antaram api kṛtrima akṛtrimāṇām iva maṇi muktā pravāla ādīnām kvacid puṣpe bhede nīla itara kusumayoḥ iva sūryayoḥ kvacid phale vandhyetarayoḥ iva karkoṭakayoḥ kvacid rase vanyetarayoḥ iva trapuṣayoḥ kvacid prabhāve sparśa upayoga sraṃsinyoḥ iva harītakyoḥ tasmāt na su vivecitam kāryam kāraṇam vyabhicarati hetu viśeṣe api kāryā viśeṣe doṣāt 
[I,089,i]	anvaya vyatirekāt yaḥ yasya dṛṣṭaḥ anuvartakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya tad hetuḥ atas bhinnāt na sambhavaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhau a niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt avaśyambhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti saṅgrahaślokāḥ 
[I,089,ii]	api ca artha antara nimittaḥ hi dharmaḥ syāt anyaḥ eva saḥ na hi tasmin niṣpanne aniṣpannaḥ bhinna hetukaḥ vā tad svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ ayam hi bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ vā bhāvānām yat uta viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca tatas ced na bheda siddhiḥ na kasyacid kutaścid bhedaḥ iti ekam dravyam viśvam syāt tatas saha utpatti vinā asau sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt anyathā ekam iti eva na syāt nāma antaram vā artha bhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt 
[I,090,i^1]	nanu anartha antara hetu tve api bhāva kāle anitya tā niṣpatteḥ tulyā tad svabhāva tā na vai kācid anitya tā nāma anyā yā paścāt niṣpadyeta saḥ eva hi bhāvaḥ kṣaṇa sthiti dharma anitya tā iti ukta prāyam vacana bhede api dharmi dharma tayā nimittam bheda antara ākṣepānākṣepau iti ādi prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa vārttike nirṇītaḥ tam asya svabhāvam manda buddhiḥ paśyan api na vyavasyati satta upalambhena sarvadā tad bhāva śaṅkā vipralabdhaḥ sadṛśa apara utpatti vipralabdhaḥ vā antyakṣaṇa darśinām niścayāt paścāt asya anupalabdhi ā sthiti pratipatteḥ niścaya kālaḥ iti tadā anitya tā vyavasthāpyate iti api uktam anyathārtha antaram eva anitya tā syāt anya nimitta tve animitta tve vā tathā ca bhāvaḥ tadvān na syāt anupayogāt upayoge vā saḥ eva asya sva ātma bhūta anitya tā iti kim anyayā svabhāvena vā acalasya artha antara yoge api tad bhāva anupapatteḥ sa ca artha antarāt bhavan anitya tā anyaḥ vā dharmaḥ hetuḥ phalam vā syāt ahetu phalasya asambandhāt tatra bhāva anumānasya asambhavāt tatra paścāt bhāvān na hetu tvam phale api ekānta tā kutas 
[I,090,i^2]	 sa hi niṣpanne bhāve artha antarataḥ paścāt bhavan katham tasya hetuḥ syāt phalasya api para upaskāra apekṣiṇaḥ na avaśyam hetau bhāvaḥ iti tad bhāva hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam bhāva mātra bhāvi tve siddhānya an apekṣaṇāt ahetu tā tanmātra anubandhaḥ ca tatas api kasyacid bhāve tad anupayogāt apracyutiḥ iti pūrvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tat na avināśa svabhāve bhāve tad anumānam 
[I,091,i_I,092,i]	katham na anumānam yāvatā na anitya tā bhāve kvacid utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā adarśanāt ca vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ tatas avyabhicāraḥ iti na yukta adṛṣṭi mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā sambhāvya vyabhicāra tvāt sthālī taṇḍula pāka vat na hi bahulam pāka darśane api sthālī antargata mātreṇa pākaḥ sidhyati vyabhicāra darśanāt etāvat tu syāt evaṃsvabhāvāḥ etad samāna pāka hetavaḥ pakvāḥ iti anyathā śeṣavat etat anumānam vyabhicāri 
[I,092,ii_I,092,iii]	kim punar etat śeṣavat yasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate sa tasya vyatirekaḥ aniścitaḥ iti vipakṣe vṛttiḥ āśaṅkyate vyatireka sādhanasya adarśana mātrasya tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam na hi sarva anupalabdhiḥ abhāva pratipādikā tasmāt eka nivṛttyā anya nivṛttim icchatā tayoḥ kaścid svabhāva pratibandhaḥ api eṣṭavyaḥ anyathāgamakaḥ hetuḥ syāt 
[I,093,i]	hetoḥ triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayaḥ tena varṇitaḥ asiddha viparīta artha vyabhicāri vipakṣataḥ na hi asati pratibandhe anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ asti tena tam eva darśayan niścayam āha prasiddhaḥ tu dvayoḥ api sādhanam iti tatra anvaya niścayena viruddha tad pakṣyāṇām nirāsaḥ vyatireka niścayena anaikāntikasya dvayoḥ iti eka prasiddha pratiṣedhaḥ prasiddhaḥ iti sandigdhayoḥ śeṣa vat asādhāraṇayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ 
[I,093,ii]	asati api pratibandhe adarśana mātreṇa vyatireke yat āha eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat ubhayam vaktavyam viruddha anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa iti yat vaidharmya vacanam anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa yadi tena vipakṣe adarśanam khyāpyate tat anukte api gamyate na hi tasya prāk darśana bhrāntiḥ yā vacanena nivartyeta smṛtiḥ vācā darśane kriyate iti ced darśanam khalu apratīyamānam anaṅgam iti yuktam tatra smaraṇa ādhānam vacanam adarśanam tu darśana abhāvaḥ sa darśanena bādhyate tad abhāve tu siddhaḥ eva iti apārthakam tad siddhaye vacanam 
[I,094,i]	na anupalabhamānasya tāvatā na asti iti bhavati tad artham vacanam yadi anupalabhamānaḥ api na asti iti na pratīyāt vacanāt api na eva pratyeṣyati tat api hi anupalambham eva khyāpayati na ca eka anupalambhaḥ anya abhāvam sādhayati atiprasaṅgāt na sa tena sādhyate api tu anupalambhena svayam yuktaḥ dṛśyasya adarśane abhāvaḥ sa tad abhāve na yuktaḥ kvacid yadṛcchayā tathā abhāve api tayoḥ apratibandhāt vyāpti asiddheḥ na api tena na asti iti vacanāt tathā bhavati atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt vyāvṛttim icchatā tatra nyāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ yatas asya vyāvṛttam iti bhavati 
[I,094,ii_I,095,i]	na ca na asti iti vacanāt tat na asti eva yathā yadi na asti sa khyāpyate nyāyaḥ tadā na asti iti gamyate iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ nanu tad abhāve anupalambhāt siddhā vyāvṛttiḥ uktam atra kiñcid api ca yadi adṛṣṭyā nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat vyabhicāri kim yathā pakvāni etāni phalāni evaṃrasāni vā rūpa aviśeṣāt eka śākhā prabhava tvāt vā upayukta phala vat atra api upayukta vyatirikta pakṣīkaraṇe hetoḥ sādhya abhāve anupalambhaḥ asti iti katham vyabhicāraḥ 
[I,095,ii]	pratyakṣa bādhā śaṅkā avyabhicāraḥ iti eke na pakṣīkṛta viṣaye abhāvāt kadācid bhavet iti ced tathā śaṅkāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ anyatra api abhāva niyama abhāvāt vṛttam pramāṇam bādhakam avṛtta bādhane sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ vyatirekaḥ tu siddhaḥ eva sādhanam iti tathā abhāve niścayam apekṣate anupalambhāt tu kvacid abhāva siddhau api apratibaddhasya tad abhāve sarvatra abhāva asiddheḥ saṃśayāt avyatirekaḥ vyabhicāraḥ śeṣavataḥ
