[I,095,iii]	kim ca vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt iti nirātmakānām ghaṭa ādīnām dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭānām prāṇa ādi abhavena vyāpteḥ tad nivṛttau vyāpya nivṛtteḥ ātma gatiḥ syāt adṛśya anupalambhāt abhāva asiddhau ghaṭa ādīnām nairātmya asiddheḥ prāṇa ādeḥ anivṛttiḥ abhyupagamāt siddham iti ced katham idānīm ātma siddhiḥ parasya api apramāṇikā nairātmya siddhiḥ abhyupagamena ca sa ātmakān ātmakau vibhajya tatra abhāvena gamaka tvam kathayatā āgamika tvam ātmani pratipannam syāt na anumeya tvam 
[I,096,i]	yā api asiddhi yojanā tathā sa pakṣe san asan iti evamādiṣu api yathāyogam udāhāryam iti sā api na vācyā anupalambhaḥ eva saṃśayāt upalambhe tad abhāvāt anupalambhāt ca vyatirekaḥ iti saṃśayitaḥ anivāryaḥ syāt yathāyoga vacanāt anivāritaḥ eva iti ced na yaḥ eva tu ubhaya niścita vācī ityādi vacanāt tena anupalambhe api saṃśayāt anivṛttim manyamānaḥ tat pratiṣedham āha 
[I,096,ii]	śrāvaṇa tvasya api nitya anityayoḥ adarśanāt tad vyāvṛttiḥ iti tad vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt na hi tad vyāvṛtteḥ anyat tad vyavacchedanam avyavacchedaḥ tu kutaścid vyāvṛtteḥ eva aniścayāt yaḥ hi yatra na asti iti niścitaḥ sa bhavan katham tad abhāvam na gamayet pramāṇa antara bādhanāt na ubhaya vyavacchedaḥ anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka vyavacchedena anya vidhānāt apratiṣedhaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ virodhāt na tarhi idānīm adarśanam pramāṇam bādhā sambhavāt tathā anyatra api pramāṇa antara bādhā sambhāvyate lakṣaṇa yukte bādhā sambhave tad lakṣaṇam eva dūṣitam syāt iti sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ anumāna viṣaye api pratyakṣa anumāna virodha darśanāt anāśvāsa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na yathā ukte abhāvāt viruddha avyabhicārī avacanam iti ced anumāna viṣaye avacanāt iṣṭam viṣayam ca asya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ 
[I,097,i]	yat api āha yadi adarśana mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca saḥ api yuktaḥ iti katham ayuktaḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddheḥ nanu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ sparśasya yuktaḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ dṛśya tad svabhāva viṣaya mātrā pratiṣedhāt pṛthivī ādi sāmānyena gṛhītvā ayam pratiṣedham āha tatra ca tūla upala pallava ādiṣu tad bhāve api sparśa bheda darśanāt kvacid viśeṣasya api sambhavāt śaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti sarvatra adarśana mātreṇa ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ 
[I,098,i]	api ca yadi kathañcid vipakṣe adarśana mātreṇa apratibaddhasya api tat avyabhicāraḥ kvacid deśe kānicid dravyāṇi kathañcid dṛṣṭāni punar anyatra anyathā dṛśyante yathā kāścid oṣadhayaḥ kṣetra viśeṣe viśiṣṭa rasa vīrya vipākāḥ bhavanti na anyatra tathā kāla saṃskāra bhedāt na ca tad deśaiḥ tathā dṛṣṭāḥ iti sarvāḥ tattvena tathā bhavanti sambhavat viśeṣa hetūnām guṇa antara sambhavāt viśeṣa hetu abhāve tu syāt anumānam yathā adṛṣṭa kartṛkam api vākyam puruṣa saṃskāra pūrvakam iti vākyeṣu viśeṣa abhāvāt sarva prakārāṇām puruṣaiḥ karaṇa darśanāt na evam asambhavat viśeṣa hetavaḥ puruṣāḥ yena vacana ādeḥ kiñcid mātra sādharmyāt sarva ākāra sāmyam anumīyeta sarva guṇeṣu viśeṣa darśanāt saṃskāra bhedena viśeṣa pratipatteḥ tadvat anyasya api sambhavāt asambhava anumāne ca bādhaka hetu asambhavāt vairāgya adṛṣṭeḥ adṛṣṭena ca bādhya bādhaka bhāva asiddheḥ rāga ādi avyabhicāri kāryā sambhavāt sambhave api viśeṣāṇām draṣṭum aśakya tvāt teṣām ca apratikṣepa arha tvāt 
[I,098,ii]	na evam vākyāni dṛśya viśeṣa tvāt adṛśya tve api adṛṣṭa viśeṣāṇām vijātīyatva upagama virodhāt tad viśeṣāṇām anyatra api śakya kriya tvāt pratyakṣāṇām śabdānām apratyakṣa svabhāva abhāvāt bhrānti nimitta abhāvāt bādhaka abhāvāt bhrāntyasiddheḥ puruṣeṣu viśeṣa darśanasya bādhaka tvāt asamānam para bhūtasya ca vākya viśeṣasya ātad viśeṣa tvāt tat abhinna svabhāvānām sarveṣām puruṣa kriyā na vā kasyacid 
[I,099,i_I,099,ii]	tasmāt tanmātra sambaddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet yathā vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapām śākhā ādimat viśeṣasya eva kasyacid tathā aprasiddheḥ sa tasyāḥ svabhāvaḥ svabhāvam ca parityajya katham bhāvaḥ bhavet svabhāvasya eva bhāva tvāt iti tasya svabhāva pratibandhāt avyabhicāraḥ kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ nivartayet kāraṇam api nivartamānam kāryam nivartayati anyathā tat tasya kāryam eva na syāt atas kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api svabhāvam niyamayati iti ubhayathā svabhāva pratibandhāt eva nivṛttiḥ 
[I,100,i]	anyathā eka nivṛttyā anya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet na aśvavān iti martyena na bhāvyam gomatā api kim sannidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya sannidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim iti antaraślokau tasmāt svabhāva pratibandhāt eva hetuḥ sādhyam gamayati sa ca tad bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ vā saḥ eva avinābhāvaḥ dṛṣṭāntābhyām pradarśyate 
[I,100,ii]	atas eva vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ na iṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭānte hi sādhya dharmasya tad bhāvaḥ tanmātra anubandhena khyāpyate yaḥ kṛtaka svabhāvam janayati saḥ anityam svabhāvam santam janayati iti pramāṇam dṛṣṭāntena upadarśyate tena ca pramāṇena sādhya dharmasya tanmātra anubandhaḥ gamyate hetu bhāvaḥ vā tasmin sati eva bhāvāt iti artha antarasya tathā prasiddhe tad bhāve hetu bhāve vā anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvam na bhavati dahana abhāve ca dhūmaḥ tathā hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ vā katham svabhāvam hetum vā antareṇa bhavet iti āśrayam antareṇa api vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte prasidhyati vyatirekaḥ hetu svabhāva abhāvaḥ atas pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid hetuḥ tau eva hi nivartamānau sva pratibaddham nivartayate iti kasyacid arthasya pratiṣedham api sādhayitu kāmena hetoḥ vyāpakasya vā svabhāvasya nivṛttiḥ hetu tvena ākhyeyā anyathā pratibaddha nivṛttyānya nivṛtti asiddheḥ 
[I,101,i]	 yukta upalambhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam pratiṣedha hetuḥ pratiṣedha viṣaya vyavahāra hetuḥ tad hetuḥ iti uktaḥ svayam tathābhūta anupalambhasya pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt hetu vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ ubhayasya api hetuḥ iti eṣa trividhaḥ eva pratiṣedha hetuḥ upalabhya sattvasya hetoḥ tathā abhāva niścaye vyāpakasya sva ātmanaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ iti sa tad tad viruddha ādya gati gati prayoga bhedena aneka prakāraḥ uktaḥ 
[II,001,i_II,001,ii]	para artham anumānam tu sva dṛṣṭa artha prakāśanam yathā eva hi svayam trirūpāt liṅgāt liṅgini jñānam utpannam tathā paratra liṅgi jñāna utpipādayiṣayā trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam para artham anumānam kāraṇe kārya upacārāt atra sva dṛṣṭa artha grahaṇam āgamāt para dṛṣṭam na sādhanam na api anarthataḥ siddhiḥ iti jñāpana artham 
[II,001,iii_II,002,i]	yathā āhuḥ eke parasya pratipādya tvāt svayam adṛṣṭam api paraiḥ dṛṣṭam sādhanam yathā acetanāḥ sukha ādayaḥ buddhiḥ vā utpatteḥ anitya tvāt vā rūpa ādi vat iti tat ayuktam anumāna viṣaye vācaḥ prāmāṇya abhāvāt prāmāṇye vā na anumāna pravṛttiḥ syāt vacana mātreṇa artha siddheḥ hetu ādi vaiyarthyāt vacana viśeṣasya prāmāṇyāt adoṣaḥ iti ced uktam atra āgama prāmāṇya cintāyām na api asya kaścid viśeṣaḥ pramāṇa asaṃvāde saṃvāde vā na tad siddham parasya eva siddham tat nābhyupagamāt parīkṣā vṛttiḥ api tu parīkṣāyāḥ abhyupagamaḥ iti na para upagatena sādhanam 
[II,002,ii_II,003,i]	tad āgama bādhanāya param prati sādhana ukteḥ tadā asya aprāmāṇyāt tad siddham asiddham iti katham tatas siddhiḥ tat āgamavataḥ tat siddham iti ced kasya kaḥ āgamaḥ bādhyamānaḥ ca pramāṇena sa katham āgamaḥ riktasya jantoḥ jātasya guṇa doṣam apaśyataḥ vilabdhāḥ vata kena ime siddhānta viṣamagrahāḥ iti antaraślokaḥ 
[II,003,ii]	tad āgama viruddha abhyupagamaḥ ca tena eva katham bhavet tad upagamaḥ āgamasya tyāga aṅgasya apramāṇa tvena apratipatti yogya tvāt tad upagamāt āgamaḥ tatas sādhana dharmaḥ tasmāt vastu sthitiḥ iti ca su vyavasthitāni vastūni puruṣa icchayā ca hetu tad ābhāsayoḥ tattva vyavasthāne kaḥ idānīm hetuḥ ahetuḥ vā vastutas tasyāḥ vastu vṛtti niyama abhāvāt sankhalu api arthaḥ prati iti apekṣaḥ sādhanam na āsan pratīti mātreṇa yatas para upagatena siddhiḥ syāt sataḥ api avastu kṛtā pratipattiḥ asat pratipattim na atiśete apratyaya tvāt 
[II,004,i_II,004,iii]	uktam ca na kārya svabhāva anupalambha viśeṣebhyaḥ aparam pratipatti aṅgam asti iti tat vastutas siddha lakṣaṇam asiddham kim ātmanaḥ pareṇa api anyatas pratipattum ayuktam eva yaḥ tu para parikalpitaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ yathā deśa kāla avasthā viśeṣa niyata eka dravya saṃsarga avyavacchinna svabhāva antara virahāt aneka vṛtteḥ ekasya na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ tathābhūta svabhāvasya virodhāt bhinna deśa ādi yogena saḥ eka dharma upagame apara dharma upagama sandarśana arthaḥ tad anabhyupagame ca ubhaya nivṛttiḥ vivekasya kartum aśakyatvāt tasya anyatra vastutas pratibandhāt katham idānīm asambhavinaḥ arthasya pratipattiḥ iti ced saḥ api tatra asambhavī yaḥ asambhavinā vyāptaḥ iti tad abhyupagame aparaḥ niyata prāptiḥ iti durnivāraḥ 
[II,005,i]	nanu tathā api asiddhiḥ hetoḥ pratijñāyāḥ ca abhyupeta ādi bādhā svayam abhyupagama antara avasthānāt na parīkṣā kāle kasyacid anabhyupagamāt sa yam artham pratipadyate tam pratipadyamānaḥ aparam api sāmarthya āyātam abhyupagacchati prabhā abhyupagame pradīpa abhyupagama vat iti pratipattiḥ eva sā na darśana antara avasthitasya doṣa udbhāvanam sa hi tasya upagama kālaḥ tatra yāvān arthaḥ yukti sāmarthyāt āpatati sa sarvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na vā kaścid iti na api asiddhi ādayaḥ yadi evam idam api syāt na vā ubhayam iti dharmayoḥ sambandha upadarśanāt ekānta parigrahe syāt eṣa doṣaḥ na vā sati hetau yukti prāptasya avaśyam parigraha arha tvāt na ca abhyupagamaḥ yukti bādhane samarthaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ abhyupagata eka dharmaṇaḥ avaśyam apara abhyupagamaḥ yukti kṛtaḥ iti asati tu hetau maulasya hetoḥ vyāpi avyāpaka bhāva sādhana prakāraḥ eṣaḥ na viparyaya sādhanam hetoḥ apramāṇa tvāt 
[II,006,i_II,006,ii]	iha api yadi viparyayeṇa evam anitya tā utpatti niṣedhaḥ kriyate na kaścid evam karoti na ca śakyam evam kartum caitanyena anayoḥ virodha asiddheḥ prasaṅga viparyaya sādhanayoḥ agamaka tvāt ekasya bhāve avikala kāraṇasya prāk bhavataḥ abhāvāt virodhaḥ paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā vā na ca ayam utpatti vināśābhyām caitanyasya prasidhyati ekasya tu yathā ukta svabhāva antara viraha upagamāt eva bhinna deśa ādibhiḥ yoga abhāvaḥ tad abhāvasya tad bhāvasya ca anyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvena virodhāt ayam eva ca ācāryaiḥ avayavi pratiṣedha ādiṣu bahu mukhaiḥ upanyāsaiḥ ekatva aneka vṛttyoḥ virodhāt tathāvidha svabhāva niṣedhaḥ kriyate viruddhayoḥ eka upagamasya aparatyāgana āntarīyaka tva anna ubhaya dharma asti iti siddhānta upagama nibandhaneṣu vicāra prastāveṣu anyathā abhyupagamya vicāra ayogāt 
[II,007,i]	anarthaḥ khalu api kalpanā samāropitaḥ na liṅgam yathā pakṣa sa pakṣa anyatara tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ vā iti na hi atra śabda ghaṭayoḥ śabda ākāśayoḥ vā vāstavī pratyāsattiḥ api tu vaktuḥ vivakṣā kṛtā tad abhāve vivakṣita itarayoḥ āsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt vastu svabhāva tve ca punar vivakṣā antare parāvṛttyayogāt yugapad ekatra viruddha guṇa upasaṃhārā yogāt ca tasmāt ete kartuḥ icchā mātra anurodhinaḥ dharmāḥ na vastu svabhāvam anuvidadhati tasya evam avṛtteḥ tasmāt na tatas artha siddhiḥ vastu rūpayoḥ pratyāsatti viprakarṣayoḥ asiddheḥ siddhau tu syāt yathā tādṛśam rūpa sādharmyam kvacid abhisamīkṣya āhuḥ eṣa piṇḍaḥ viṣāṇī go ga vayayoḥ anyatara tvāt iti 
[II,007,ii_II,008,ii]	atha punar mayā evaṃvivakṣita tvāt iti āha tadā sidhyati artha śūnyam vivakṣā mātram tatas na artha siddhiḥ tad icchāyāḥ vastuni vṛtti niyama abhāvāt tathā hi aśakya darśanam etat yatra tad icchā tatra vastu bhāvaḥ iti vyāpti asiddheḥ vyabhicāraḥ etena mad upagama ādayaḥ hetu prayogāḥ vyākhyātāḥ āgama siddhāḥ ca vacanasya vaktuḥ icchā mātreṇa pravṛtteḥ kalpanā āgamayoḥ kartuḥ icchā mātra anurodhataḥ vastunaḥ ca anyathā bhāvāt tad kṛtāḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam para artham anumānam iti arthān na pakṣa vacanam sādhanam iti uktam veditavyam katham na sādhanam sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā tatas siddheḥ anutpatteḥ 
[II,008,iii]	sākṣāt tāvat arthāt artha gateḥ śaktiḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ na arthe tena tayoḥ na asti svatas sādhana saṃsthitiḥ arthaḥ eva hi artham gamayati na antarīyaka tvāt na abhidhānam sambandha niyama abhāvāt tatas na pakṣasya hetoḥ vā vacanam sādhanam svatas artha siddheḥ saṃśayaḥ tu pakṣa vacanāt arthe dṛṣṭaḥ na niścayaḥ iti sākṣāt na sādhanam 
[II,009,i_II,009,ii]	sādhya abhidhānāt pakṣa uktiḥ pāramparyeṇa na api alam śaktasya sūcakam hetu vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam na api pāramparyeṇa sādhyasya eva abhidhānāt hetu vacanam tu svayam aśaktam api śaktasya vācakam iti sādhanam iṣṭam upacāreṇa tatas hetu vacana pravṛtteḥ tat api śaktam eva iti ced saṃśayena jijñāsoḥ prakaraṇa pravṛtteḥ teṣu api prasaṅgaḥ vipakṣa vacana mātrāt api saṃśaye pratipakṣa hetu vacana pravṛtteḥ sambhavāt tat api tena saha sādhanam syāt tasmāt triṣu eva rūpeṣu antaraṅgam artha siddhau sāmarthyam avasthitam tatra ca smṛti samādhānam tad vacasi iti tat eva sādhanam 
[II,010,i]	akhyāpite viṣaye hetu pravṛtteḥ asambhavāt viṣaya khyāpanāt eva sāmarthyam iti ced uktam atra api ca vinā api anena yāvān kaścitkṛtakaḥ sa sarvaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti ukte api śabdaḥ anityaḥ iti arthāt gamyate eva tat na avaśyam asya nirdeśaḥ tena anuktau api pakṣasya siddheḥ apratibandhāt triṣu anyatama rūpasya eva anuktiḥ nyūna tā sādhana doṣaḥ iti uktam veditavyam 
[II,011,i_II,011,iii]	na tarhi idānīm sādhanasya ātad nirdeśana antarīyaka tvāt pakṣasya lakṣaṇam vācyam vācyam sādhya asādhya viparyayeṇa vipratipatti darśanāt tad nirāsa artham sa ca anumeyaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ svayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ atra caturbhiḥ svarūpa nipāta iṣṭa svayampadaiḥ asiddha asādhana artha ukta vādi abhyupagama grahaḥ veditavyaḥ tena siddham yathā śrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti asiddham api sādhana tvena iṣṭam yathā asiddhau hetu dṛṣṭāntau aprakaraṇa āśrayaḥ anāntarīyaka abhyupagamaḥ ca śāstra upagame api vādinaḥ nirastaḥ 
[II,012,i]	katham idānīm aśrūyamāṇaḥ sādhya tvena iṣṭaḥ iti gamyate prakaraṇāt yathā saṃhatānām pārārthyam sādhyaḥ ātma artha tvam tad anuktam api icchayā vyāptam sādhyam iti darśana artham iṣṭa grahaṇam ayam eva dharma dharmiṇoḥ viśeṣaḥ uktaḥ vyapekṣātaḥ asaṃhata viṣayam pārārthyam eṣām iti vacane dharma viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt tasya viśeṣaḥ para arthāḥ santaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ asaṃhata arthāḥ iti dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti vyavasthā mātram bhidyate na arthaḥ 
[II,012,ii_II,013,i]	artha antare ca prakṛtāt viśeṣe sādhye kaḥ tayoḥ sambandhaḥ yena evam uktaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ anvākarṣati atiprasaṅgāt tathā ca sarvaḥ hetuḥ viruddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca sādhya vikalaḥ syāt tāvataḥ dharma kalāpasya kvacid ananvayāt tatas na kutaścid gatiḥ syāt ukta dharmān anvayaḥ eṣa doṣaḥ na anyatra iti ced na sādhya tva aviśeṣāt adoṣe ca iṣṭa vighātaḥ api na syāt tasya sādhya vipakṣaḥ eva vṛttyā tad viparyāsana lakṣaṇa tvāt yathā ukte tu dharma dharmi viśeṣaḥ iṣṭaḥ eva ananvaya doṣaḥ yat āha ātmā paraḥ ced saḥ asiddhaḥ iti tasya eva ceṣṭasya vighāta kṛt viruddhaḥ 
[II,013,ii]	tat api na sādhyam anukta tvāt iti ced yad vivādena sādhanam upanyastam tat ced na sādhyam kim idānīm sādhyam tathā ca viparyaya siddhiḥ vaiphalyam eva vā yathā prāk sañjñina abhisambandhāt arthavat śabda rūpam vibhakti darśanāt sādhyam na ca sva rūpa mātra artha vat arthavat ca tatas bāhyena arthena arthavat tvam aniṣṭam syāt tathā para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṅghāta tvāt siddhāḥ api pāra arthya aviśeṣe na ātma arthāḥ saṃhata para artha kriyā upagamāt eṣām sādhana vaiphalyam 
[II,014,i_II,014,ii]	tasmāt anuktaḥ api icchayā vyāptaḥ sādhyaḥ tad vaikalya ādayaḥ ca dṛṣṭānta ādi doṣāḥ etena sa dvitīya prayogeṣu niranvaya doṣaḥ vyākhyātaḥ yathā abhivyakta caitanya śarīra lakṣaṇa puruṣa ghaṭā anyatarasa dvitīyaḥ ghaṭaḥ anutpala tvāt kuḍya vat iti tathābhūtena puruṣeṇa sa dvitīya tva asiddheḥ kuḍyasya 
[II,014,iii]	atha sāmānyena sādhyam iṣṭam iti na viśeṣa ākṣepaḥ uktam atra tad anākṣepe kim sādhana phalam aniṣṭam ca iti yadi ca na viṣayīkṛtam eva tad sādhanena katham atas tad siddhiḥ sidhyan vā katham aviṣayaḥ viṣayaḥ ced sva āśrayām doṣa gatim katham na spṛśet sa ca nāma tad āśrayām siddhim sādhanāt upajīvati na paraḥ dūṣaṇam iti vyaktam iyam rāja kula sthitiḥ tasmāt yāvatīm artha gatim sādhanam sāmarthyena vyāpnoti siddheḥ ākṣepāt tāvatīm tad dūṣaṇam api 
[II,015,i]	tathāvidhasya ca dehasya ghaṭāt artha antara bhāva anabhyupagame sāmānyena api sādhanam na sambhavati anyatara artha antara bhāva abhāvāt dvayoḥ hi tathā abhāva sambhave anyataroktiḥ samarthā bhavati yathā devadatta yajñadattayoḥ anyataram bhojaya iti na ekasya bhojana asambhave anākāṅkṣāyām vā itas api na anyatara artha antara bhāvaḥ ghaṭasya svatas artha antara bhāvasya anabhyupagamāt virodhāt ca dehaḥ eva artha antara bhūta iti sāmarthyena vākya artha vyavasthāpa nādapārthakam anyatara grahaṇam anyathā vipratiṣiddham etat vacanam syāt ghaṭasya ātmanā tad bhāva artha antara bhāva virodhāt yadi dehāt eva artha antara bhāvaḥ syāt saḥ eva tathā ucyeta anyatara vacana sāmarthyāt haṭasya api saḥ iti virodhaḥ 
[II,016,i]	itas ca na sāmānya āśrayaḥ sarva vyakti sambhava abhāve tad sāmānya ayogāt yathā abrāhmaṇa ādi tve varṇa tvasya aindriyaka tvasya iva vā nitīraṇa ajñāne tathā hi na tat cākṣuṣam tat jñāna vat tad artha apratipatteḥ tad vikārān anukārāt tad abhāve bhāvāt ca tathā śrāvaṇa ādi api iti na aindriyam tathā ghaṭa śarīrayoḥ anyataradartha antara bhūtam iti sāmānyena anyatara artha antara bhāvaḥ tayoḥ ekasya tathā abhyupagame syāt sa ca na śarīrasya ananvaya śaṅkayā na ghaṭasya virodhāt iti sāmānyena api na sambhavati asti nāma īdṛśasya sambhavaḥ deva datta yajñadattayoḥ anyataraḥ bhojanīyaḥ na devadattaḥ na yajñadattaḥ iti na devadattaḥ eva iti abhiprāyāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na anyatara grahaṇena aprasaṅgāt tasmāt idam anyatara grahaṇam eka parigrahe api avirodhe samartham bhavati yathā anyatara bhojana codanāyām eka bhojane vikalpa viṣaya tvāt asya tatra hi ghaṭena eva sa dvitīyaḥ dehena eva vā iti na iṣyate vidhera yogāt ca dvayoḥ ekasya vidhīyamānasya vikalpa samuccaya ayoge kim idānīm vidheḥ sāmarthyam iti riktā vācā uyuktiḥ 
[II,017,i_II,017,ii]	etena pakṣasapakṣa anyatara tvam api pratyuktam api ca dvayoḥ api sambhava avirodhaḥ etat evam syāt anyathā tu asiddham eva tat śabde tathā hi pakṣaḥ eva sa tathāvidhaḥ śabdaḥ na pakṣa sa pakṣayoḥ anyataraḥ vikalpa eka pratiniyamayoḥ virodhāt sāmānyena vihiteṣu api artheṣu sāmarthyāt viśeṣa sthiteḥ ca dehaḥ eva pratyayaḥ na ghaṭe yathā kaḥ api āyātaḥ iti na parvate vṛkṣe vā śaṅkā bhavati na hi viśeṣa śabda sannidhiḥ eva sāmānya śabdānām viśeṣa avasthiti hetuḥ api tu prakaraṇa sāmarthya ādikam api iti 
[II,017,iii]	tasmāt na anyatarat sāmānyena artha antara bhūtam artha antara bhūta dvaya ayogāt na vā kaścid artha antara bhūtaḥ dvayoḥ ekasya api anabhyupagamāt śabda ghaṭa bhedena kalpane anitya tāyām api tulyam iti ced na siddhayā anitya tayā tadvatas śabdasya sādhanāt tathā kasyacid artha antara bhūtasya upagame syāt anyatara artha antara bhāvaḥ 
[II,018,i]	etena iṣṭa sādhya tva vacanena dharmi dharmābhyām viśiṣṭau dharma dharmiṇau nirākurvan pratyākhyātaḥ yathā na anitya śabdaḥ śabdaḥ na śabda anitya tvavān veti samudāya apavādasya dharmiṇī avirodhāt anityaḥ hi śabdaḥ na anitya śabdaḥ śabdaḥ tad bhāva iṣṭau na anityaḥ śabdaḥ syāt śabde anitya śabda tva prasādhanāt anitya śabdaḥ śabdaḥ syāt sa ca na iṣṭaḥ iti na iṣṭa vighātaḥ kaścid 
[II,018,ii_II,019,i]	tasmāt kevalaḥ eva dharmaḥ dharmiṇi sādhyaḥ viparyāsanīyaḥ vā tathā iṣṭa samudāyasya siddhiḥ vighātaḥ vā kṛtaḥ bhavati sarvatra hi tad samudāya viparyāsāt eva viruddhaḥ sa kadācid dharma mukhena dharmi mukhena tad viśeṣa mukhena vā kriyate iti tena vyapadiśyate svayaṃśrutiḥ punar ekasya dharmiṇaḥ śāstre nānā dharma vyavasthāyām api svayam ātmanā eva iṣṭaḥ sādhyaḥ śāstra upagame api na itaraḥ iti darśana arthā tatra sarvānyeṣṭa nirākaraṇe api āśaṅkā sthāna vāraṇam sva vṛttau svayaṃśruteḥ āha sūtrakāraḥ svayam iti śāstra anapekṣam abhyupagamam darśayati iti 
[II,019,ii]	śāstra upagamāt sarvaḥ tat dṛṣṭaḥ sādhyaḥ iti syāt āśaṅkā sambhavaḥ vipratipattiḥ tu dṛśyate eva bhavati eva śāstra dṛṣṭam sādhyam tad prabādhane ca hetu pratijñayoḥ doṣaḥ iti eke teṣām kṛtaka tvena śabda nāśe sādhye gandhe pṛthivī guṇa tva viparyāsanāt hetuḥ viruddhaḥ syāt aprakaraṇāt na iti ced tad anyatra api samānam na atra dharmiṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt iti ced na dharmi prakrame api vastu pratibandha abhāvāt kevalam śāstra upagama dvāreṇa eṣām anuṣaṅgaḥ sa ca sarvatra tulyaḥ iti nānayoḥ bhedaḥ 
[II,020,i]	atha vādinaḥ api iṣṭim sādhayet sādhya dharma vat sādhya samudāya eka deśa viśeṣa tvāt na sādhya samudāya eka deśa viśeṣaḥ iti eva aprakaraṇa icchā bhavati tad bhāva aparityāgāt arthasya icchā pravṛttyoḥ avirāma prasaṅgāt tasmāt iyam kutaścid prakaraṇāt bhavantī tena eva gamyate tām aprakaraṇām api viparīta anubhava pratiṣiddha vṛttim balāt asti iti sādhayan adhyakṣa viruddham ācarati 
[II,020,ii^1]	kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ icchā bhavet sā gamyate ca taiḥ balāt tava iccheyam iti vyaktam īśvara ceṣṭitam vat annakāliṅgaḥ tām vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate anāntarīyake ca arthe bādhite anyasya kā kṣatiḥ uktam ca na āgama apekṣam anumānam sva gocare siddham tena su siddham tat na tadā śāstram īkṣyate vāda tyāgaḥ tadā syāt ced na tadā anabhyupāyataḥ upāyaḥ hi abhyupāye ayam anaṅgam sa tadā api san tathā viśuddhe viṣaya dvaye śāstra parigraham cikīrṣoḥ sa hi kālaḥ syāt tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam tad virodhena cintāyāḥ tad siddhārtheṣu ayogataḥ tṛtīya sthāna saṅkrāntau nyāyyaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ tatra api sādhya dharmasya sambaddhasya eva bādhanam parihāryam na ca anyeṣām anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ kena iyam sarva cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti sthitiḥ 
[II,020,ii^2]	kṛta idānīm asiddhāntaiḥ grāhyaḥ dhūmena na analaḥ yadi sādhanaḥ ekatra sarvam śāstram nidarśane darśayet sādhanam syāt iti eṣā lokottarā sthitiḥ asambaddhasya dharmasya kim asiddhau na sidhyati hetuḥ tad sādhanāya uktaḥ kim duṣṭaḥ tatra sidhyati dharmān anupanīya eva dṛṣṭānte dharmiṇaḥ akhilān vāgdhūma ādeḥ janaḥ anveti caitanya dahana ādikam svabhāvam kāraṇam vā arthaḥ avyabhicāreṇa sādhayan kasyacid vāda bādhāyām svabhāvāt na nivartate prapadyamānaḥ ca anyaḥ tam na antarīyakam īpsitaiḥ sādhya arthaiḥ hetunā tena katham apratipāditaḥ yadi kiñcid kvacid śāstre na yuktam pratiṣidhyate bruvāṇaḥ yuktam api anyat iti rāja kula sthitiḥ sarvān arthān samīkṛtya vaktum śakyam na sādhanam sarvatra tena utsannā iyam sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,023,i]	tasmāt sādhya bādhakaḥ eva viruddhaḥ abādhya bādhakayoḥ ekatas siddhiḥ aviruddhā api śāstra bādhāyām yadi viruddha iṣyate sa anya viṣaye api tulya iti viruddhaḥ syāt tena tatra eva bādhane bhavati na anyatra iti ced na hetoḥ sarvasya guṇa doṣayoḥ sva sādhye cintya tvāt tasya sva sādhya anuparodhe api śāstra uparodhāt virodhe saḥ anya kṛte api tulyaḥ iti virodhaḥ syāt bhavati eva anya kṛte api pratijñā doṣaḥ iti ced astu viṣaya antare api kim na bhavati bādhanīya dharmaṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ abhidhānāt iha eva bhavati na anyatra iti ced bādhanīya arthasya śāstrasya upagamāt anyatra api astu tasmāt na idam pratijñā doṣa lakṣaṇam nyāyyam atiprasaṅgāt 
[II,023,ii_II,024,i]	api ca śāstra upagamāt sarvaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ ced asiddha hetu abhidhānam api pratijñā syāt nipāta vacanena sādhana tvena iṣṭasya pratikṣepāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na nyāya prāptasya sādhyasya vacanena nivartayitum aśakyatvāt pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ svayaṃśabdaḥ api na artham kañcana puṣṇāti śāstreṣu icchayā pravṛtti arthaḥ iti ced kutas punar iyam śaṅkā yena tad artham yatnaḥ kriyate saḥ anivāritaḥ pramāṇena pravartamānaḥ kena nivartyate nivāritaḥ vā pramāṇena vācā kena pravartyate 
[II,024,ii]	samaya lakṣaṇa āhita bhedasya dharmiṇaḥ parihāreṇa prasiddha dharmi parigraha arthām svayaṃśrutim aparaḥ prāha tatra api vicāra prastāvāt eva āśrayaḥ prasiddhaḥ siddhaḥ iti na kiñcid etat na hi sva icchā kalpita bhedeṣu anartha tantra upayogiṣu padārtheṣu vyavasthām uparacayan kaścid nivāryate na hi tathā uparacitaḥ aprasiddha rūpa sāmānyaḥ viśeṣa āśrayam vicāram āśrayate 
[II,025,i]	atha prasiddha apadeśena dharmiṇaḥ siddhasya asādhyatām āha na sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ iti anena eva gata tvāt siddha sādhana rūpeṇa hi nirdeśa sambhave sādhya tvena eva nirdeśyaḥ iti idam phalavat syāt svayaṃsiddhasya dharmiṇaḥ parigraha avacane dharmiṇam eva sādhyam kuryāt iti ced na anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya tvena eva gata artha tvāt dharmi sattāyām sādhyāyām sva lakṣaṇam sādhyam syāt tat ca pratikṣiptam iti na atra evam avacane api pakṣe kiñcid virudhyate atha dharmiṇam eva sādhyam kuryāt tatas kim syāt aśakyam etat kasmāt hetoḥ viśeṣeṇa anvaya abhāvāt nanu ayam hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ doṣaḥ na pakṣasya uttara avayava apekṣa tvāt anyathā sarve hetu ādi doṣāḥ pakṣa doṣāḥ syuḥ sarvatra pakṣasya eva uparodhāt tasmāt tanmātra anuṣaṅgiṇaḥ eva pakṣa doṣāḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodha vat 
[II,025,ii]	hetu ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ bādhyam muktvā pakṣasya lakṣaṇam ucyate parihāra artham avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ svayaṃnipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iṣṭa śruti ḥ avyāpti bādhanī sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣa lakṣaṇam teṣu apakṣatā nirākṛte bādhanataḥ śeṣe alakṣaṇa vṛttitaḥ dṛṣṭeḥ vipratipattīnām atra ākārṣīt svayaṃśrutim iṣṭa akṣatim asādhya tvam anavasthām ca darśayan iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,026,i_II,027,i]	atra svayam iṣṭa śrutibhyām gata arthe api avadhāraṇe kṛtyā antena abhisambandhāt mā bhūt nirdekṣyamāṇe api prasaṅgaḥ iti tad vyavaccheda artham āha tena anaṅga miṣeḥ niṣṭhā atra īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva tayā asiddha hetu ādiḥ pratiṣidhyate etena svayam vādinā iṣṭasya anumeya tva vacanena aniṣṭa saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya api asādhya tvam tad bādhāyām ca adoṣaḥ pakṣa hetvoruktaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā sādhyam abādhanāt yathā ākāśa guṇa tva eka artha samavāyi anitya tva abhāvam api sādhayati iti 
[II,027,ii]	anena eva ca anumāna kāle śāstra anāśraya vacanena aprakaraṇa āpanna pakṣīkaraṇam api pratyuktam yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ vā iti prakaraṇe vyatirikta indriya grāhya sāmānya eka artha sama vāyi anitya tva yuktaḥ śabdaḥ iti sati hi śāstra āśraye tad artha pakṣīkaraṇam yuktam syāt tad avabodha arthi tve vā prativādinaḥ anyathā asambaddha pralāpaḥ eva ayam iti anavadheyaḥ syāt dvayoḥ anāśrita śāstrayoḥ kasyacid parīkṣāyām kaḥ prastāvaḥ aprastuta pakṣīkaraṇasya 
[II,027,iii]	nanu viśeṣasya sāmānya ākṣepāt tad siddhau siddham eva iṣṭam bhavati na pratipad tṛ vāñchāyāḥ prakaraṇāt atas eva prakaraṇena sādhya dharma iṣṭi gatiḥ iti ucyate na hi avaśyam sāmānya arthī viśeṣa pratiniyama arthī bhavati viśeṣa antare vivāda asambhavāt ca na ca śāstra dvāreṇa vivādaḥ tadā tasya ana antarīyaka tvāt na ca evaṃvidhāḥ dharmāḥ kvacid asamaya sthāyinam pratyanvayinaḥ avyabhicārī vā hetuḥ asti sa dvitīya prayogāḥ ca pratyuktāḥ śāstra āśraye api prastāva atikrame ati prasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ tasmāt prakaraṇa āpannam eva āviśeṣaṇam dharma mātram sādhyam ākarṇanīyam vā anyathā artha antara gamanāt avasādaḥ syāt 
[II,028,i]	sa ca ayam sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pratyakṣa artha anumāna āpta prasiddhanā nirākṛtaḥ nirdeśyaḥ yadi nāma nirdeśyaḥ pratyakṣa arthena anumānena āptābhyām prasiddhena ca anirākṛtaḥ abhyupagamaḥ hetum apekṣate pratyakṣe artha grahaṇam indriya jñānasya kasyacid vitatha artha tvāt tad parihāreṇa pramāṇa viṣaya parigraha artham 
[II,029,i_II,029,ii]	kim punar nirākṛtaḥ na pakṣaḥ sandigdhe hetu vacanāt vyastaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ vyastaḥ pramāṇābhyām nirākṛtaḥ viparyaye pramāṇa vṛtteḥ anāśrayaḥ pratipramāṇasya viruddhayoḥ ekatra samyak jñāna ayogāt viṣaya upadarśana artham ca pakṣaḥ ucyate sa nirākṛte viṣayiṇaḥ asambhavāt apakṣaḥ eva tasmāt sandigdhaḥ hetu vyāpāra viṣayaḥ anumānasya bhedena sā bādhā uktā caturvidhā sā iyam pakṣasya bādhā caturvidhāḥ darśitā vidhā anumānam bhittvā tatra abhyupāyaḥ kārya aṅgam svabhāva aṅgam jagat sthitiḥ āpta vacanam kārya lakṣaṇam liṅgam svabhāva lakṣaṇam prasiddhiḥ 
[II,030,i]	ātma aparaḥ vā yathārtha darśana pravṛtta vāc abhimataḥ āptaḥ tat vacanam na antareṇa artha tathā bhāvam pravartate iti kāryam tasya sa sva kārya saṃsūcitaḥ sva viparyaya upagamam pratibadhnāti tat evam sva vacanam śāstram ca abhisamasya sāmyāt ekam uktam yathā ātmanaḥ aprāmāṇye vacanasya apravṛttiḥ tathā śāstra an āśraye tad prasiddhe vicārasya iti prastāva āśraya tve śāstram bādhakam iti amum artham vaktum sva vacanena asya sahoktiḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye kṛtā atas eva udāharaṇam api atra sadṛśam āha na santi pramāṇāni prameya arthāni iti pramāṇānām abhāve śāstra sva vacanayoḥ ayogāt sva vacana virodhe spaṣṭam udāharaṇam āgame tu diś mātra darśanam etat atra udāharaṇam pretya asukha pradaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
[II,030,ii]	dharmi vyavasthiteḥ tad āśrayāt tad prabādhane adhikaraṇa pratyasta mayāt na viśeṣa cintā pravṛttiḥ iti avaśyam evaṃvidhe viṣaye śāstram pramāṇayitavyam katham idānīm na tīrtha snāna ādiḥ a dharma śodhanaḥ iti nābhyupeta bādhā sarveṣām adṛṣṭa pratipatti śāstrāṇām evam avacanāt na pratiṣedhe doṣaḥ sva upagama āśrayam hi śāstram virundhānaḥ vihanyate na aparam anabhyupagamāt tasya api snānāt śuddhi vādinaḥ śāstrasya sva vacanena api asya arthasya pratibādhanāt lobha ādi mūlaḥ adharmaḥ iti sarva śāstreṣu vyavasthā alubdhāt viṣṭāmūḍhānām pāpa anabhyupagamāt sā vyavasthā snāna ādīnām pāpa śodhana vādam bādhate nidāna apraśamanena nidāninaḥ avicchedāt madhura śītala snigdhaiḥ iva vyādheḥ ślaiṣmikasya iti atas eva śāstra dṛṣṭeṣu artheṣu virodha udbhāvana prāyā cintā yat śāstram vastu bala pravṛttena pramāṇena sva vacanena ca ābādhitam dṛśya adṛśyayoḥ viṣayayoḥ tat grāhyam iti 
[II,032,i]	śāstravataḥ api atad ālambane vastuni viruddha uktau api na bādhā pratibandhaḥ tu syāt dvayoḥ tulya kakṣa tvāt yathā sva vacane tadā ca asya sva vacanena virodhaḥ na śāstreṇa tayoḥ yasya pramāṇam asti tad aparasya bādhakam bhavati anyathā katham pratijñām tulya kakṣyām anumānam vā yathārtham apeta yuktikā pratijñā bādheta pratiṣiddham ca āgamānām prāmāṇyam tasmāt abhyupetya vicāreṣu ayam doṣaḥ 
[II,032,ii_II,032,iii]	atas eva viṣaya bheda pradarśana artham pṛthakkṛtaḥ anumānāt abahis bhūtaḥ api abhyupāyaḥ bādhanābhyupagamāt anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt vyartha tā vā pṛthakkaraṇasya sva vacanasya api pṛthakkaraṇa nimittam vāc mātra vacane pratibandhaḥ apramāṇa tvam śāstre api tulyam iti tatra api pratibandhaḥ astu pratibandhaḥ hi adhikaraṇe sati bhavati yathā siddhe vacane prāmāṇya itarayoḥ anyonyam siddhāyām vā yoṣiti prasava itara dharma tvayoḥ sa dharma gataḥ yatra tu dharmyā iva asiddhaḥ tatra kva kena kim pratibadhyate prastāvasya eva abhāvāt tasmāt dharmiṇam pratiṣṭhāpayan śāstram pratiṣṭhāpayati tatas tat bādhakam iti 
[II,033,i_II,033,ii]	tat tarhi śāstram apramāṇakam katham dharmiṇam pratiṣṭhāpayati prāmāṇyena abhyupagamāt sva upagamaḥ eva tarhi prāmāṇyam ādadhat dharmiṇam pratiṣṭhāpayati dharma antaram ca saḥ eva punar prativahati iti na bhidyate sva vacana virodhāt śāstra virodhaḥ tatas pratibandhaḥ eva na bādhā kaḥ tarhi idānīm anayoḥ bhedaḥ na kaścid katham tarhi pṛthak vacanam vākya bhedāt etat syāt pūrveṇa pratiṣṭhāpitam uttaram pratihanti iti abhyupagama virodhaḥ atas eva pūrva abhyupagamena iti āha tat eva vākyam sva artham virundhānam sva vāc viruddham yathā na anumānam pramāṇam iti 
[II,033,iii]	pratibandhaḥ api katham apramāṇasya atas eva tulya kakṣa tvāt yadi hi tatra ekasya prāmāṇyam syāt siddhiḥ eva na pratibandhaḥ pramāṇena apramāṇasya bādhanāt tena upagamāt pramāṇam sarva vastuṣu śāstram bādhakam eva iti ced katham punar upagama aviśeṣaḥ ekam pramāṇam bādhakam ca na aparam iti yat kiñcid etat puruṣa icchā akṛtā ca asya paripūrṇā pramāṇa tā 
[II,034,i]	yadi sva vacana abhyupagama virodhayoḥ pratibandhaḥ doṣaḥ tathā api atas artha saṃśayaḥ eva saḥ anavadya pakṣa nirdeśe api tulyaḥ iti katham pakṣa doṣaḥ na vai tad vacanāt aniścaya utpatteḥ dṛṣṭa vacanaḥ kim tarhi yat yāvatā vacanena samarthanīyam tasya asamarthanāt sambhavī sva abhiprāyaḥ pratijñā vacanena darśanīyaḥ sa ca yathā pramāṇa bādhāyām na sambhavati tathā ekatra viruddhayoḥ upasaṃhāre api vacana guṇa doṣau hi para arthe anumāne adhikriyete na arthasya vaktuḥ upālambhāt ayathārtha abhidhānena 
[II,034,ii]	yadi sva vacana upagama virodhayoḥ na kaścid bhedaḥ kaḥ tarhi viṣaya bhedaḥ pūrva upagama virodhasya yatra anāśrite kasmiṃścid samaye na pravartate vicāraḥ saḥ avaśyam āśrayaṇīyaḥ na antarīyaka tvāt iti saḥ eva tasya pratibandha viṣayaḥ sarvatra sva vāc viruddha abhidhānam atra api kaḥ ayam avaśyam para āśrayaḥ saḥ eva tam artham para mukhena vyavasthāpya punar vyutthāpayati iti 
[II,035,i]	prasiddhiḥ khalu api virodhinam pratijñā artham bādhate puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ artheṣu aśakya pratiṣedha tva āt iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvasya sa dharmaḥ vyavahāra jaḥ prasiddhi śabdena uktaḥ yogyam hi viśvam svabhāvataḥ kṛta akṛtānām śabdānām icchā mātra vṛtteḥ tayā artha mātra anurodhinyāḥ bhāvinyāḥ bhūtayā vā śabda yogya tayā tām pratirundhānaḥ bādhyate 
[II,035,ii_II,035,iii]	tad yogya tā balāt eva vastutas ghaṭitaḥ asyām sarvaḥ śabdaḥ iti apratīte api tasmin tad siddha tām āha yatra api asādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāve śābda prasiddhena viruddhena arthena apodyate na sa pakṣaḥ iti tatas eva bādhā heta urasādhāraṇa tvam kvacid acandre asiddheḥ aśakya niṣedha tām asya darśayan evam āha apratipramāṇa tayā niścayam vā tat niṣedhaḥ hi anumānāt syāt pratyakṣeṇa yogya tā aniścayāt tatra ca sarva hetūnām asādhāraṇa tā yatra sattvam eva na anvayi iti udāharaṇam evam phalam 
[II,036,i]	saṅketa āśrayāḥ śabdāḥ sa ca icchā mātra āśrayaḥ tat na asiddhiḥ śabda siddhānām iti darśayan śābda prasiddhena iti āha śaṅkita pratibandhānām saṃśayāt asiddheḥ ciram adṛṣṭānām api punar pratibhā utpatti dṛṣṭeḥ sati sambhave tad abhāvasya puruṣa mātreṇa aniścayāt atas pramāṇān niścaya abhidhānāt anumāna viṣaye viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ asambhavam artha āpattyā darśayati 
[II,036,ii^1]	etena pratyakṣa anumāne vyākhyāte dvayoḥ api prāmāṇya aviśeṣāt ekasya tad lakṣaṇa yoge api pratidvandvi darśanāt pratyakṣasya api evambhāvaḥ syāt na ca pramāṇa lakṣaṇa vyatiriktaḥ anyaḥ asti viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣasya yaḥ ekānta sādhana tvam vyavasthāpayati yatas tad viśeṣa bahirbhāvāt apramāṇam anumānam syāt eka saṅkhyā vivakṣayā pradarśita pratidvandvinaḥ prāmāṇyāt adoṣaḥ iti ced asti nāma īdṛśasya viniścaye sambhavaḥ na asya pratidvandvī vidyate iti aviśiṣṭa lakṣaṇe dṛṣṭasya aparatra vyatireka niścayasya kartum aśakyatvāt iti uktam na ca puruṣa pratibhā vaśāt pramāṇayoḥ lakṣaṇam ucyate 
[II,036,ii^2]	kim tarhi vastu sthityā sā ca evam aśakya niścaya iti na tad sandigdha lakṣaṇam vyavahāra yogyam pakṣa dharma tva ādi sandeha vat lakṣaṇe jñāna grahaṇāt ca ukta lakṣaṇe anumāne tad lakṣaṇasya pratiyoginaḥ asambhavāt asambhavaḥ anumāne viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ tad eka saṅkhyā vivakṣā api atra viṣaye na iṣṭā eva viṣayam ca asyāḥ nivedayiṣyāmaḥ tat evam pramāṇe bādhake bruvāṇaḥ tatas niścayam āha tatas sa pratipakṣa sambhāva nām aḥ taṅgamayati tatas anumāna viṣaye viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ abhāvam sūcayati iti 
[II,038,i]	atha vā lokasya bruvataḥ anumāna abhāvam āha tena bhinna viṣayā pratītiḥ anumānāt iti uktam bhavati tena anumānāt vastu sada satta anurodhinaḥ bhinna viṣayāyāḥ pratīteḥ na vastu vaśāt vṛttiḥ iti sūcitam bhavati sa hi śaśinaḥ candra tvam anicchan kāmanyām pratītim icchet iti tam pratyadṛṣṭāntam anumānam tena asādhāraṇam āha 
[II,038,ii]	yasmāt na etat eva ekam udāharaṇam adhikṛtya idam ucyate sarva pratīti virodhānām sāmānyena lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā na vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapa iti uktau api bādhanāt atra api loke karpūra rajata ādiṣu dṛṣṭa tvāt na asādhāraṇa tā syāt na ca samayāt vartamānasya kācid asādhāraṇa tā yadi hi tasya kvacid sidhyet siddham vastu balena tat pratīti siddha abhyupagame śaśini api anivāraṇāt tad vastuni siddham śaśini api anivāryam eva tad vastu abhāve śaśini nivāraṇe api na kaścid doṣaḥ tasmāt avastu niyata saṅketa śabda bhāvinām dharmāṇām yogyāḥ sarva padārthāḥ icchāyāḥ nirodha abhāvāt 
[II,039,i_II,039,ii]	etena saṅketa anuvidhāyinām śabdānām na kaścid artha niyamaḥ atra ca eṣām pratiṣedhe virodhaḥ iti uktam bhavati naimittikyāḥ śruteḥ artham artham vā pāramārthikam śabdānām pratirundhānaḥ na bādhyaḥ tena varṇitaḥ tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśanāya pṛthakkṛtā anumāna abahis bhūtā pratītiḥ api pūrvavat iti antaraślokau 
[II,039,iii_II,040,i]	pratyakṣa virodhe api nānā rūpasya yat eva śrutau rūpam pratibhāsate advayam sambandhi antara abhāvāt śabala ābhāsāyāḥ buddheḥ adṛṣṭeḥ tasya eva pratikṣepe virodhaḥ yathā aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti tad arthā ca artha uktiḥ tat eva rūpam tatra arthaḥ śeṣam vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam avastu rūpam sāmānyam atas tat na akṣa gocaraḥ tena sāmānya dharmāṇām apratyakṣa tva siddhitaḥ pratikṣepe api abādhā iti śrāvaṇa uktyā prakāśitam sarvathā avācya rūpa tvāt siddhyā tasya samāśrayāt bādhanāt tat balena uktaḥ śrāvaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,040,ii_II,040,iii]	anumāna virodhe api yathā nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti abhighāta saha tvam paśyataḥ bhrāntyā etat syāt tat ca dṛṣṭa avarugṇa ghaṭa vat utpatti ādeḥ na sambhavati na kaścid anityaḥ ghaṭaḥ tatra api vyakti tirodhānāt iti ced atādavasthyam anitya tām brūmaḥ tādavasthyam ca tattvam tad avarugṇe asti vināśāt tirodhānāt vā iti na atra nirbandhaḥ tat ca upalabhya madhya rūpam pūrva aparayoḥ koṭyoḥ asti iti bruvāṇaḥ padārtha vyavasthām bādhate sattva rajaḥ tamasām caitanyasya ca evam paraspara rūpa vivekena vyavasthā ayogāt na hi tatra api anupalambham antareṇa anyaḥ kaścid vyavasthā āśrayaḥ tat idam upalabhya lakṣaṇam dadhi ādi kṣīra ādiṣu anupalabhyamānam kṣīram vā tatra na asti iti nyāyyaḥ eṣaḥ 
[II,041,i]	asti eva upalambhaḥ dadhi ādīnām kṣīra ādiṣu anumānam aśaktāt anutpatteḥ na tādṛśām bhāvaḥ anumāna viṣayaḥ sa hi sandṛśyaḥ eva bhavati sa ced bhavet madhya avasthāvat upalabhyeta tad lakṣaṇa tyāgaḥ eva hi tasya vināśaḥ apara bhāvaḥ ca vailakṣaṇyam viruddha svabhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt bhedasya iti ukta prāyam tasmāt utpatteḥ tad kāraṇasya tad janana svabhāvaḥ sidhyet na tad bhāvaḥ 
[II,041,ii_II,042,i]	yadi asataḥ utpattiḥ kim na kṣīrāt śaśa viṣāṇam kaḥ hi viśeṣaḥ abhāva aviśeṣaḥ iti ced na hetoḥ svabhāva bhedāt atadātma tve api kṣīrasya sa tasya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ dadhi jananaḥ na śaśa viṣāṇa jananaḥ sa tasya kutas iti ced sva hetu samutthaḥ iti anādi hetu prakṛti paramparā tasmāt tad janana svabhāvasya hetoḥ abhāvāt śaśa viṣāṇa anutpattiḥ tad bhāvāditarasya iti atha kā iyam śaktiḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ uta anyadeva kiñcid saḥ eva ced tathā eva upalabhyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt viśeṣe ca uktam anyat ced katham anya bhāve saḥ asti upacāra mātram tu syāt etena apara bhāvaḥ pratyuktaḥ iti 
[II,043,i_II,043,ii]	pakṣa dharma prabhedena sukha grahaṇa artham hetu prakaraṇasya sūtra saṅkṣepaḥ ucyate sa pakṣe san asandvedhā pakṣa dharmaḥ punar tridhā pratyekam asapakṣe api sat asat vividha tvataḥ pakṣaḥ dharmī prayojana abhāvāt anupacāraḥ iti ced na sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt tad eka deśa tvāt tad upacāra yogya dharmi pratipatti artham tathā ca cākṣuṣa tva ādi parihāraḥ 
[II,043,iii]	dharma vacanena api dharmya āśraya siddhau dharmi grahaṇa sāmarthyāt pratyāsattyā sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ iti ced na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api pratyāsatteḥ sa pakṣe sattva vacanena dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattva siddheḥ dharmi dharma vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ karaṇīyaḥ ayam vyākhyāne yatnaḥ sa pakṣa vacanena samāhitaḥ sāmarthyāt artha gatau pratipatti gauravam ca parihṛtam bhavati 
[II,044,i_II,044,ii]	pakṣasya dharma tve tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti ced na ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt yathā caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ na anya yoga vyavacchedena yathā pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti ukta prāyam saḥ eṣa pakṣa dharmaḥ tridhā bhidyate sa pakṣe san asandvedhā ca iti sa trividhaḥ pratyekam punar tridhā bhavati asapakṣe san asandvedhā ca iti evam 
[II,044,iii_II,045,i]	sādhya dharma sāmānyena samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tad abhāvaḥ asapakṣaḥ katham idānīm abhāve san iti ucyate na vai tad niṣedha mātram asapakṣaḥ kim tarhi sarvaḥ pratiyogī niṣedhaḥ paryudastaḥ ca atattva lakṣaṇa tvāt asa pakṣasya tad vivakṣite pratiyogini ca tulyam vyatireka gateḥ sarvatra tulya tvāt sākṣāt artha āpattyā vā tasya asya pakṣa dharmasya tattvam sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sat asat tvam ca yathāyogam hetu ādiṣu yathāsvam pratipatti sādhanaiḥ niścitam grāhyam sandigdha viparyasta rūpayoḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa prakāśa nayoḥ apratipatti sādhana tvāt viparīta sandigdha pratipatti śruti vat 
[II,045,ii]	anaikāntikasya tu pakṣa dharma tvam eva asambaddhāt vimarśā yogāt na tu sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sattvam asat tvam vā niścaya apekṣam niścaye api sandeha mukhena eva doṣāt saḥ aniścaye api tulyaḥ iti tathāvidha udbhāvanam api atra dūṣaṇam eva anyatra tu saṃśaye dvayoḥ ekasya vā viparyaye ca ekasya na sādhanam na dūṣaṇam tathā apratipatti aṅgasya asāmarthyāt 
[II,045,iii]	asādhāraṇaḥ api ubhaya vyāvṛtteḥ niścaya ayogāt ubhaya bahis bhūtasya abhāvāt ubhayoḥ ekatra bhāve ca pratīti sādhana abhāvāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ saṃśayāt eva saṃśaya hetuḥ viniścita aparabhāva samāna guṇa puruṣa sambhāvita strī garbhaḥ iva puruṣeṣu yathā āha yaḥ hi asādhāraṇaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ sa yāvatā bhedena sarva saṅgrahaḥ tatra saṃśaya hetuḥ tadvatām tad saṅgrahāt ekānta vyāvṛtteḥ ca iti tadvatām tad saṅgrahāt iti prabheda bāhyasya abhāvam āha yamayam vastu dharmaḥ tṛtīyam āśrayet ekānta vyāvṛttyā ca eka bhāve pratīti sādhana abhāvam āha asya hi dvayasya ekatra samuccayāt sarveṣu prabhedeṣu saṃśayaḥ uktam ca vyāvṛtti niścaye viśeṣasya vyavaccheda hetuta asya kena nivāryate iti 
[II,046,i]	niścaya hetau api apratibhānāt syāt saṃśayaḥ sa ca na ekāntena anaikāntikaḥ tad niścita tad bhāvaḥ nirdiṣṭa guṇa niścayāt eva iti aniścitaḥ na anaikāntikaḥ syāt na vai vastu dharma samāśrayeṇa eva para arthe anumāne sādhana doṣa udbhāvanam api tu vaktṛ doṣeṇa api nyūna tā ananvaya viparīta anvaya vat tena hi nirṇīta guṇe vaktavye anyathā abhidhānāt doṣaḥ eva pakṣa dharme api tarhi sandeha anyatara asiddheḥ dūṣaṇam syāt evam etat iṣṭāprāpteḥ nanu viparyaya prāptiḥ api na eva asti na vai viparyaya prāptyā eva dūṣaṇam kim tarhi sādhana sāmarthya vighātāt tathā hi na prameya tva ādiṣu api viparyaya prāptiḥ asti cākṣuṣa tve vā kaḥ viparyayaḥ ubhaya siddhyā nirdeṣṭavyasya anubhaya siddhiḥ iha api tarhi niścayena nirdeṣṭavyasya aniścayaḥ astu viparyayaḥ 
[II,047,i_II,047,ii]	tasmāt hetu viruddhayoḥ eva niścayāt sādhanam dūṣaṇam vā te ete nava pakṣa dharmāḥ nirdiśyante prameya tvāt nityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ anitya tvāt prayatna anantarīyakaḥ kṛtaka tvāt nityaḥ sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt nityaḥ anitya tvāt aprayatna anantarīyakaḥ anityaḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tvāt nityaḥ asparśa tvāt iti 
[II,048,i]	katham asa pakṣa apekṣayā bhede asataḥ anadhikaraṇa tvāt asattvam sattvam vā iti ced uktam atra yathā asati niṣedhaḥ asapakṣaḥ ca atattva lakṣaṇaḥ iti nanu etasmin asa pakṣe hetu abhāva prasaṅgaḥ sarvasya anya dharma yogāt na bhavati yathā abrāhmaṇaḥ iti na hi saḥ eva brāhmaṇaḥ tad jāti yogāt abrāhmaṇaḥ ca dharma antara samāveśāt loke pratīyate kim tarhi vivakṣita dharmān āśrayaḥ vastu anya viṣaye api nañi vibhāgena niyoga vṛtteḥ sa pakṣa lakṣaṇa virodhāt ca na evam pratītiḥ sādhya dharma sāmānyena samānaḥ iti atra yadi sādhya dharma sāmānyena eva iti syāt tadā na eva kaścid sapakṣaḥ tathāvidhasya asambhavāt tasmāt apratikṣipta dharma antaram sādhya dharma sāmānyam samāviśat ghaṭa ādikam sapakṣayati tena āsapakṣaḥ iti na sarvānyadharma yogini pratītiḥ kim tarhi tad dharma virahiṇī iti adoṣaḥ anya grahaṇe api 
[II,049,i_II,049,ii]	kim punar kāraṇam evam navadhā pakṣa dharmaḥ vibhajyate svabhāva kārya siddhi artham dvau dvau hetu viparyayau vivādāt bheda sāmānye śeṣaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ svabhāva kāryayoḥ eva ātma pratibandhāt gamaka tvam viparyaye vā viparyāsanam iti darśana artham anityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ca iti dvau hetū nityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ca iti viruddhau dvau ca nirdiṣṭau na hi svabhāvāt anyasya sarvatra sa pakṣe sattvam kārya vyabhicārāt kāraṇasya tasmāt sa pakṣe dvidhā vṛtti kāryam na hi anityāḥ iti eva sarve prayatna anantara bhāvi jñāna kārya ārambhiṇaḥ tena tad sa pakṣe dvidhā vartate 
[II,050,i_II,050,ii]	katham idam avagamyate prayatna anantara bhāvi jñānam anitya kāryam iti prayatna anantaram jñānasya prāc sataḥ niyamena ayogāt prayatnasya āvaraṇa indriya śabdeṣu anupayogāt na hi tasya upalambha āvaraṇam sambhavati sataḥ api vā kasyacid tad ātmānam akhaṇḍayataḥ sāmarthya tiraskārā yogāt na hi tatra atiśayam anutpādayat kiñcitkaram nāma akiñcitkaram ca kim kasya āvaraṇam anyat vā 
[II,050,iii]	kuḍya ādayaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām kam atiśayam utpādayanti khaṇḍayanti vā yena āvaraṇam iṣyante na brūmaḥ te kiñcid atiśāyayanti iti api tu na sarve ghaṭa kṣaṇāḥ sarvasya indriya jñānasya hetavaḥ paraspara sahitāḥ tu viṣaya indriya ālokāḥ parasparataḥ viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa antara utpādāt vijñāna hetavaḥ anupakāryasya apekṣā ayogāt śakta svabhāvasya nityam jananam ajananam vā anyathā syāt te ca avyavahitāḥ pratighātinā anyena anyonyasya upakāriṇaḥ avyavadhāna deśa yogya tā sahakāri tvāt teṣām vyavadhāne hetu abhāvāt samartha kṣaṇa antara anutpatteḥ jñāna anutpattiḥ pūrva utpanna samartha nirodhāt vā sati vyavadhāne anyasya utpitsoḥ kāraṇa abhāve anutpatteḥ kāraṇa vaikalyāt jñāna anutpattiḥ iti kuḍya ādayaḥ āvaraṇam ucyante na prāk yogyasya pratibandhāt tasya svabhāva apracyuteḥ 
[II,051,i_II,052,i]	atha vā sambhavati api bhāvānām kṣaṇikānām anyonya upakāraḥ acintya tvāt hetu pratyaya sāmarthyasya asarva vidā tena yat indriya viṣaya madhya sthitam āvaraṇam tau vijñāna utpādana vaiguṇya tāratamyena atiśāyayet api āvaraṇa bhedena śabda ādau śruti māndya pāṭava darśanāt anyathā kvacid api akiñcitkarasya sannidhānasya api asannidhāna tulya tvāt asya idam iti upasaṃhāraḥ api vikalpa nirmite eva syāt na vastu āśrayaḥ na ca samāropa anuvidhāyinyaḥ artha kriyāḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ dahana upacārāt ādhīyate pāke tasmāt satyām api kalpana āyāma tatparāvṛttayaḥ bhāvāḥ yathā svabhāva vṛttayaḥ eva tad sati api āvaraṇe jñāpayeyuḥ eva indriya ādayaḥ na ca tathā tasmāt tena ādheya viśeṣāḥ iti gamyante na tu evam nityānām śabdānām kasmiṃścid sati atiśaya hāniḥ utpattiḥ vā tat yadi teṣām jñāna jananaḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvasya sarvadā sarvāṇi sva viṣayāṇi jñānāni janayeyuḥ na ced na kadācid kasyacid kiñcid iti ekāntaḥ eṣaḥ 
[II,052,ii]	syāt etat na āvaraṇāt nityam sarve śabdāḥ na śrūyante api tu kiñcid eṣām pratipattau sahakāri pratiniyatam asti indriya upakārī anyat vā tat kadācid kasyacid bhavati iti tat kṛtam eṣām kadācid kvacid śravaṇam iti na vai vayam kāraṇānām saha kārīṇi pratikṣipāmaḥ kim tu apekṣante eva kāraṇāni tad avasthā upakāriṇam artham tatas labhyasya atiśayasya kārya upayogāt tathā śabdaḥ api yadi kiñcid apekṣya kāryam kuryāt karotu pūrva svabhāva niyate iti etat na syāt tasya pracyuteḥ apekṣyāt ca prayatnāt prayatna saṃskṛtāt indriyāt anyatas vā svabhāva antara pratilambhāt na hi anupakāri apekṣyate iti ukta prāyam tad upakārasya ca artha antara tve tasya iti sambandha abhāva ādayaḥ api uktāḥ tasya ca ajñeya tvam upakārāt eva jñāna utpatteḥ tasmāt eṣa śabdaḥ na indriyam na sannikarṣam na ātmānam anyat vā kiñcid jñāna utpatti samāśrayam sva vijñāna janane apekṣeta sarvasya tatra akiñcitkara tvāt etena prayatnasya indriya śabda upayogāt sāphalyam pratyuktam indriya upakāreṇa api sahakāri kāraṇam śabdasya upasaṃharet tat ca anapekṣa tvāt asya nirastam 
[II,054,i_II,054,iv]	tat ayam upalabhya svabhāvaḥ svasmāt svabhāvāt kadācid na apaiti iti nityam upalabhyeta evam hi sa nityaḥ syāt yadi na kutaścid sāmarthyam labhyeta pracyaveta vā tatas jñāna janana sāmarthyasya anantara tvāt artha antara tve ca doṣāt na ca asya prayatna anārambha virāme kadācid upalambhaḥ tena tadā ātmānam pratyasya kaścid upakāraḥ sambhāvyate kāraṇa dharma darśanāt atas prayatna anantara bhāvi jñānam anitya svabhāva kāraṇa kāryam iti siddham prayatna anantaram jñānam prāc sataḥ niyamena na tasya āvṛtyakṣa śabdeṣu sarvathā anupayogataḥ kadācid nirapekṣasya kārya ākṛti virodhataḥ kādācid ka phalam siddham tat liṅgam jñānam īdṛśam iti saṅgraha ślokau 
[II,055,i]	etena eva udāharaṇena nidarśite api hetu lakṣaṇa viṣaye svabhāvasya pṛthak karaṇam kārya udāharaṇāt sarvasya tādātmya pratītiḥ mā bhūt iti vyutpatti artham ca hetu vacana mukta artham api anumāne adhikriyate tena iha prabheda mātram ākhyātam lakṣaṇam tu tat eva etena kārya liṅga udāharaṇena svabhāvaḥ api ekadeśa bhāj uktaḥ veditavyaḥ tena eva ca sadṛśam udāharaṇam āha prayatna anantaram vyakti janmanoḥ tathā abhidhānāt 
[II,055,ii]	yat na antarīyakā sattā yaḥ vā ātmā svaḥ avibhāgavān sa tena avyabhicārī syāt iti artham tad prabhedanam saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratibandhaḥ na tādṛśaḥ na te hetavaḥ iti uktam vyabhicārasya sambhavāt sati vā pratibandhe astu saḥ eva gati sādhanaḥ niyamaḥ hi avinā abhāvaḥ aniyataḥ ca na sādhanam iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,056,i_II,057,i]	nanu yathā ukta lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ api kācid tṛtīyaḥ hetuḥ sa kim na udāhṛtaḥ saḥ api svabhāva hetau antarbhavati iti udāhṛtaḥ eva tathā hi na hi anya anupalabhyeṣu na astita anupalambhanāt tad jñāna śabdāḥ sādhyante tad bhāvāt tad nibandhanāḥ uktam etat na anyā eva anupalabdheḥ dṛśya svabhāva asattā tayā siddhayāsat jñāna śabdāḥ tad nimittāḥ sādhyantaḥ iti katham nimitta bhāve api naimittika bhāva aniyamāt evampratītiḥ siddhaḥ hi vyavahāraḥ ayam dṛśya adṛṣṭa avasan iti tasyāḥ siddhau asan digdhau tad kārya tve api dhīdhvanī 
[II,057,ii]	na hi eṣa pravartanīyaḥ vyavahāraḥ yena aniyataḥ syāt kim tarhi siddhaḥ eva dṛśyasya svabhāvasya adṛṣṭa avasan iti sa tu pratipanna tad vyavahāraḥ api prasiddheṣu nirupākhyeṣu sati api viṣaye kathañcid viṣayiṇam asmaran smāryate na hi asat vyavahārasya kvacid aparam kiñcid nibandhanam asti sa ca anena asakṛt ācarita pūrvaḥ iti na anayoḥ sambandhaḥ sādhanīyaḥ tasmāt dṛśya adṛṣṭi siddhau asan digdhā eva tad nimitta tve api asat jñāna śabdayoḥ tad yogya tā sāsnādi siddhau iva go vyavahāraḥ 
[II,057,iii]	vidyamāne api viṣaye mohāt atra ananubruvan kevalam siddha sādharmyāt smāryate samayam paraḥ kārya kāraṇa tā yadvat sādhyate dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭitaḥ kārya ādi śabdāḥ hi tayoḥ vyavahārāya kalpitāḥ kāraṇāt kārya saṃsiddhiḥ svabhāva antargamāt iyam hetu prabheda ākhyāne na darśita udāhṛtiḥ pṛthak iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,058,i_II,059,i]	asat vyavahāra yogya tā vā anupalabdheḥ vyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sādhyate vyāptiḥ ca anyatra vyavahārasya tanmātra siddhyā viśeṣa abhāvāt siddhena anupalambha ātmanā sattvena asat vyavahāraḥ sādhyate iti uktam saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ katham siddhaḥ katham vā saḥ abhāvaḥ kasyacid kāraṇam na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt eka upalambha anubhavāt idam na upalabhe iti buddheḥ upalabhe vā iti kalpikāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ na hi bhāvānām sva viṣaya jñāna abhāvāt evam bhavati idam na upalabhaḥ iti yatas abhāva vyavahāraḥ kim tarhi sva viśiṣṭa jñāna bhāvāt sarva apratipattau kvacid abhāva apratipatteḥ tasmāt kasyacid pratyakṣa tāyām tad pramāṇa balena dvau vikalpau bhavataḥ idam upalabhe aparam na upalabhe ca iti 
[II,059,ii]	yasmāt artha viśeṣa gatiḥ saṃvedana viśeṣāt saṃvedanasya tu tathāvidhātma saṃvedanāt eva bheda pratītiḥ tad svayam svatas siddha viśeṣam artham arthāt viśeṣayati anyathā saṃvedanasya api saṃvedana antara viśeṣāt viśeṣa siddhiḥ tasya api anyatas iti anavasthānāt na kasyacid viśeṣa siddhiḥ syāt arthasya tu sva sattā viśeṣābhyām na tad siddhiḥ kim tarhi sva jñāna sattā viśeṣābhyām iti na svatantrā siddhiḥ na evam saṃvedanasya saṃvedana antara sattā viśeṣābhyām tad siddhiḥ sarva apratipatti prasaṅgāt 
[II,060,i]	tasmāt viśiṣṭa rūpa anubhavāt anyā na anya nirākriyā tad viśiṣṭa upalambhaḥ atas tasya api anupalambhanam tasmāt anupalambhaḥ ayam pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati na hi eka ākāra pratiniyatāt asaṃsargiṇaḥ anubhavāt anyaḥ anya pratikṣepaḥ saḥ eva hi tat niyamāt tat eva asti iti niścāyayat nāparaḥ asti apara anubhavaḥ vā iti niścāyayati sāmarthyāt 
[II,060,ii_II,060,iii]	tasmāt eka niyata upalambhaḥ anya an upalambhaḥ tad abhāva vyavahāra siddhi hetuḥ ca sa ca sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa siddhaḥ nanu sva viśiṣṭa pratyayam antareṇa api bhavati abhāva buddhiḥ yathā santamase hasta sañcāreṇa na tatra api tathā āsañcāriṇaḥ hastasyā aantara sparśa viśeṣa upalambhāt anya abhāva gateḥ yatas hi sparśa viśeṣa upalambhāt satyasati vā prayatne sañcarati me hastaḥ iti bhavati tatas eva anya abhāva gatiḥ tad abhāve abhāva apratipatteḥ 
[II,061,i_II,061,ii]	nanu satsu upalambha kāraṇeṣu anyeṣu upalabhyasya anupalambhāt abhāva siddhiḥ tat mā bhūt svāpa ādi avasthāyām kasyacid abhāva pratītiḥ tatra indriya sādguṇyādeḥ upalambha pratyayasya eva abhāvāt tat na viśiṣṭa upalambha abhāvāt tatra kasyacid abhāva apratipattiḥ kim tarhi tādṛśaḥ anupalambhasya eva abhāvāt atra api satsu upalambha kāraṇeṣu iti teṣām indriya ādīnām vṛttisāt guṇyena upalambha vṛttim darśayati tadā hi tāni aviguṇāni bhavanti yadā eṣām kārya vṛttiḥ syāt sā ca upalabdhiḥ eva upalabhyasya anupalambhena api tasyāḥ eva viśiṣṭa upalabdheḥ eka ākāra pratiniyamaḥ tasmāt viśiṣṭa upalabdhiḥ eva anya anupalabdhiḥ 
[II,062,i_II,062,ii]	anyathā arthasya nāstitvam gamyate anupalambhataḥ upalambhasya na astitvam anyena iti anavasthitiḥ anyathā yadi sva viṣaya jñāna abhāvena abhāva siddhiḥ syāt tad abhāvaḥ api anyena anupalambhena sādhanīyaḥ iti anavasthānāt apratipattiḥ eva abhāvasya na hi saṃvedana abhāvaḥ svatas sidhyati tad aviśeṣāt viṣaye api prasaṅgāt saṃvedanam hi ātma viśeṣāt apara sādhanam na evam abhāvaḥ na sva viṣaya jñāna abhāvāt abhāva siddhiḥ yatas ayam doṣaḥ na api sva viśiṣṭa jñāna bhāvāt kim tarhi yaḥ ayam upalambhaḥ na asti ghaṭaḥ iti tatas eva abhāva upalambhāt tat ca svatantram pramāṇam iti 
[II,062,iii]	sa tarhi abhāva pratyayaḥ kutas bhavati na hi abhāvaḥ kasyacid nimittam asāmarthyāt sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt ca bhāvasya tad apāya abhāvāt tanmātra bhāvinaḥ nityam bhāva prasaṅgāt anapekṣa tvāt apekṣāyāḥ viśeṣa pratilambha lakṣaṇa tvāt tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca bhāvasya abhāvaḥ na syāt abhāvaḥ iti api bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ tad abhāvāt bhavati iti bhāvāt na bhavati iti hetu pratiṣedhaḥ asya kṛtaḥ syāt tatas ca ahetuka tvam anyathā abhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ eva kaścid nāma antareṇa uktaḥ syāt tasmāt na asya pratyayasya sambhavaḥ 
[II,063,i]	darśana ānantaryam ca svatantrasya na syāt tad bala utpattau ca tasya eva tatra sāmarthyam iti tat eva pramāṇam syāt tad ākāra niyama sāmarthyena apara pratikṣepāt ākāra antara saṃsarge tasya abhāvāt tasmāt ayam pramāṇa antara bala utpannaḥ anakṣa liṅga āśrayaḥ anupalambha vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam darśanam eva hi tat tathā utpannam yena anantaram vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpau bhavataḥ yathā nīlam paśyataḥ nīlam etat na pītam iti tasmāt na tau pramāṇam 
[II,064,i_II,064,ii]	adṛśye niścaya ayogāt sthitiḥ anyatra vāryate yathā aliṅgaḥ anya sattveṣu vikalpa ādiḥ na sidhyati aniścaya phalāḥ hi eṣā na alam vyāvṛtti sādhane ādya adhikriyate hetau niścitena eva sādhanāt iti antaraślokau tasyāḥ svayam prayogeṣu svarūpam vā prayujyate artha bādhana rūpam vā bhāve bhāvāt abhāvataḥ 
[II,064,iii_II,065,i]	sā iyam abhāva niścaya phalā vyatireka sādhanī anupalabdhiḥ yadā svayam abhāva sādhanāya prayujyate tadā svarūpeṇa vā prayujyate yathā na asti iha dhūmaḥ anupalabdheḥ na asti iha śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt na asti iha dhūmaḥ anagneḥ iti pratiṣedhya artha bādhaka rūpa upanyāsena vā prayujyate yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ agneḥ iti udāharaṇāni pūrvavat 
[II,065,ii_II,065,iv]	sa punar ayam virodhaḥ katham gamyate kvacid avikala kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt virodha gatiḥ yathā śīta uṣṇa sparśayoḥ anyonya bheda siddheḥ vā dhruva bhāva vināśa vat anyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā vā virodhaḥ nitya anitya tva vat pramāṇa bādhanāt vā api sa apekṣa dhruva bhāva vat pramāṇam vā yadi tattve bādhakam syāt tad liṅgena api virodhaḥ yathā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvayoḥ 
[II,065,v]	pramāṇam punar na vināśa niyatāḥ tad kāraṇa vādinā utpattimantaḥ abhyupeyāḥ tad bhāve para apekṣa tvena upagata tvāt ye yad bhāve para apekṣa tvena upagamyante na te tad bhāva niyatāḥ iṣyante vāsāṃsi iva rāge tad hetūnām api tatra niyamāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na teṣām sākalya apratibandha niyama asambhavāt na hi tasmin bhavati sva kāraṇa sāmagrī adhīnaiḥ anyaiḥ api tad unmukhaiḥ bhavitavyam anāyatta tvāt tad dharmatāyām vā tatas kṣaṇika tā tasya iṣṭā syāt tattve viśeṣa abhāvāt apūrva bhāvinaḥ paścāt api abhāva prasaṅgāt sa ca tad hetuḥ vā anitya tā hetu niyamana svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāva janana svabhāvaḥ vā kim na iṣyate kim pāramparyeṇa ante api tad svabhāvasya eva tad bhāve sāmarthyāt etena kādācitka svabhāva tā anapekṣa tayoḥ virodhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ 
[II,066,i]	nanu evam api virodhinoḥ paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā eva virodhaḥ aniyamena niyama bādhanāt pramāṇam pratiyoginam sādhayati bādhā punar tatas eva iti na pramāṇa bādhanāt virodhaḥ satyam virodhi vyāptena api svabhāvena arthataḥ virodhāt tad upanyāsena anupalabdheḥ prayogaḥ syāt iti darśana artham etat uktam yathā ayam eva anantara udāhṛtaḥ prayogaḥ 
[II,067,i]	atha yat idam na santi pradhāna ādayaḥ anupalabdeḥ iti tatra katham asat vyavahāra vidhiḥ sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhaḥ vā katham ca na syāt tad artha pratiṣedhe dharmi vācinaḥ aprayogāt abhidhānasya tasya pratiṣedhāt nirviṣayasya ca pratiṣedhasya ayogāt na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt anādi vāsanā udbhūta vikalpa pariniṣṭhitaḥ śabda arthaḥ trividhaḥ dharmaḥ bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayaḥ tasmin bhāva anupādāne sādhye asya anupalambhanam tathā hetuḥ na tasya eva abhāvaḥ śabda prayogataḥ 
[II,067,ii]	na ete śabdāḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ anādi kāla vāsanā prabhava vikalpa pratibhāsinam artham viṣaya tvena ātmasātkurvanti vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca tad vikalpa bhājaḥ yathā pratibhāsi vastu pratipādana samīhā prayogāt tad ākāra vikalpa jananāt ca na ca upādāna kārya pratyaya apratibhā asi rūpam śakyam tad viṣaya tvena adhyavasātum sa tu vikalpaḥ sat asat ubhaya pratyaya ahita vāsanā prabhavaḥ iti tad pratibhā asi a ākāra adhyavasāya vaśena ca bhāva abhāva ubhaya dharmaḥ iti ucyate tat atra dharmiṇi vyavasthitāḥ sat asat tvam cintayanti kim ayam pradhāna śabda pratibhāsi arthaḥ bhāva upādānaḥ na vā iti tasya bhāvān upādāna tve sādhye sa ca pratyātma vedya tvāt apratikṣepa arhaḥ arthaḥ dharmī na ca saḥ eva arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum asamprāpta vinaṣṭayoḥ api arthayoḥ tasya anapāyāt vastu viparīta ākāra niveśiṣu api tīrtha āntarīya pratyayeṣu bhāvāt 
[II,068,i_II,069,i]	parama artha eka tāna tve śabdānām anibandhanā na syāt pravṛttiḥ artheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu atīta ajātayoḥ vā api na ca syāt anṛta artha tā vācaḥ kasyāścid iti eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā matā iti saṅgraha ślokau tasya ca yathā samīhita rūpa anupādāna tve sādhye tathā anupalambhaḥ dharmaḥ asti iti na sādhana dharma asiddhiḥ 
[II,069,ii]	na tu punar atra ayam eva śabda vikalpa pratibhāsi arthaḥ apahnūyate tasya buddhau upasthāpanāya śabda prayogāt tad abhāve tad ayogāt kim ca sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phala udayaḥ na hi śabda arthaḥ sannasanvā kañcid puruṣa artham uparuṇaddhi samādadhāti vā yathā abhiniveśam atattvāt yathātattvam ca asamīhita tvāt tasmāt ayam pravartamānaḥ sarvadā sat asat cintāyām avadhīrita vikalpa pratibhāsaḥ vastu eva adhiṣṭhānīkaroti yatra ayam puruṣa arthaḥ pratibaddhaḥ yathā agnau śīta vinodana ādiḥ na hi atra śabda arthaḥ samarthaḥ tad anubhava āptau api tad abhāvāt tat ayam artha kriyā arthī tat asamartham prati na datta anuyogaḥ bhavitum yuktaḥ na hi vṛṣasyantī ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūpya parīkṣāyām avadhatte 
[II,070,i_II,070,ii]	yat punar etat uktam kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ iti tasya kaḥ arthaḥ kalpanā viṣaya tvāt śabda arthaḥ eva kalpitaḥ tasya vastu āśraya anupalambhaḥ dharmaḥ iti ayam atra abhiprāyaḥ sthitam etat svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva hetau antarbhavati iti sā tad udāharaṇena eva udāhṛtā sa punar upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ kevalaḥ vā kṛtaka tva sattva vat nāśe nirdiśyate iti uktam 
[II,070,iii_II,071,i]	tatra sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced na sattā sādhyate katham ananvayaḥ hi bhedānām vyāhataḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ yadi sattvam anitya tve anyatra vā hetuḥ syāt sādhyam api kasmāt na iṣyate tad kila evam prasādhyamānam viśeṣībhavati na ca viśeṣaḥ sādhayitum śakyate ananvayāt yathā āha pramāṇa viṣaya aparijñānāt iti saḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ na sādhyaḥ eva vyāhanyate kim tarhi hetau api tulya doṣa tvāt na hi hetuḥ ananvayaḥ siddheḥ aṅgam tatas saṃśayāt 
[II,071,ii_II,071,iii]	na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt bhāva upādāna mātre tu sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syāt aniṣiddham ca tādṛśam na sarvathā sattā sādhane viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavati bhāva mātra viśeṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ asti kaścid dharmi iti prasādhayataḥ anirdiṣṭa svabhāva viśeṣasya kasyacid sattā mātre virodha abhāvāt na iha sattā sādhane pratiṣedhaḥ kim tu tathā asti kaścid iti kañcana asya bhedam aparāmṛśan bruvāṇaḥ kam sva artham puṣṇāti tasmāt anena upātta bhedaḥ eva sādhyaḥ 
[II,072,i_II,072,iii]	upātta bhede sādhye asmin bhavet hetuḥ ananvayaḥ sattāyām tena sādhyāyām viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet sa hi dharmī pradhāna lakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ nityaḥ sukha ādi ātmakaḥ anyaḥ vā iti yathā kathañcid api viśeṣitaḥ tad svabhāvaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavati sa ca tathā na anveti yat api sattā mātram anveti na tena siddhena kiñcid nanu evam agni ādiṣu api prasaṅgaḥ tatra api hi na agni sattāyām kaścid vivādaḥ viśiṣṭa ādhāra viśeṣaṇasya tu abhimatasya ananvayāt asiddhiḥ na vai saḥ ādhāraḥ tam viśeṣīkaroti ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt iti uktam tasmāt tatra sāmānyam eva sādhyate tad ayoga vyavacchedena 
[II,073,i]	na tathā iha api kvacid sattāyāḥ sādhanam pradhāna ādi śabda vācyasya eva kasyacid arthasya abhāvāt nirviśeṣaṇā eva sā katham abhāvaḥ jñeya abhidheya prameya tvaiḥ saḥ api siddhaḥ eva tat kim idānīm jñeyam asti iti siddhiḥ astu tathā api kim siddham syāt nanu bauddhaḥ vikalpa pratibhāsaḥ śabda arthaḥ tasya ca sva lakṣaṇa upādāna tā sādhyate sādhya tām kim tu asau api pradhāna ādi lakṣaṇa bhedān āśrayaḥ śabda artha mātra tāyām avatiṣṭhate tathā ca pūrvavat abhidhā iyam kim api asti iti sādhyam syāt na hi śabda arthāḥ svatas kañcid guṇa viśeṣam āviśanti upādāna dharmaḥ teṣu upacaryate tad asiddha upādāneṣu na sambhavati tat ime nirviśeṣaṇāḥ teṣu artha upādāna tva sādhanam artha sattā mātra sādhanam eva na artha viśeṣa sādhanam iti apārthakam anyatra tu tat eva agni sāmānyam tatra asiddham iti sādhyate 
[II,074,i]	nanu ca atra api tad ayoga virahiṇā sāmānyena anvayaḥ na siddhaḥ eva na vai kaścid tathābhūtena ātmanā anvayam karoti pratipādayatā hi param dhūmaḥ agninā antarīyakaḥ darśanīyaḥ yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti sa tathā agni mātreṇa vyāptaḥ siddhaḥ yatra eva svayam dṛśyate tatra eva agni buddhim janayati tatra sādhya nirdeśena na kiñcid tatra darśana sambandha ākhyāna mātra ādiṣṭa siddheḥ tad anirdeśe vā katham tad viśiṣṭena anvayaḥ tat ayam agninā vinā bhāvī siddhaḥ arthāt eva agneḥ tad pradeśa ayogam vyavacchinatti iti sa tathā sādhyaḥ ucyate na punar tathā asya upanyāsa pūrvakaḥ anvayaḥ sādhya ukteḥ iha anaṅga tvāt tad pūrvaka tve vā kaḥ pratijñām sādhanāt apākaroti tathā ca āha liṅgasya avyabhicāraḥ tu dharmeṇa anyatra darśyate tatra prasiddham tat yuktam dharmiṇam gamayiṣyati iti tasmāt na agni ādi sādhana vat sattā sādhanam api anavadyam 
[II,075,i_II,075,ii]	aparāmṛṣṭa tad bhede vastu mātre tu sādhane tanmātra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate sādhane punar sattve svabhāva viśeṣa aparigraheṇa vastu mātra vyāpini sādhya dharme na anvaya vyāghātaḥ na hi tatra avaśyam viśeṣa parigrahaḥ kāryaḥ sat mātra āśraye api sādhana sāmarthyāt na sādhya tve vaiphalyāt 
[II,075,iii_II,075,v]	api ca na asiddhe bhāva dharmaḥ asti vyabhicāryu bhaya āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham sattāyām hi sādhyāyām sarvaḥ tad hetuḥ na trayīm doṣa jātim ativartate asiddhim vyabhicāram virodham ca tatra yadi bhāva dharmaḥ hetuḥ ucyate sa katham asiddha sattāke syāt yaḥ hi bhāva dharmam hetum icchati sa katham bhāvam na icchet svabhāvaḥ eva hi kayācid apekṣayā dharmaḥ iti vyatirekī iva dharmiṇaḥ nirdiśyate na hi dharma dharmi vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ vācye kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti iti nirloṭhitam etat pramāṇa vārttike 
[II,076,i]	atha punar ubhaya dharmam brūyāt anāśrita vastunaḥ aparyudāsena vyatireka mātrasya abhāve api avirodhāt yathā na bhavati mūrtaḥ iti amūrta tvam nirupākhye api syāt nirupākhyasya abhāvāt apratiṣedha viṣaya tā iti ced tat kim idānīm vidhi viṣayaḥ astu tat api na iti ced katham idānīm na pratiṣedha viṣayaḥ vidhi nivṛtti rūpa tvāt pratiṣedhasya parisaṅkhyāteṣu eva pratiṣedha vṛttiḥ iṣṭā tat na anupākhyeṣu amūrta tva ādikam iti ced duḥkham vatā ayam tapasvī sa aṅketikam icchā mātra anurodhinam artham niyantu kāmaḥ jīvati tasya sa uraḥ tāḍam krandataḥ api lokasya anivṛtteḥ yathā saṅketam pratipatteḥ tanmātra prayojana tvāt śabda prayogasya iṣṭa aviśeṣāt ubhayatra apratīti prasaṅgāt tatas api pratīteḥ samāśrayāt tasya anyatra api tulya tvāt tat etat vyavaccheda mātram dvayoḥ api sambhavat vipakṣa pracāra śaṅkā vyavacchedena labhyam gamaka tvam katham ātmasāt kuryāt 
[II,077,i_II,077,ii^1]	avyavaccheda rūpāḥ api khalu jñeya tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ kathañcid avastūnām api buddhyā vyavasthāpanāt sādhāraṇāḥ santi te api etena vyākhyātāḥ sa ca sva vāca ubhaya dharma tām bruvāṇaḥ sataḥ anyatra api asya vṛttim bhāṣate sattāyām ca avyabhicāram iti katham na unmattaḥ vipakṣa vṛttyā vyabhicāraḥ tad pakṣa sa pakṣa ani atara tva ādīnām avipakṣa vṛtteḥ ubhaya dharma tve api adoṣaḥ na hi pakṣaḥ eva vyabhicāra viṣayaḥ kam punar atra bhavān vipakṣam pratyeti sādhya abhāvam katham idānīm hetuḥ avipakṣa vṛttiḥ ubhaya dharmaḥ ca na hi pakṣa vipakṣa pravibhāga apekṣayā hetoḥ avyabhicāraḥ vāstava tvāt na hi avinābhāvaḥ hetoḥ vyavasthayā darśyate sarvaḥ apakṣaḥ kṛtakaḥ anityaḥ iti kim tarhi vastu bala āyātā eva khalu vyāptiḥ pramāṇaiḥ upadarśyate sarvam kṛtakam anityam iti tathā asiddhau eva hi sa dharmaḥ tasya gamakaḥ syāt 
[II,077,ii^2]	na anyathā puruṣa pravṛtteḥ avastu pāratantryāt yam hi puruṣaḥ sādhayitum icchati sa pakṣaḥ sa yam evam vyabhicāra viṣayam paśyati tam eva pakṣīkuryāt na ca anumāna viṣaye pratyakṣa ādi bādhā asti pramāṇasya pramāṇa antareṇa bādhāyām tasya aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt lakṣaṇa yukte bādhā sambhave tad lakṣaṇam eva dūṣitam syāt iti uktam abādhanasya api lakṣaṇa tve tasya aniścaya lakṣaṇa tā tathā ca āgamaka tvam iti kim kasya sādhanam yad artham avyabhicāraḥ cintyate tasmāt vastutas yat yena vyāptam avyāptam vā tat tasya gamakam agamakam ca iti na puruṣa icchayā vastu dharmaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate yadā ayam pakṣīkaroti tadā na vyabhicāraḥ anyadā tena vyabhicāraḥ iti su vyavadātam prāmāṇyam 
[II,079,i_II,079,ii]	abhāva dharmam tu bhāva mātra vyāpinaḥ arthasya vyavacchedam hetum sattāyām vadataḥ asya viruddhaḥ hetuḥ syāt tasya bhāve kvacid asambhavāt abhāve ca sarvatra bhāva vyavacchedasya bhāvāt tat ayam tri prakāraḥ api dharmaḥ sattā sādhane na hetu lakṣaṇa bhāj na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt na sattā sādhyate 
[II,080,i_II,080,iii]	sādhana tve punar asyāḥ sāmānyena tanmātra vyāpini vastu dharme siddha sattāke dharmiṇi na asiddhiḥ tena ca sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptiḥ yadi kathañcid niścīyeta tadā na virodha vyabhicārau iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ iti eṣa dvividhaḥ hetuḥ svabhāva lakṣaṇaḥ kārya lakṣaṇaḥ ca saḥ eva sva vyāpaka viparyaye sādhye viruddhaḥ iti darśayan caturaḥ pakṣa dharmān āha bheda sāmānyayoḥ ca anaikāntikayoḥ aikāntika tām bruvāṇam prativahan dvau tat ca hetvābhāseṣu eva avasara prāptam vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,080,iv]	vyāvṛtti prādhānya sādhana artham hetoḥ trīn pakṣa dharmān āha tathā hi na anvaya mukhena hetuḥ gamakaḥ anitya tvāt aprayatna anantarīyaka tvasya āgateḥ mā bhūt atas gatiḥ kevala tvāt avyatirekatayā anvayasya iti ced iha tarhi bhavatu asparśa tvāt nityaḥ iti na atra api anvayasya aprādhānyāt iti ced iha tu balavān anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ ca durbalaḥ hetoḥ sa pakṣa vyāpteḥ vipakṣe ca kvacid abhāvāt yathā prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ anitya tvāt iti na bhavati sarvatas vipakṣāt avyāvṛtteḥ iti ced evam tarhi yaḥ kṛtakaḥ saḥ anityaḥ eva iti nitya vyavacchedena gamakateṣṭā syāt anyathā sarvatas vipakṣāt vyāvṛtteḥ darśayitum aśakyatvāt tat asya na bhāva mātreṇa na sāmyena na prādhānyena gatiḥ 
[II,081,i_II,082,ii]	aprādhānye api anvayasya vyatireka vyāptau asti yathā anityaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti tasmāt evam eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ yaḥ prayatna ānantarīyaḥ saḥ anityaḥ eva iti nitya vyavacchedena asya vākyasya śabda pradeśa ādiṣu nitya anagni vyavacchedena vyatireka gatau sāmarthya parisamāpteḥ na ca eteṣām bheda mātram gamyate kim tu tat eva sāmānyam apratipakṣam idam eva iha na anyat iti yadi avaśyam ete ananya saṃsargiṇaḥ gamyāḥ saḥ eva eṣām asaṃsargaḥ gamyaḥ astu tāvatā kārya parisamāpteḥ kim antar gaḍunā sāmānyena iti vyāvṛtti sādhanena darśayati yaḥ tarhi samarthena hetunā kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate sa katham trividhe hetau antarbhavati hetunā yaḥ samarthena kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate artha antara anapekṣa tvāt sa svabhāvaḥ anuvarṇitaḥ 
[II,082,iii]	asau api yathāsannihitāt na anyam apekṣate iti tanmātra anubandhī svabhāvaḥ bhāvasya tatra hi kevalam samagrāṇām kāraṇānām kārya utpādana yogya tā anumīyate yogyatā ca sāmagrī mātra anubandhinī iti svabhāva bhūtā eva kim punar kāraṇam sāmagryāḥ kāryam eva na anumīyate yena na samagrāṇi iti eva kāraṇa dravyāṇi sva kāryam janayanti sāmagrī janmanām śaktīnām pariṇāma apekṣa tvāt kārya utpādasya atra antare ca pratibandha sambhavān na kārya anumānam yogyatāyāḥ tu dravya antara anapekṣa tvāt aviruddham uttarottara śakti pariṇāmena samartheyam kāraṇa sāmagrī kārya utpādane śakti pariṇāma pratyayasya anyasya apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt iti pūrva sva jāti mātra hetu tvāt śakti prasūteḥ sāmagryā yogyatā ananyā apekṣaṇī iti ucyate 
[II,083,i]	samagrāṇi eva kāraṇāni yogyatām api anumāpayanti asamagrasya ekānta asāmrthyāt iti na tatas kārya anumānam vipakṣe vṛtti adarśane api śeṣavat yathā deha indriya buddhibhyaḥ rāga ādi anumānam ātma ātmīya abhiniveśa pūrvakāḥ hi rāga ādayaḥ aham mama iti ca apaśyataḥ anunaya pratighā abhāvāt ayoni śomanaskāram antareṇa doṣāṇām anutpatteḥ deha ādīnām hetu tve api na kevalānām sāmarthyam asti iti vipakṣa vṛtteḥ adṛṣṭau api śeṣavat etat vyabhicāri liṅgam 
[II,084,i]	yā tarhi akārya kāraṇa bhūtena anyena rasa ādinā rūpa ādi gatiḥ sā katham sā api eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpa ādeḥ asatas gatiḥ hetu dharma anumānena dhūma indhana vikāra vat tatra api hetuḥ eva tathābhūtaḥ anumīyate pravṛtta śakti rūpa upādāna kāraṇa sahakāri pratyayaḥ hi rasa hetuḥ rasam janayati indhana vikāra upādāna hetu sahakāri pratyaya agni dhūma janana vat tathā hi sva kāraṇasya phala utpādanam pratyābhimukhyena vinā na rasaḥ tat eva ca rūpa upādāna hetūnām pravṛtti kāraṇam sā api rasa upādāna kāraṇa pravṛttiḥ rūpa upādāna kāraṇa pravṛtti sahakāriṇī tasmāt yathābhūtāt hetaḥ rasaḥ utpannaḥ tathābhūta m anumāpayan rūpam anumāpayati tatra api atīta eka kālānām gatiḥ nā anāgatānām vyabhicārāt tasmāt iyam api kārya liṅga jā 
[II,085,i_II,085,iii]	etena pipīlika utsaraṇa matsya vikāra ādeḥ varṣa ādi anumānam vyākhyātam tatra api bhūta pariṇāmaḥ eva kaścid varṣa hetuḥ pipīlikā saṅkṣobha ādi hetuḥ ca iti rūpāt sparśa anumānam kārya liṅga jam rūpa ādīnām bhūta āśraya tvāt yat tarhi idam viṣāṇī go tvāt iti tat katham tatra api samudāya vyavasthāyāḥ kāraṇam samudāyinaḥ asatsu teṣu sā na syāt iti go tvāt viṣāṇitā 
[II,086,i_II,086,iii]	sāsnā viṣāṇa ādi samudāyaḥ hi gauḥ tat iyam samudāya vyavasthā samudāyi nibandhana tvāt tad abhāve na syāt bhavantī sva nimitta sannidhim sūcayati iti go tvāt viṣāṇita apratipattiḥ kārya liṅga jā ādhārataḥ abhinirvṛtteḥ ātmanaḥ tādṛśaḥ ambhasaḥ kāryam tasya yaḥ api sthiram ambhaḥ dṛṣṭvā adṛṣṭaḥ api adhastāt ādhāra sambhavaḥ anumīyate tat api kārya liṅga jam eva tādṛśasya ātmanaḥ ambhasaḥ tatas ādhārāt abhinirvṛtteḥ na hi tasmāt upakāram ananubhavataḥ tatas avasthā viśeṣa pratilambhaḥ yuktaḥ upakārasya artha antara tve api uktam 
[II,086,iv]	na vai tatas ātma viśeṣa utpatteḥ ambhasaḥ tathā sthitiḥ kim tarhi saṃyogāt kim punar sa tayoḥ saṃyogaḥ tābhyām jananāt samavāyāt vā sa kim ekatra na samavaiti janyate vā tasya asāmarthyāt tat asamartham pṛthak tatra sahitam api tādṛśam eva iti anupakāraka tvāt na saṃyogena tadvat syāt sahitasya tad anya upakārāt viśeṣa utpatteḥ sāmarthyam kaḥ ayam ajanya janaka bhūtānām upakāraḥ svarūpasya siddheḥ akārya tvāt para rūpa kriyāyām api tatra anupakārāt ubhayathā akārakasya akiñcid kara tvena anupakāraka tvāt iti ukta prāyam tasmāt sarve eva vastu sambandhāḥ janakasya eva upayoga viśeṣa vaśāt pravibhāgena kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vyavasthāpyante tat ayam kuṇḍa bhū tala ādīnām api ādhāra bhāvaḥ badara udaka ādiṣu janana śaktiḥ eva tasmāt eteṣu tad ātmanā vyapadeśa ādayaḥ janya janaka bhāva kṛtāḥ eva bhavantu sati api saṃyoge tat na antarīyaka tvāt eṣām paramparā kalpanāyāḥ ca vaiyarthyāt 
[II,088,i^1]	sthāpaka tvāt ādhāraḥ na janaka tvāt iti ced sthiteḥ artha antara anartha antara tve upakāreṇa vyākhyāte pāta pratibandhāt sthāpakaḥ iti ced kaḥ pratibandhaḥ sa hi tasya pāta pratibandhaḥ na artha antaram eva yaḥ sthāpayitrā kriyate artha antara tve tatra eva upayogaḥ iti kaḥ patataḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibandhāt apāte api tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ kṛtaḥ nāma sa tena pratibandha ākhyaḥ padārthaḥ sa tu bhāvaḥ prasarpaṇa dharma apracyuta anutpanna ātma bhūta viśeṣaḥ kim na patati iti pratibandhāt atiśaya pratipattau tasya api ātma antara tve tat eva vastunaḥ tādātmyāt patanam anavasthā ca na ca tathābhūta ātma kriyām pratibandham abhyupaiti tasmāt pāta abhāvaḥ pratibandhaḥ sa katham kenacid kriyate abhāvam karoti iti hi na abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid kāryaḥ 
[II,088,i^2]	tasya kathañcid kārya tve abhāva ayogāt pūrvavat prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt bhāva kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ eṣa bhāvam na karoti iti yāvat tena ayam evam vācyaḥ syāt pātam na karoti iti tat api iṣṭam eva na hi tasya tad kṛtaḥ pātaḥ svayam patana dharma tayā pātāt ākāśa kṣipta vat tathā ca ayam atra akiñcitkaraḥ katham asya sthāpayitā tat ayam na kenacid pratibaddhaḥ iti na kadācid tiṣṭhet tasmāt pāta pratibandhaḥ iti api kṣaṇikānām bhāvānām upādānasamāna deśa utpādaḥ ucyate 
[II,089,i_II,090,i]	tasmāt siddhā tādṛśaḥ ambhasaḥ ādhārāt utpattiḥ balākā api vṛtteḥ toya samāśrayāt kāryam tasya iti anuvartate toya āśritā hi balākāyāḥ vṛttiḥ tatas śarīra sthitim pratilabhamānā tad kārya tayā pratibandhena toyam gamayati deśa ādi apekṣayā anayā diśā anyeṣu api gamakeṣu pratibandhaḥ sādhyaḥ tat na trividhāt hetoḥ anyaḥ gamakaḥ asti apratibaddha svabhāvasya avinābhāva niyama abhāvāt iti 
[II,091,i_II,092,i]	asiddha jñāpana aṅgasya jñāpanam pratyaśaktitaḥ trairūpya asiddhi sandehe prapattṝṇām asādhanam jñāpakaḥ hi hetuḥ yat ātma tayā jñāpayati tad asiddhau sandehe vā na jñāpakaḥ śabda vat trairūpyāt ca hetuḥ artham gamayati asambaddhāt apratipatteḥ mahānasa ādi dṛṣṭa dhūma āt iva udadhau agneḥ apratibandhāt ca sarvatas sarva pratipatti prasaṅgāt tasmāt pratipādya pratipāda kayoḥ asiddha sandigdha dharmi sambandha anvaya vyatirekāḥ dharmāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ tatra eka aprasiddhi sandehe aprasiddhaḥ vyabhicāra bhāj dvayoḥ viruddhaḥ asiddhau ca sandehe vyabhicāra bhāj ekaikasya rūpasya asiddhau sandehe vā asiddhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ ca hetvābhāsaḥ bhavati dharmi sambandha asiddha avasiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ cākṣuṣa tvāt 
[II,092,ii_II,092,iii]	cetanāḥ taravaḥ sarva tvac apaharaṇe maraṇāt iti prativādi anabhyupagataḥ vijñāna indriya āyuḥ nirodha lakṣaṇa tvāt maraṇasya katham ca maraṇam abhyupayat na caitanyam abhyupeyāt maraṇa śabda pravṛtteḥ siddham eva iti ced icchātaḥ śabdāḥ pravartante na tad vaśāt vastu sthitiḥ atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt śoṣa mayam taruṣu maraṇam āha na ca īdṛśam prāṇi maraṇam iti na idam taruṣu sidhyati na hi anapekṣita vastukam śabda mātram icchā vṛtti vidyate iti vastu gamyam vastu sidhyati etena anitya tva saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādayaḥ acetana tva viśiṣṭa buddhi pūrvaka tva ādi sādhanāḥ buddhi bhuvana ādīnām vyākhyātāḥ tatra api hi śabdaḥ eva kevalaḥ siddhaḥ na arthaḥ 
[II,092,iv]	na hi pare apracyuta ātmanaḥ upalayanam anitya tām icchanti nanu avivakṣita viśeṣam sāmānyam siddham eva tad siddhau viśeṣa vikalpena asiddhi codanā mithyā uttaram eva bhavati syāt mithyā uttaram yadi dvayoḥ api iṣṭam kiñcid vastu sāmānyam syāt yat nibandhanaḥ ayam anitya śabdaḥ kṛtaka tva ādi vat nanu asti eva tirodhānam na vai paraḥ tat anitya tvam āha kim tarhi vināśam nanu vinaṣṭa tirohitayoḥ dvayoḥ api avyaktiḥ tulya iti asti eva sāmānyam atha kā iyam avyaktiḥ adṛśya ātma tā nanu anena lakṣaṇena pradhāna puruṣa ādayaḥ api anityāḥ prasajanti prāc anya dharmaṇaḥ avyaktiḥ anitya tā iti ced anya dharmā ca prāc apracyuta ātmā iti ca su vyāhṛtam 
[II,093,i^1]	etena tad avasthā nivṛttiḥ vyākhyātā yaḥ api avasthā nivṛttim tirodhāna sadṛśīm śabda viṣayam āha tasya api sā katham nivṛttā apracyutā ca avasthā nivartate na avasthāta iti ced kā iyam avasthā yā iyam udaka dhāraṇa ādi artha kriyāyām upanidhīyate yāmayam jantuḥ adhyakṣa madhyavasyati ghaṭaḥ ayam iti tad nivṛttau anivṛttau api aparasya asya sarvasya abhāvāt evam tarhi sā eva avasthā ghaṭaḥ astu yathā ukta lakṣaṇa tvāt asya sa ca nivṛttaḥ iti anivṛttaḥ avasthāta avasthitaḥ paryanuyojyaḥ sanvā na ghaṭaḥ bhāvikaḥ atad lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu ekam eva avasthā antara āveśāt bheda dṛṣṭiḥ iti ced 
[II,093,i^2]	saḥ eva avasthā bhedaḥ vastu bheda lakṣaṇam kim na iṣyate evam hi sukha ādīnām asandigdhaḥ bhedaḥ bhavati kasyacid rūpasya anukārāt avasthā bhede api abhedaḥ iti ced nanu etat sukha ādīnām puruṣāṇām ca tulyam bhede krama abhivyakti virodhāt aikyam iti ced tad kim idānīm akrama abhivyakteḥ ghaṭa dadhi ādiḥ anekaḥ kaḥ vā virodhaḥ krama abhivyakteḥ abheda vyāpana asiddhau kramaḥ tu tad kārya tvāt tasya tad aniṣpattau aniṣpatteḥ abhedaḥ eva atitarāma krama tva prasaṅgaḥ eka ātma tva vat kārya tvāt eva abhedaḥ iti ced yuktaḥ yadi pratibandhaḥ sidhyet sa ca ananvayasya na sidhyati iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,094,i_II,095,iii]	sarvathā na asti samānaḥ dharmaḥ dhvasta itarayoḥ abheda kalpanāyām api yam ayam anitya śabdaḥ samāviśet yathā utpattim hetubhyaḥ kṛtaka śabdaḥ sambandhi bheda vyudāse api tathā maraṇa sāmānyam vṛkṣa puruṣayoḥ yad darśanāt prāṇi antare mṛta pratipattiḥ tādṛśam yadi taruṣu upalabhyeta syāt etat atha śoṣa ādikam eva maraṇa śabdena vadet tasya api pratibandhaḥ caitanyena sampradhāryaḥ yatas sidhyet tathā saṃsthānam api yādṛśam prāsāda ādi bhedeṣu anuvṛttimat buddhi pūrvakam dṛṣṭam yat dṛṣṭeḥ akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛta buddhiḥ bhavati yadi tādṛśam syāt sarve eva hetavaḥ tathā syuḥ api ca 
[II,096,i]	siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi tat yuktam tasmāt yat anumīyate vastu bhede prasiddhasya śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ na yuktā anumitiḥ pāṇḍu dravyāt iva hutāśane anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛd vikārasya kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyet valmīkasya api tad kṛtiḥ sādhyena anugamāt kārye sāmānyena api sādhane sambandhi bhedāt bheda ukti doṣaḥ kārya samaḥ mataḥ jāti antare prasiddhasya śabda sāmānya darśanāt na yuktam sādhanam go tvāt vāc ādīnām viṣāṇi vat vivakṣā paratantra tvāt na śabdāḥ santi kutra vā tad bhāvāt artha siddhau tu sarvam sarvasya sidhyati vastu svarūpe asiddhe ayam nyāyaḥ siddhe viśeṣaṇam adoṣa kṛt asiddhau api ākāśa āśraya vat hvaneḥ asiddhau api śabdasya siddhe vastuni sidhyati aulūkyasya yathā bauddhena uktam mūrti ādi sādhanam iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,097,i]	yā punar śāstra āśrayeṇa anyatarā siddhiḥ udbhāvyate yathā abhivyakti vādinaḥ kṛtaka tvam asiddham iti na tat sarvatra anumāne pramāṇa dṛṣṭasya pratijñayā asiddhi codanā ayogāt anadhikārāt ca śāstrasya anumāne pramāṇena eva bādhane tad bhāva pramāṇa apratītau vā kim abhivyakti vādena tasmāt śāstra āśrayaḥ eva anumāne anyatara asiddhiḥ śāstreṇa anyatra tu ajñānāt iti na vāda udāharaṇam udāharaṇa diśam tu ācāryaḥ prāha 
[II,098,i]	yaḥ punar pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ asiddhaḥ ucyate yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ śabda tvāt iti saḥ api sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhedāt sādhyasya dharmiṇaḥ sva sādhane sādhana tva asiddheḥ hetu bhāvena asiddhaḥ ucyate na hi saḥ eva tasya sādhanam bhavati tad bhāva mātra anuṣaṅgiṇi punar tad nirdeśasya vaiyarthyāt na hi tatra aparaḥ viśeṣaḥ nirdiśyate sa śabda tayā tathā abhavan pakṣa nirdeśaḥ eva tathā sidhyati punar api svatas eva tathā abhāvāt tasmāt sa svayam ātmanaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ 
[II,098,ii_II,098,iii]	katham vai śabdaḥ asiddhaḥ siddhaḥ śabdaḥ saḥ ātmani hetu rūpaḥ na siddhaḥ iti asiddhaḥ ucyate sa ca śabdaḥ pakṣīkṛtaḥ na ca aparaḥ śabdaḥ yaḥ hetuḥ syāt tasya eva ca hetu tve apunar nirdeśyaḥ iti uktam avivādaḥ ca nityam tad bhāva siddheḥ anvaya adṛṣṭeḥ asiddhiḥ iti ced tat kim idānīm dharmī dharmi antare anvayībhavitā pradīpa ādayaḥ tu svabhāva yogyatayā ātmani jñānam utpādayantaḥ tathā prakāśamānāḥ sva ātma prakāśakāḥ iti ucyante na evam liṅga liṅginoḥ bheda āśraya tvāt tad bhāvasya na hi svayam jñāna viṣaya tā liṅgasya liṅgi pratipādanam dharmiṇaḥ tu sva sādhane ayam prasaṅgaḥ 
[II,099,i]	sarva bhāveṣu dharmi dharma bheda asiddheḥ sarvatra eṣa doṣaḥ tulyaḥ iti ced uktam atra bhāvānām vyāvṛtti samāśraya vyavahāra bhedāt sādhya sādhana bhedaḥ iti parama artha vicāreṣu tathābhūta asiddheḥ tattva anya tvam padārtheṣu sāṃvṛteṣu pratiṣidhyate anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ punar pratyaya siddham bhedam avalambya prakalpyate 
[II,100,i_II,100,iii]	yathāsvam bheda niṣṭheṣu pratyayeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāḥ ca bhāsante vyavahāraḥ tad āśrayaḥ vyavahāra upanītaḥ atra saḥ eva āśliṣṭa bheda dhīḥ sādhyaḥ sādhana tām nītaḥ tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ iti saṅgraha ślokau tasmāt na dharmī hetuḥ ubhaya asiddheḥ etena dharmaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ tatra api yadi tatas eva siddhiḥ sa prāk eva nirdiṣṭaḥ iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ vācyaḥ anvayā siddhi vacane api na hi saḥ eva ātmānam anveti iti asambaddham
