[II,100,iv_II,101,i]	yadā tarhi vipakṣa vyatirekaḥ hetuḥ ucyate tadā katham tatra api sādhya abhāvaḥ vipakṣaḥ iti tad vyatirekaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ eva iti asiddhaḥ nanu pakṣa ādīnām para sparataḥ bhedāt avipakṣa tvam pakṣe asti eva kaḥ pakṣaḥ kaḥ vā vipakṣaḥ yatra kaścid dharmaḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tad vyatirekaḥ vipakṣaḥ sa tarhi icchayā vyavasthita lakṣaṇaḥ katham vipakṣasya vastu vaśāt vyavasthām apanudet hetuḥ ca evam na kaścid anaikāntikaḥ syāt vipakṣasya api icchā kṛta tvāt iti ukta prāyam sādhya vyatireke ca vipakṣe tad vyatirekaḥ yadi dharmiṇi siddhaḥ kim asiddham yad artham hetuḥ ucyate 
[II,101,ii]	na vai sādhya asiddhi mātreṇa sarvaḥ vipakṣaḥ kim tarhi tad vyatirekeṇa ubhaya niścitaḥ iti aniścayāt siddham avipakṣa tvam dharmiṇi sandigdha sādhya dharmā api evam avipakṣaḥ iti tad avipakṣa tvam aniścita sādhya vyatireka vyāvṛtti rūpam katham sādhanam aniścita tad lakṣaṇa tvāt tena eva niścayaḥ kriyate iti ced katham aniścayāt niścayaḥ vyatireka aniścayaḥ hi avipakṣa śabdena ucyate tatas eva katham abhāva niścayaḥ yasmāt idam iha sandigdham tasmāt idam iha na asti iti ca subhāṣitam 
[II,102,i]	tasmāt anapekṣita pakṣa vyavasthau dharmāṇām vṛtti vyatirekau paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇau na tṛtīyam rāśim vyatirecayataḥ tayoḥ ekasya nivṛttiḥ aparasya vṛttiḥ iti katham anitya abhāva vyatirekaḥ anitye sādhye dharmiṇi sidhyet tat kim idānīm pakṣaḥ api vipakṣaḥ syāt api paryāyeṇa lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ tu kathitaḥ eva na hi avipakṣa śaṅkāyām sādhya abhāva vyavaccheda artham hetuḥ ucyate na ca hetoḥ sambandha upadarśana kāle pakṣa ādi vikalpaḥ asti yatas ayam doṣaḥ syāt sa hi kevalaḥ eva kasyacid bhāva abhāvayoḥ vṛtti vyatirekavān upadarśitaḥ svayam bhavat sāmarthyena tat tathābhūtam āpādayati iti sa tasya pāścātyaḥ sāmarthya viṣayaḥ pakṣaḥ ucyate tena tad lakṣaṇa mukhena āyātaḥ dharmaḥ na pratyāyana kāla bhāvi iti anaṅgam 
[II,102,ii_II,103,i]	yat tarhī damita rata dviparīta vinirmukta tvāt iti na tatra eṣa doṣaḥ itara grahaṇāt kevalaḥ hi tad viparīta virahaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ syāt na punar kutaścid asate iti asti sādhya sādhanayoḥ viśeṣaḥ atra api viśeṣaṇa upādānam iṣṭasya eva bādhakam na hi tasya asattā anabhyupagamaḥ itara grahaṇam samartham bhavati yathā māṭharāditaraḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhojanīyaḥ iti māṭharasya abrāhmaṇye brāhmaṇaḥ bhojanīyaḥ iti eva vācyam syāt 
[II,103,ii]	parasya ayam abhiprāyaḥ asat iti tad abhiprāya vaśāt evam uktam tena itara asat viraheṇa tvayā upagata tvāt iti arthaḥ tatra api kaḥ pāramārthikaḥ asatām parasparataḥ vibhāgaḥ ekasya hi rūpam anyatra apaśyantī buddhiḥ idam asmāt vibhaktam iti pratyeti tad arūpāṇām kutas bhāve vā na asantaḥ syuḥ tad lakṣaṇa tvāt sattvasya kevalam vikalpa viracitam asantam api eṣām ātmānam vibhāgavantam iva anyānyaiḥ vyapadeśaiḥ vaktāraḥ pradarśayanti na ca tad kṛtaḥ vibhāgaḥ vastu vyavasthāyāḥ samāśrayaḥ atiprasaṅgāt iti uktam itaretara vibhāgam ca anena sattā anuṣaṅgiṇam prathayatā asattā eva sarvatra utsāditā bhavati tathā api īdam asiddham eva asataḥ virahāt iti vyabhicāri vā 
[II,104,i]	atha api tad abhimatāt kutaścid nānā bhāvaḥ evambhāvaḥ syāt na tarhi tatas nānābhāvāt evambhāvaḥ bhavati kim tarhi tad mateḥ punar icchā parāvṛttau anyatra api evambhāvasya abhimateḥ tat iha icchāyām eva sāmarthyam avasthitam iti sā eva iṣṭa vastu svabhāva anukarṣiṇī proktā syāt tat kim eṣām paraspara viraheṇa sā eva hetuḥ vācyaḥ syāt tatra ca vastu pratibandhaḥ vācyaḥ anyathā asiddheḥ etena ātma para upagama ādayaḥ puruṣa vyavasthā samāśrayāḥ sarve hetavaḥ vyākhyātāḥ yathā avipakṣa tvāt tad samudāya eka deśa tvāt ityādayaḥ anayā diśā sarva prayogeṣu vacana parāvṛtti kṛtam vibhramam utsṛjya artha vyavasthāpana nītiḥ anusartavyā 
[II,105,i]	anityaḥ prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti eṣa katham na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ tasya eva abhinna vyāvṛtti samāśraya tvāt abhinna pratyaya viṣayasya vyavahāra upanītasya sādhya dharmiṇaḥ sādhana tve pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam uktam viśeṣam punar sādhya dharmiṇam kṛtvā sāmānyam hetum bruvāṇasya dharma bhedāt aṅga aṅgitā na virudhyate 
[II,105,ii]	bheda sāmānyayoḥ dharma bhedāt aṅga aṅgita iṣyate yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ prayatna uttha tayā dhvaniḥ pakṣa aṅga tve api abādha tvāt na asiddhiḥ bhinna dharmiṇi yathā aśvaḥ na viṣāṇi tvāt eṣa piṇḍaḥ viṣāṇavān sādhya kāla aṅga tā vā na nivṛtteḥ upalakṣya tat tatas eva apratijñā arthaḥ viśeṣaḥ dharma bhedataḥ iti antaraślokāḥ 
[II,106,i_II,106,vi]	tathā svayam tad āśrayasya vā sandehe ahetuḥ yathā bāṣpa ādi bhāvena sandigdhaḥ bhūta saṃhātaḥ agni siddhau yathā ca iha nikuñje mayūraḥ kekāyitāt iti tad āpāta deśa vibhrame dharmya siddhau api yathā sarvatra sukha ādi sambhavāt vibhuḥ ātmā iti evam ekasya pakṣa dharmasya hetu rūpasya asiddhau sandehe vā asiddhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ tathā ekasya rūpasya asiddhau sandehe vā anaikāntikaḥ katamasya ekasya vyatirekasya asiddhau yathā caturvidhaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ pakṣa dharma prabhede nirdiṣṭaḥ sandehe yathā asarva jñaḥ kaścid vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ rāga ādimān vā vacana ādeḥ iti 
[II,107,i]	sandigdhaḥ atra vyatirekaḥ sarvajñaḥ vaktā na upalabdhaḥ iti evamprakārasya anupalambhasya adṛśya ātma viṣaya tvena sandeha hetu tvāt iti uktam kaḥ hi atra virodhaḥ yadi vaktā ca syāt sarva jñaḥ ca yadi atra bhavataḥ manda buddhi cakṣuṣaḥ anupalabdhiḥ artha anapākuryāt hanta hataḥ asi pitṛ vyapadeśa nibandhanasya api apāvṛtti prasaṅgāt vacana sarvajña tvayoḥ dvividhasya api virodhasya abhāvāt yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sa vaktā na bhavati iti vyatirekaḥ adarśane api na sidhyati sandehāt bādhaka bhāve hi aparābhāvaḥ niścīyate na ca aviruddha lakṣaṇam atīndriyam su jñāna bādhanam tat na vyāpti siddhiḥ sarvaḥ vaktā sarva jñaḥ iti 
[II,107,ii]	sarva vaktṛ dharma tā paricchedasya ca kartum aśakyatvāt saḥ eva hi evam sarvajñaḥ syāt iti apratiṣedhaḥ sva ātmani sva saṃviditena anena aparatra paricchedaḥ iti ced nanu evam ātmani dṛṣṭasya aparatra upanaye ati prasaṅgaḥ dṛṣṭa viruddhasya anupanayaḥ iti ced tulye nyāye kim na upanayaḥ na ca eṣa nyāyaḥ lakṣaṇa yukte virodha sambhavāt na darśana mātreṇa kim tarhi vyatirekāt api tad abhāvāt ananya upanayaḥ iti ced tulyā vṛtti tad sandehābhyām abhāva asiddhiḥ iti anupanayaḥ dṛśya tayā ca tayoḥ ātmanoḥ virodha upalabdhiḥ iti asādhya tvam adṛśya ātmanām tu sva pratiyogibhiḥ virodhaḥ api mā bhūt yena nirasta pratipakṣāḥ niyamena niścīyante tat ayam puruṣaḥ ātmānam āntaraiḥ kaiścid ananya vedyaiḥ dharmaiḥ yuktam pratisaṃvedayamānaḥ tad upasaṃhāreṇa sarvatra vyavaharan prakāmam āsādita vidyā śrama phalaḥ yaḥ strī śūdra sādhāraṇam api vivekam na avagāhate tasmāt ātmani darśana mātreṇa anupasaṃhāraḥ tāvatā vyāpti asiddheḥ atas sandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ 
[II,108,i_II,109,ii]	pūrva uktāt ca anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāt i īdṛśām prayogāṇām sandeha hetu tvam unneyam rāga ādīnām api artha antara tvāt agatiḥ vacanāt anumāna lakṣaṇāt abhyūhyā apratibandhāt asati rāge vacanam na asti iti aniścitaḥ vyatirekaḥ na hi rāga ādīnām eva kāryam spanda vacana ādayaḥ vaktu kāma tā sāmānya hetutvāt sā eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ nitya sukha ātma ātmīya darśana ākṣiptam sa āsrava dharma viṣayam abhūta guṇa abhinandanam rāgam āhuḥ tad ānanda viṣaya uparodhini tad kṛtaḥ cetasaḥ vyāroṣaḥ dveṣaḥ saḥ eva ubhaya āśrayaḥ pūrvakaḥ viparyāsaḥ mohaḥ na evam karuṇā ādayaḥ anyathā api bhāvāt iti vyākhyātam vārttike tatra yathā raktaḥ bravīti tathā viraktaḥ api iti vacana mātrāt apratītiḥ na api viśeṣāt abhiprāyasya durbodha tvāt vyavahāra saṅkareṇa sarveṣām vyabhicārāt 
[II,109,iii]	prayojana abhāvāt avyāhāraḥ iti ced na para artha tvāt na yuktaḥ vīta rāga tvāt iti ced na karuṇayā api vṛtteḥ sā eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭam na nāma nivāryate rūpam tu bhinnam aśubha abhinandinaḥ pratisandhi bandhāt atas eva aviparyāsa udbhavā sā na doṣaḥ asatya ātma grahe duḥkha viśeṣa darśana mātreṇa abhyāsa bala utpādinī bhavati eva karuṇā tathā hi dharma ālambana ādayaḥ maitrī ādayaḥ sūtre deśitāḥ etāḥ ca sajātīya abhyāsa vṛttayaḥ na evam rāga ādayaḥ viparyāsa abhāve abhāvāt kāruṇikasya api niṣphalaḥ ārambhaḥ viparyāsāt iti ced na para arthasya eva phala tvena iṣṭa tvāt tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca phalasya 
[II,110,i]	vaktari ātmani rāga ādi darśanena anyatra tad anumāne ati prasaṅgaḥ api uktaḥ vyabhicārāt ananya anumānaḥ iha avyabhicāraḥ iti kutas niścayaḥ adarśane api uktam dṛśya ātmanoḥ nāma ayam arvāk darśanaḥ sahabhāvam itaram vā paśyet viprakṛṣṭe punar arthe abhāva nirṇayaḥ anaikāntikaḥ tasmāt karaṇa guṇa vaktu kāmate vacanam anumāpayet nanu atra api eṣa tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ na ātmani darśanena anumānam iti na tayoḥ iha anvaya vyatirekābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddheḥ anyatra anumānāt na tu evam aśubha abhinandena viparyāsena ca vacanasya tad siddhiḥ ātmani eva anyathā darśanāt 
[II,111,i]	rāga utpatti yogya tā ra hite vacana adarśanāt tad anumāne vyatireka asiddheḥ na kārya kāraṇa tā siddhiḥ acetanā vyatireka viṣayaḥ iti ced na evaṃvidhāt vyatirekāt kāraṇa śakti siddhiḥ satsu hi samartheṣu tad anyeṣu kāraṇeṣu kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa antaram anumāpayati na ca evaṃvidhaḥ vyatirekaḥ acetaneṣu sambhavati caitanya karaṇa guṇa ādeḥ eva dṛṣṭa śakteḥ hetoḥ teṣu asambhavāt saṃśayaḥ rāgasya anupayoge katham tat śaktiḥ upayujyate svabhāva guṇasya śaktau upacārāt yatra saḥ asamarthaḥ na tatra śakteḥ sāmarthyam asti iti 
[II,111,ii_II,112,i]	tasmāt na āntarīyakam eva kāryam kāraṇam anumāpayati tad pratibandhāt na anyat vipakṣe adarśane api sarva darśinaḥ hi darśana vyāvṛttiḥ sarva abhāvam gamayet kvacid tathā adṛṣṭānām api deśa kāla bhedena anyathā darśanāt yathā āmalakyaḥ kṣīra avasekena madhura phalāḥ bhavanti na ca evam bahulam dṛśyante tena evam syāt yuktam vaktum mādṛśaḥ vaktā rāgī iti rāga utpatti pratyaya viśeṣeṇa ātma darśana ayoni śoma naskāreṇa yogāt tadā api apārthakaḥ vacana udāhāraḥ tasmāt na asya api vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa vyāvṛttiḥ asandigdhā tena ayam api ekasya rūpasya sandehāt anaikāntikaḥ dvayoḥ viruddhaḥ asiddhau ca yathā kṛtaka tva prayatna ānantarīyaka tve nitya tva sādhane tayoḥ sa pakṣe asattvam vipakṣe bhāvaḥ ca iti dvayaḥ rūpayoḥ asiddhiḥ viparyaya siddhiḥ iti yāvat tat etau dvau hetū viparyaya sādhanāt viruddhau 
[II,113,i]	nanu tṛtīyaḥ api iṣṭa vighāta kṛt viruddhaḥ asti yathā para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṅghāta tvāt śayana āsana ādi aṅga vat iti tad iṣṭa asaṃhata pārārthya viparyaya sādhanāt viruddhaḥ sa kasmāt na uktaḥ sādhya tā abhedāt na hi ayamābhyām sādhya viparyaya sādhana tvena bhidyate na hi iṣṭa uktayoḥ sādhya tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti uktam viśeṣe tu viruddha vat hetuḥ api pṛthak iṣṭa sādhanaḥ vācyaḥ syāt ekasya eva tu vacanena sādhya tā aviśeṣaḥ darśitaḥ tatas eva tad viparyaya sādhanaḥ viruddhaḥ api ekaḥ eva prayoga bhedāt tu tad bhedaḥ kvacid ukti sāmarthyābhyām kvacid vivakṣayā dharma dharmiṇoḥ viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt viruddha vat hetuḥ api evam kim na bhinnaḥ iti ced kaḥ pratiṣeddhāḥ vibhettuḥ anukta sāmarthya ākṣiptam iṣṭam paraḥ abhipraiti iti tad abhiprāya vaśa ādiṣṭa vighāta kṛt iti ucyate na punar lakṣaṇa bhedāt atas eva apṛthak nirdeśaḥ iti uktam 
[II,114,i]	nanu saṃhatānām asaṃhata para upakāra niyama abhāvāt anaikāntikaḥ eva iti aviruddhaḥ kaḥ hi eṣa niyamaḥ saṃhatāḥ para upakāriṇaḥ iti yadi api kvacid kārye avadhānavatām arthānām sāmagrī saṅghātaḥ tathā api na avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti pratibandha ādi sambhavāt iti vyabhicāraḥ eva apratibaddha upakārāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ para upakāriṇaḥ ced atra api saṃhata upakāriṇaḥ eva iti kaḥ pratibandha niyamaḥ 
[II,114,ii]	pratyupayogam tebhyaḥ upakāryasya svabhāva antara utpatteḥ tathā upayoginām nānā svabhāva upakāra sādhanam etat na eka kāla aneka upakāra sādhanam upakārasya artha antara tve atad upakāra ādayaḥ api uktāḥ anubhaya kāriṇāma anartha kyāt tāt arthya sādhanam vipratiṣiddham tasmāt upakurvāṇāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ ādheya atiśayam eva upakurvate sa tasmāt eka svabhāvaḥ na bhavati iti viruddhaḥ 
[II,115,i_II,115,ii]	caśabdaḥ dvayoḥ ekasya asiddhau aparasya ca sandehe vyabhicāra bhāj iti sūcanā arthaḥ yathā vīta rāgaḥ sarvajñaḥ vā vacanāt iti vyatirekaḥ atra asiddhaḥ sandigdhaḥ anvayaḥ sarvajña vīta rāgayoḥ viprakarṣāt vacana ādeḥ tatra sattvam asat tvam vā sandigdham sandehe vyabhicāra bhāj dvayoḥ iti vartate yatra anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ ca sandigdhaḥ yathā sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt iti 
[II,115,iii]	na hi sa ātmakān ātmakābhyām anyaḥ rāśiḥ asti yatra prāṇa ādiḥ varteta ātma vṛtti vyavacchedābhyām sarvasya saṅgrahāt na api anayoḥ ekatra vṛtti niścayaḥ tādātmyena prasiddhe asiddheḥ tasmāt jīvat śarīra sambandhī prāṇa ādiḥ anubhaya ātma tā bahis bhāvāt tābhyām na vyatiricyate na tatra anveti eka ātmani api asiddheḥ atas eva anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sandehāt anaikāntikaḥ sādhyetarayoḥ atas aniścayāt 
[II,116,i]	na api apratipattiḥ kenacid sambandhāt asambandhāt vimarśaḥ na jāyate yathā cākṣuṣa tvāt śabde sambandhāt kiṃsambaddhaḥ ayam iti katham na vimṛśet aparijñāta sambandhāt garbhāt puruṣa viśeṣa sambandhe asambandha ayogāt yathā saṃśete tathā iha api sarva anantarbhāva ayogāt saṃśayaḥ apratipattiḥ anubhaya pratipatti saṃśaya rūpā sa ubhaya bahis bhāve syāt antarbhāve katham apratipattiḥ evam tarhi cākṣuṣa tvāt api astu na asambandhāt iti uktam tasmāt saṃśaya hetu rasa ādhāraṇaḥ 
[II,116,ii_II,117,i]	viśeṣataḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ viprakarṣāt ātmanaḥ vṛtti vyatireka asiddheḥ tatra prāṇa ādīnām api artha antarāt akārya bhūtāt asiddheḥ ca na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prāṇa ādīnām ātmanaḥ ca sidhyati tasya upalambha anupalambha āśraya tvāt tena na apratibaddhasya bhāve bhāvaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ gamakāḥ eva ātmanaḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ tad vyatirekasya aikāntika tvāt iti a paraḥ vipakṣāt eva hi prāṇa ādayaḥ nivartante na sa pakṣāt asataḥ nivṛtti ayogāt tasmāt aikāntika anvayavat aikāntika vyatirekaḥ api gamakaḥ eva na ca evam śrāvaṇa tvam ubhayatas vyāvṛtteḥ iti 
[II,117,ii]	tena evamprakāram vyatirekam varṇayatā vinābhāvaḥ eva uktaḥ bhavati tathā hi ātmā abhāvaḥ eva na bhavati eva iti arthāt ananya saṃsargiṇī ātma vṛttiḥ sūcitā bhavati sā eva avinābhāvaḥ tatas eva anvaya siddhiḥ iti na vyatirekī pratibandhaḥ ca avinābhāvaḥ sa ca ātma pratibandhaḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām anyaḥ na asti iti uktam te ca darśanena vinā na sidhyataḥ tat na ātma avinā bhāvī prāṇa ādiḥ tatas eva na ātma nivṛttau asya nivṛttiḥ api yatas vyatirekī iti ucyate na hi apratibaddhaḥ kasyacid nivṛttau niyamena nivartate tasmāt viśeṣasya na vyatirekaḥ na anvayaḥ adarśana mātram āśritya ācāryeṇa śrāvaṇa tve vyatirekaḥ uktaḥ na tāvatā abhāva gatiḥ iti uktam anyathā saṃśaya hetuḥ eva na syāt na hi yaḥ yatra na sambhavati tad upalabdhyā tatra saṃśayaḥ yuktaḥ 
[II,118,i_II,118,ii]	prāṇa ādi abhāvena nairātmyasya vyāpteḥ ātma nivṛttau prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ iti ced na apratibaddha abhāvena anupayoginaḥ abhāvasya vyāpti asiddheḥ yadi prāṇa ādayaḥ tad ātma tayā tad utpattyā vā ātma pratibaddhāḥ syuḥ te tad nivṛttyā nivarteran tadā prāṇa ādi abhāvaḥ nairātmyam vyāpnuyāt tad abhāve abhāva siddhyā vyāptiḥ iti sā na sidhyati viparyaye pratibandha asiddheḥ upalambha anupalambhābhyām hi tayoḥ pratibandham jānīyāt tau ca atyanta parokṣasya na sidhyataḥ ke ca nirātmānaḥ prāṇa ādi abhāvena vyāptāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ ced anyatra adṛṣṭaḥ sa ghaṭa ādau na iti kutas tena ajñāta vyatirekasya vyāvṛtti vyāptiḥ asiddhā prāṇa ādayaḥ api hi kvacid darśanāt eva sat asantaḥ pratīyante na ca evam ātmā iti na tasya sat asattva pratītiḥ yat api āha yadi na sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādi viraha prasaṅgaḥ nairātmyāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti tat api akārya kāraṇa bhāve na sidhyati uktam hi prāk na anupalabdhau akārya kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ gamakaḥ iti sa ca kāraṇa bhāvaḥ adarśanāt ātmanaḥ na sidhyati iti uktam 
[II,119,i]	darśane api vyatireka asiddheḥ na sidhyati ghaṭa ādayaḥ vyatireka viṣayāḥ iti ced na evaṃvidhāt vyatirekāt kāraṇa sāmarthya siddhiḥ satsu samartheṣu anyeṣu hetuṣu kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa antara bhāvam gamayati iti uktam buddhi ādayaḥ api hi prāṇa ādeḥ hetavaḥ ghaṭa ādau na santi tasmāt sandigdha sāmarthya ātmanaḥ vyatirekaḥ te api buddhi ādayaḥ nairātmye na syuḥ iti ced na tatra anyeṣām eva sāmarthya darśanāt cakṣuḥ ādi buddhīnām tāvat yathāsvam indriya viṣayau hetū pūrvakam ca aviguṇam vijñānam tasya viṣaya antara vikṣepa pratighāta ādau uttara vijñāna anutpatti vyākulatā ādi darśanāt manaḥ vijñānasya pūrvakam aviguṇam vijñānam indriya ādīnām api pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ sabhāga avasthā bhedaḥ upādāna hetuḥ buddhiḥ ca pratyayaḥ iti etāvataḥ ayam ātma bhāvaḥ anvaya vyatireka bhāj iti ayam eva hetuḥ anavasthānya kalpane syāt 
[II,120,i_II,120,ii]	yasmin sati bhavati eva yat tatas anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetūnām anavasthitiḥ iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ tulyaḥ ca śrāvaṇa tvena prāṇa ādiḥ vyabhicāreṇa na tad vyatirekasya vyabhicārāt katham vyabhicāraḥ na hi tasya āsapakṣāt eva vyatirekaḥ iti nanu evam asya sa pakṣe anuvṛtti abhāvaḥ kathyate saḥ aparasya api tulyaḥ iti katham asamaḥ prāṇa ādiḥ 
[II,120,iii]	asapakṣaḥ eva na asti iti ca asya sa pakṣe astitā ucyate pratiṣedha dvayena prakṛta gamanāt anyathā vyavacchedya abhāvāt avadhāraṇasya kim phalam syāt anavadhāraṇe ca vākyasya vyatirekasya avyabhicāra asiddheḥ tatas eva sa pakṣaḥ eva asti asapakṣaḥ eva na asti iti dṛṣṭāntayoḥ anyatareṇa artha apattyā ubhaya pradarśanam āha tasmāt īdṛśaḥ vyatireka avyabhicāraḥ ananvayeṣu na sidhyati sidhyan ca balāt anvayam āpādayati pratiṣedha niṣedhasya vidhāna rūpa tvāt 
[II,121,i_II,121,ii]	asataḥ sa pakṣāt na nivṛttiḥ iti asa pakṣaḥ eva na asti iti ced na iti sā eva nivṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ asataḥ katham iṣṭā abhāva pratiṣedhaḥ hi bhāvaḥ asati api asti bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ tu na sambhavati iti askhalita prajñaḥ devānām priyaḥ yaḥ tad viṣayam pratiṣedham na icchati asat abhāvaḥ iti evamādi ca vyavaharati nirloṭhitaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ asati na astitā iti atra antare tena na iha pratanyate na ca āsannātmā sattā sādhana vṛtteḥ sandigdhaḥ syāt na ca pareṇa tathā upagataḥ iti apramāṇāt abhyupagamāt tathā eva bhavati atiprasaṅgāt na ca upagama balena sa pakṣāsa pakṣau vyavasthāpya pramāṇa pravartanam yuktam evam hi āgama siddhaḥ ātmā syāt na anumāna siddhaḥ 
[II,122,i]	tasmāt avyatireke api asataḥ sa pakṣāt vyatirekaḥ sandigdhaḥ syāt prāṇa ādīnām ātmanaḥ sandehāt atas eva vipakṣāt api ekatra hi niyame siddhe anya nivartanam sidhyet anyathā hi kvacid dṛṣṭe abhāva siddhau api syāt eva adṛṣṭeṣu saṃśayaḥ tathā hi asakala vyakti bheda vyāpinaḥ api arthāḥ kecid tad jāti sambhavinaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ pārthiva āloha lekhya vat virodhasya ca adṛṣṭeḥ sandehaḥ eva nairātmyena prāṇa ādīnām ukta lakṣaṇasya virodhasya asiddheḥ sandigdhaḥ nairātmyāt vyatirekaḥ ātma pratiniyame hi tad kārya ātma tayā prāṇa ādīnām nairātmyena saha virodhaḥ syāt sa ca na sidhyati iti uktam 
[II,123,i_II,123,ii]	astu nāma nirātmakebhyaḥ vyatirekaḥ prāṇa ādīnām tad bhāve ca nairātmya vyāvṛttiḥ tathā api na anairātmyāt ātmā jīvat śarīre sidhyati yena ayam na vyatirekasya abhāvam bhāvam icchati yathā vyatireka abhāve api sa pakṣe prāṇa ādiḥ neṣṭaḥ sa pakṣāvyatirekī ced hetuḥ hetuḥ atas anvayī na anvayya vyatirekī ced anairātmyam na sa ātmakam iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ 
[II,123,iii_II,124,ii]	na prāṇa ādi sambhavena nairātmya vyāvartanāt ātma gatiḥ kim tarhi vidhi mukhena eva prāṇa ādayaḥ ātmānam gamayanti iti ced kim idānīm nairātmyāt vyatirekasya phalam sa hi tatra asambhavan sva sambhavena tat asambhavam sādhayati iti tatas vyatirekī varṇyeta anyathā ātma sannidhāyane kaḥ nairātmyāt vyatirekasya upayogaḥ katham vā aprasiddha ātma niyamāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ ātmānam vidadhati iti vaktavyam atiprasaṅgaḥ hi evam syāt iti asādhāraṇa anaikāntikaḥ eva prāṇa ādiḥ sādhāraṇam api khalu prameya tvam asaṃskṛta apavādinaḥ asati anvayā yogāt avyabhicarita anvayam sa pakṣaḥ eva asti iti anvayinam eva hetum āha 
[II,124,iii]	atra api katham avyatirekaḥ vipakṣāt katham vā sa pakṣaḥ eva asti iti kim hi asya avadhāraṇasya phalam yadi na vipakṣe astitvam vyavacchidyeta vyavacchede vā katham avyatirekaḥ na hi sattā pratiṣedhāt anyaḥ vyatirekaḥ vipratiṣiddham ca etat na anvayaḥ na vyatirekaḥ iti yaḥ eva khalu na iti anvaya pratiṣedhaḥ saḥ eva vyatirekaḥ iti 
[II,125,i]	tat punar idam āyātam asataḥ vyatireka ayogāt iti atra idam eva punar vācyam katham asataḥ anvaya pratiṣedhaḥ iti vastu rūpa anukarṣī khalu asati pratiṣedhaḥ na sambhavet na hi paryudāsaḥ eva ekaḥ nañaḥ viṣayaḥ kim tarhi prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ api na hi tasya asati virodhaḥ saḥ api na sambhavati adhikaraṇa ādi arthānām pratiṣedha viṣaya upadarśanīnām vibhaktīnām ayogāt iti ced ukta uttaram etat tasmāt na hetuḥ kaścid anvayī nāma 
[II,125,ii]	na ca prameya tvasya vipakṣe anvayā yogaḥ trividhaḥ hi dharmaḥ bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayaḥ iti uktam na abhāvasya kaścid dharmaḥ iti ced nanu ayam eva asya dharma virahaḥ dharmaḥ na hi vastu rūpam eva dharmaḥ asantaḥ api kenacid prakaraṇena imam vyavahāra patham upanīyante anyathā hi tatra avyavahāraḥ eva syāt na ca satām api paramārthataḥ kaścid dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ kevalam buddhiḥ evaṃsambandham uparacayati iti uktam vārttike buddhi kṛtā ca ghaṭanāsatsu kena nivāryate 
[II,126,i]	sat asat ubhaya anubhaya vyavasthāḥ ca tat atad samayavatām aniścita sādhanāḥ na ekānta grāhiṇyaḥ syuḥ tasmāt yathā kathañcid api anena asataḥ niścinvatā prameyāḥ vaktavyāḥ na hi bhāva viṣayam eva pramāṇam avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇa tvāt pramāṇasya tad sadasatī tad bhāvena vyavasthāpayan na ced sva viṣaye pareṇa bādhyate tat asya pramāṇa lakṣaṇam asti iti prameyaḥ abhāvaḥ 
[II,126,ii]	na eva abhāvaḥ kaścid sarveṣām kathañcid bhāvāt iti ced yathā te na santi sa prakāraḥ abhāvaḥ śaśa viṣāṇayoḥ ca ayam bhāvāt śaśa viṣāṇa abhāva vādinam upahasan ātmānam eva upahasati śaśa avayava bhūtam viṣāṇam na asti iti abhidhātari kaḥ prastāvaḥ śaśaḥ api asti viṣāṇam ca iti uttarasya na hi ayam viṣāṇa mātram apahnute yatas tena pratirudhyeta kim tarhi śaśa sambandhi yadi evam sambandhaḥ na asti iti vaktavyam na viṣāṇam kim vai sambandha mātram viśiṣyate viṣāṇinām api viṣāṇeṣu na dravya svabhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ api pratikāryam kāraṇa svabhāva bhedāt tat kaḥ ayam sambandha abhāvaḥ vācyaḥ iti upālambhaḥ asti viṣāṇinām viṣāṇa svabhāva bhedaḥ na tadvat kiñcit śaśasya bhinna svabhāvam viṣāṇam iti ced vayam api etat eva brūmaḥ yaḥ vā sambandhaḥ na asti iti ucyate saḥ eva abhāvaḥ sambandhī vidyate na sambandhaḥ iti ca nipuṇā vācaḥ yuktiḥ aṅgīkṛta sambandham dravyam api na iti ced priyam anuṣṭhitam yadi idam eva prathamamucyeta na parikleśitaḥ devānām priyaḥ syāt iti 
[II,128,i_II,128,ii]	viruddha avyabhicārī api saṃśaya hetuḥ uktaḥ saḥ iha na uktaḥ anumāna viṣaye asambhavāt na hi sambhavaḥ asti kārya svabhāvayoḥ ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ anupalambhasya vā viruddha avyabhicāritāyām na ca anyaḥ avyabhicārī tasmāt avastu darśana bala pravṛttam āgama āśrayam anumānam āśritya tad artha vicāreṣu viruddha avyabhicārī sādhana doṣaḥ uktaḥ śāstra kārāṇām artheṣu bhrāntyā viparīta svabhāva upasaṃhāra sambhavāt na hi asti sambhavaḥ yathā avasthita vastu sthitiṣu ātma kārya anupalambheṣu tatra udāharaṇam sarva gatam sāmānyam sarva deśa avasthitaiḥ sva sambandhibhiḥ yugapad sambandhāt ākāśa vat iti 
[II,128,iii]	tad sambandhi svabhāva mātra anubandhinī tad deśa sannihita svabhāva tā na hi yaḥ yatra na asti sa tad deśam ātmanā vyāpnoti nanu na ākāśa deśe rūpa ādayaḥ tad deśān ca ghaṭa ādīn vyāpnuvanti āstām tāvat ayam pradeśa pradeśi bhāvaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga samavāyābhyām laukikam tu pradeśam āśritya brūmaḥ vicchinnā vicchinna avabhāsi vijñāna utpādana yogya tā lakṣaṇam yuta ayuta siddhayoḥ sambandhau saṃyoga samavāyau iti śāstre api vyavasthā tat iyam sva sattā mātra anubandhini tad deśa sannidhau sādhye tad sambandhitāḥ hetuḥ 
[II,129,i]	nanu sva āśraya vyāpti vādinā api tad deśa sannidhiḥ iṣyate eva iti kim aniṣṭam akriyasya eka vyakti sambandhinaḥ deśa antare apūrva vyakti prādurbhāve prākta tra asataḥ tad sambandha ayogaḥ tasmāt bhinna deśaiḥ yugapad sambandhaḥ sarva vyāpini sidhyati tad eka sambandhinaḥ deśa antare agatvā tat deśaiḥ apūrvaiḥ abhisambandhaḥ ekasya tad antar āla vyāptinā antarīyakaḥ ātapa ādeḥ iva ghaṭa ādibhiḥ iti 
[II,129,ii_II,130,i]	dvitīyaḥ api prayogaḥ na sarva gatam sāmānyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya tad antarāleṣu anupalambhāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ abhivyaktiḥ abhedāt eka vyaktyā sarva vyakteḥ avyakta rūpa virahaḥ avyavadhāna m adūra sthānam dṛśya ātmatā indriyasya sva āśrayeṇa sambandhaḥ abhedāt eva āśraya asamaveta rūpa virahaḥ ca samāna deśa āśraya indriya yoga apekṣāyām āśraya samāna asamāna deśa rūpasya abheda virodhaḥ dṛśya adṛśya ātmata ādi virodhāḥ api vācyāḥ 
[II,130,ii_II,130,iii]	tat ayam anupalambhaḥ svabhāvaḥ ca paraspara viruddha artha sādhanau ekatra saṃśayam janayataḥ śāstra kāraḥ viruddha dharmanā antarīyaka tām dvayoḥ apaśyan tayoḥ avirodha darśi tayā prāha iti sambhavaḥ viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ vastu anurodhini punar anumāne yathā virodhinoḥ ekatrāsambhavaḥ tathā tad abhivyāptayoḥ api iti na tau ekatra staḥ tat na atra viruddha avyabhicārī tat ayam abhyupagama bala pravṛttaḥ 
[II,130,iv]	ācāryeṇa punar diś mātra darśanāya idam udāharaṇam uktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt nityaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt iti atra hi trayam apramāṇakam abhyupeyam vyatireki śabda tva sāmānyam indriya gamyam nityam ca atas asya pramāṇasya vṛttiḥ tat na etat vastu bala āyātam kṛtaka tvam pratibadhnāti kṛtaka tva prastāve ca anāgama āśrayāt na āgama upanyāsaḥ sādhyaḥ ca pratibandhaḥ yat śrāvaṇam tat nityam iti avyabhicāraḥ api na sidhyati iti 
[II,132,i_II,132,ii]	hetoḥ tri lakṣaṇa tvāt na dṛṣṭāntaḥ pṛthak ucyate tri lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ tāvatā ca artha pratītiḥ iti na pṛthak dṛṣṭāntaḥ nāma kaścid sādhana avayavaḥ tena na asya lakṣaṇam pṛthak ucyate gata artha tvāt hetoḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva sattvam vipakṣāt ca sarvatas vyāvṛttiḥ rūpam uktam abhedena punar viśeṣeṇa kārya svabhāvayoḥ janma tanmātra anubandhau darśanīyau uktau tat ca darśayatā yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ asati agnau na kvacid dhūmaḥ yathā mahānasa itarayoḥ yatra kṛtaka tvam tatra anitya tvam anitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tvasya asambhavaḥ yathā ghaṭa ākāśayoḥ iti darśanīyam na hi anyathā sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sat asat tve yathā ukta prakāre śakye darśayitum tad kāryatā pratiniyamaḥ svabhāva vyāptiḥ vā asmin ca arthe darśite darśitaḥ eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati etāvat mātra rūpa tvāt tasya 
[II,132,iii]	etena eva dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ api nirastāḥ bhavanti yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrta tvāt karma vat paramāṇu vat ghaṭa vat iti sādhya ādi vikalāḥ sandigdhāḥ ca rāga ādimān vacanāt rathyā puruṣa vat iti ādayaḥ ananvayaḥ apradarśita anvayaḥ ca yathā yaḥ vaktā sa rāga ādima aniṣṭa puruṣa vat anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti tathā viparīta anvayaḥ yat anityam tat kṛtakam iti sādharmyeṇa 
[II,133,i_II,133,iii]	vaidharmyeṇa api paramāṇu vat karma vat ākāśa vat iti sādhyādi a vyatirekiṇaḥ tathā sandigdha vyatireka ādayaḥ vācyāḥ na hi ebhiḥ hetoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇam viśeṣa lakṣaṇam vā śakyam darśayitum tad arthāpattyā eṣām nirāsaḥ veditavyaḥ yadi punar heturūpā saṃsparśī svatantraḥ eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhana avayavaḥ syāt tadā tad rūpā sparśane ca syāt asambandhāt apārthakaḥ 
[II,134,i]	yadi na hetoḥ avyabhicāra dharma tā dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyeta kaḥ sādhya sādhane tasya upayogaḥ asambandhāt na hi kathañcid sādṛśya mātreṇa arthānām kenacid ātma antara pratiniyamaḥ yena upamānāt sādhanam syāt na hi arthasya kenacid kathañcin na sāmyam tatas tad ātma tāyām sarvam sarva ātmakam syāt na ca etat yuktam tasmāt tad abhivyāpta dharma yogāt eva bhāvāḥ tadvantaḥ syuḥ iti abhivyāptiḥ asya dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate tat ayam na svatantraḥ tad asambandhī cāpa arthakaḥ tena eva artha parisamāpteḥ iti 
[II,135,i_II,136,ii]	dūṣaṇā nyūna tādi uktiḥ ye pūrvam nyūna tā ādayaḥ sādhana doṣāḥ uktāḥ teṣām udbhāvanam dūṣaṇam tena para iṣṭa artha siddhi pratibandhāt nanu anudbhāvite api doṣe arthasya eva asāmarthyāt na bhavati prasiddhiḥ evam etat kim tu na arthānām niṣpatti aniṣpattī sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām kriyete teṣām sarvadā tādavasthyāt kim tarhi puruṣa sāmarthya siddhiḥ sā vacanam antareṇa na sidhyati iti sa tathābhūtam eva khyāpayan tasya kartā iti ucyate yadi punar udbhāvite api doṣe sampūrṇa vacana ādinā pratisamādadhīta na tad iṣṭa pratibandhaḥ iti na dūṣaṇam syāt na tasya sādhana antara tvāt yadi pūrva pakṣa vādī sa ākāṅkṣaḥ syāt asamāpta vākyaḥ eva iti na dūṣaṇa avasaraḥ sthita vacane tu tasmin doṣam udbhāvayan dūṣakaḥ eva tasya sādhanasya tad ābhāsāḥ tu jātayaḥ mithyā uttarāṇām ānantyāt pratanyante na tāḥ iha 
[II,136,iii_II,137,i]	mithyā uttarāṇi jātayaḥ teṣām ca na antaḥ ayoniśaḥ vikalpānām apratiṣṭhānāt yathā āha paraḥ na asti ātmā iti pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma pratijñā doṣaḥ artha apahnave śabda prayoga asambhavāt prayuñjānaḥ artham upasthāpayati apahnute ca iti pratijñā padayoḥ virodhāt pratijñā doṣaḥ iti yathā ca āha dharmi viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt anityaḥ prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ iti na hi evamādīni yathā ukta lakṣaṇāsu jātiṣu antar bhavanti na ca dūṣaṇāni śabda arthān apahnavena sva lakṣaṇa pratiṣedhāt sādhya dharmi bahirbhāvāt ca iti uktam tāni api kenacid leśena asu eva antarbhavanti iti ced āsām api parasparam eṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti ekam eva kiñcid sāmānya lakṣaṇam vācyam syāt viśeṣe anantarbhāvāt tat ca sāmānya lakṣaṇam uktam eva dūṣaṇa ābhāsāḥ tu jātayaḥ iti tāḥ sādhana dūṣaṇa lakṣaṇa jñānāt eva aviṣaye apravṛtteḥ pratipatteḥ apratibandhāt pratibandha lakṣaṇa virahāt ca uttara ābhāsa tvena su jñānāḥ prabhedaḥ punar āsām ānantyāt aśakyanirdeśaḥ iti na nirdiśyate yuktaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti sūtram amoghanīteḥ draṣṭuḥ mayā āgamitam āgamam adhyupekṣya tasya api avaśyam avadāta dhiyaḥ ayam eva bhāvaḥ avibhāvita dhiyā viditaḥ janena
